### [1] [LLM-Driven CI-CD Workflow Intelligence for Cyber Systems Engineering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04579v1)
*Bonan Shen,Jiazhou Gao,Tao Ning,Wei-Jung Huang,Xin Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出基于LLM的CI/CD分析管道，在大型GitHub语料库中进行反模式检测、阶段挖掘和推荐生成，发现工作流存在大量可靠性和可维护性问题，并主张结合诊断、上下文和人工审查的CI/CD可观察性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CI/CD工作流已成为可执行操作策略，但仅识别阶段不足以判断工作流是否脆弱或异常，需要更全面的分析。

Method: 提出基于LLM的CI/CD分析管道，包括仓库丰富化、反模式检测、阶段挖掘和推荐生成，使用少样本提示生成仓库级推荐。

Result: 从59,550个仓库中识别34,225个有CI/CD的项目，分析75,201个工作流，检测到434,769个反模式，阶段使用率因语言而异，移动项目有更高的发布和缓存使用率；少样本提示平均每个仓库生成8.25条推荐，96.1%YAML有效。

Conclusion: 主张结合诊断、上下文和人工审查的CI/CD可观察性，而非仅将工作流挖掘视为阶段分类问题。

中文摘要：CI/CD工作流已成为可执行的操作策略：它们决定构建、测试、发布和部署什么，并调节维护者与交付基础设施的交互方式。这使得它们成为网络系统工程的一个重要测量点。最近的大语言模型（LLM）研究表明，工作流阶段可以直接从配置文件中识别，但仅凭阶段标签并不能告诉我们工作流是否脆弱、对其生态系统是否异常，或者是否值得优先修订。我们提出了一种基于LLM的CI/CD分析管道，它结合了仓库丰富化、反模式检测、阶段挖掘和推荐生成，应用于大型GitHub语料库。从59,550个至少拥有1000颗星的仓库开始，我们识别出34,225个具有CI/CD的项目，并收集了127,559个配置文件。在75,201个分析的工作流中，反模式检测器报告了434,769个发现，主要集中在可靠性和可维护性问题。在59,906个配置中，阶段使用率因语言而异（χ²=4168.88，p<0.001，Cramer's V=0.063），领域分析显示出不同的操作模式，包括移动项目中更高的发布和缓存使用率。对于仓库级推荐生成，少样本提示整体表现最好，平均每个仓库生成8.25条推荐，其中96.1%的YAML有效片段。综合来看，研究结果主张将诊断、上下文和人工审查相结合的CI/CD可观察性，而不是将工作流挖掘仅视为阶段分类问题。

Original abstract: CI/CD workflows have become executable operational policy: they decide what gets built, tested, released, and deployed, and they mediate how maintainers interact with delivery infrastructure. That makes them an important measurement point for cyber-systems engineering. Recent large language model (LLM) work shows that workflow stages can be recognized directly from configuration files, but stage labels alone do not tell us whether a workflow is brittle, unusual for its ecosystem, or worth revising first. We present an LLM-based CI/CD analysis pipeline that combines repository enrichment, anti-pattern detection, stage mining, and recommendation generation over a large GitHub corpus. Starting from 59,550 repositories with at least 1,000 stars, we identify 34,225 projects with CI/CD and collect 127,559 configuration files. Across 75,201 analyzed workflows, the anti-pattern detector reports 434,769 findings, dominated by reliability and maintainability issues. Across 59,906 configurations, stage usage differs significantly by language ($χ^2 = 4168.88$, $p < 0.001$, Cramer's $V = 0.063$), and domain analysis shows distinct operational profiles, including higher release and cache usage in mobile projects. For repository-level recommendation generation, few-shot prompting performs best overall, averaging 8.25 recommendations per repository with 96.1% YAML-valid snippets. Taken together, the results argue for CI/CD observability that combines diagnosis, context, and human review rather than treating workflow mining as a stage-classification problem alone.

</details>


### [2] [Finetuning Lightweight LLMs for Control Flow Graph Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04582v1)
*Hanyu Zhang,Tomoji Kishi*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过微调轻量级大型语言模型，实现了对不完整或错误代码的统一控制流图生成，并展示了跨语言泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统CFG生成方法依赖完整代码和特定语言工具，难以处理不完整或错误代码，且缺乏多语言统一支持。

Method: 设计统一的CFG输出格式和任务特定微调提示，基于LeetCode数据集构建含错误增强的训练数据，微调多个轻量级LLM（包括CodeLlama、QwenCoder、DeepSeekCoder等）。

Result: 微调后的轻量级LLM在CFG生成上表现良好，尤其对不完整或错误代码效果显著，且能泛化到未见过的编程语言。

Conclusion: 轻量级LLM通过微调可有效生成CFG，克服传统方法的局限性，支持多语言和不完整代码场景。

中文摘要：控制流图（CFG）是软件分析、代码理解和软件维护中重要的程序表示形式。传统的CFG生成技术主要依赖于字节码或抽象语法树。然而，这些方法通常需要完整、可编译且无语法错误的代码，这限制了它们对不完整或错误代码的适用性。此外，它们通常依赖于特定语言的工具，难以统一支持多种编程语言。为了解决这些限制，本文研究了使用微调的轻量级大型语言模型（LLM）进行CFG生成。我们首先设计了一个统一的CFG输出格式和一个针对CFG生成的任务特定微调提示。然后，我们基于现有的LeetCode数据集，通过自动CFG生成和错误增强构建了一个数据集。我们在六个轻量级LLM模型上评估了所提出的方法，包括三个代码特定的LLM：CodeLlama、QwenCoder和DeepSeekCoder；以及三个通用LLM：Llama3.2-3B、Qwen-4B和Phi-4B。实验结果表明，通过微调，轻量级LLM在CFG生成上取得了有前景的结果，特别是当输入代码不完整或有错误时。该方法还在未包含在微调数据中的编程语言上展示了跨语言泛化能力。

Original abstract: Control Flow Graph (CFG) is an important program representations for software analysis, code understanding, and software maintenance. Traditional CFG generation techniques mainly rely on bytecode or abstract syntax trees. However, these approaches usually require complete, compilable, and syntax error-free code, which limits their applicability to incomplete or erroneous code. Furthermore, they often depend on language specific tools, making it difficult to support multiple programming languages in a unified manner. To address these limitations, this paper investigates the use of fine-tuned lightweight large language models (LLMs) for CFG generation. We first design a unified CFG output format and a task-specific fine-tuning prompt for CFG generation. Then, we construct a dataset based on an existing LeetCode dataset through automatic CFG generation and error augmentation. We evaluate the proposed approach on six lightweight LLM models, including three code-specific LLMs: CodeLlama, QwenCoder, and DeepSeekCoder; and three general purpose LLMs: Llama3.2-3B, Qwen-4B, and Phi-4B. The experimental results show that, through fine-tuning, lightweight LLMs achieve promising results for CFG generation, particularly when the input code is incomplete or erroneous. It also demonstrates cross-language generalization capability on programming language not included in the fine-tuning data.

</details>


### [3] [Beyond Compliance: A Large Scale Study on the Completeness and Consistency of the GitHub SBOMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04614v1)
*Kawsar Ahmed Bhuiyan,Mohamed Bilel Besbes,Rachna Raj,Adam Al Assil,Diego Elias Costa*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过分析10,000个GitHub仓库，发现GitHub SBOM在核心元数据上可靠，但缺乏NTIA合规性，版本和许可证信息因生态系统而异，整体性能与Microsoft SBOM Tool相当，优于Syft和Trivy。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估GitHub SBOM作为漏洞和许可证分析数据源的可靠性，并探究不完整元数据对不同编程生态系统的影响。

Method: 对跨十个编程语言生态系统的10,000个GitHub仓库进行大规模分析，将GitHub SBOM与Syft、Trivy和Microsoft SBOM Tool三种生成器进行对比。

Result: GitHub SBOM缺乏NTIA合规性但核心元数据一致；版本和许可证信息可用性高度依赖生态系统；GitHub SBOM性能与Microsoft SBOM Tool相似，优于Syft和Trivy。

Conclusion: GitHub SBOM工具存在与生态系统依赖管理相关的潜在缺点，但总体上可作为可靠的SBOM来源。

中文摘要：现代软件开发在很大程度上依赖于开源组件。重用组件加速了创新，但增加了利用已知漏洞的供应链攻击的风险。软件物料清单（SBOM）通过列举组件、其版本及其来源来提高软件供应链的透明度。GitHub作为最大的开源软件开发托管平台，现在会自动为仓库生成SBOM，为风险评估提供有价值的元数据。然而，尚不清楚GitHub SBOM是否可以作为漏洞和许可证分析的可靠来源，以及不完整或不一致的元数据如何影响不同的编程生态系统。为解决这一问题，我们对跨十个编程语言生态系统的10,000个GitHub仓库进行了大规模分析，将GitHub SBOM与其他三种流行的SBOM生成器（Syft、Trivy和Microsoft SBOM Tool）进行了评估。我们的研究发现GitHub SBOM缺乏NTIA合规性，尽管核心元数据始终存在。我们还发现组件版本和许可证信息的可用性高度依赖于编程生态系统。与其他三种工具相比，GitHub生成的结果与Microsoft SBOM Tool相似，并且在提供版本和许可证信息方面通常优于Syft和Trivy。最后，我们讨论了GitHub SBOM工具的潜在缺点，这些缺点直接与每个生态系统管理其依赖关系的方式相关。

Original abstract: Modern software development relies heavily on open-source components. Reusing components accelerates innovation but increases exposure to supply-chain attacks exploiting known vulnerabilities. Software Bills of Materials (SBOMs) improve software supply chain transparency by enumerating components, their versions, and their provenance. GitHub, the largest open-source development hosting platform, now automatically generates SBOMs for repositories, providing valuable metadata for risk assessment. Yet, it is unclear whether GitHub SBOMs can serve as a reliable source for vulnerability and license analysis, and how incomplete or inconsistent metadata may affect different programming ecosystems. To address this, we conduct a large-scale analysis of 10,000 GitHub repositories across ten programming language ecosystems, evaluating GitHub SBOMs against three other popular SBOM generators: Syft, Trivy, and the Microsoft SBOM Tool. Our study finds a lack of NTIA compliance in GitHub SBOMs, though core metadata is consistently present. We also find that component version and license information availability is highly dependent on the programming ecosystem. Compared with the other three tools, GitHub yields results similar to the Microsoft SBOM Tool and often outperforms Syft and Trivy in providing version and license information. Finally, we discuss potential shortcomings of the GitHub SBOM Tool, directly related to how each ecosystem manages its dependencies.

</details>


### [4] [Can LLMs Really Recover Microservice Failures? A Recovery-Aware Evaluation of Diagnosis-to-Action Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04623v1)
*Jiaxing Qi,Zhongzhi Luan,Hongyu Zhang,Shaohan Huang,Carol Fung,Yongxin Tong,Hailong Yang,Depei Qian*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出R2Act框架评估LLM在云原生系统中的恢复行动能力，发现即使诊断准确，恢复有效性仍低，主要困难在于将诊断转化为有效动作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RCA和日志分析评估只关注诊断，不评估诊断后的恢复行动决策，而恢复行动对于事件响应至关重要。

Method: 提出R2Act框架，包含事件模式、质量门、动作空间表示、恢复有效性指标、离线评估器和实时重放协议，并实例化为302个Kubernetes事件的数据集，用于评估多种方法。

Result: 最强RAG-LLM在根本原因服务准确率高达91.4%–99.7%，但恢复有效性仅36.8%–60.3%；即使诊断正确，仍有39.5%–62.0%的案例选择无效动作。

Conclusion: 恢复失败主要源于将诊断证据转化为有效恢复动作的困难，而非诊断知识不足；本工作提供了可重复的评估起点。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地被用于解释操作证据并协助云原生微服务系统中的事件响应。然而，面向恢复的用例需要的不仅仅是确定根本原因。在观察到症状并诊断出故障后，操作员或代理必须将诊断转化为具体的恢复行动，将其应用于可接受的目标，并验证服务健康是否已恢复。现有的RCA和日志分析评估非常适合诊断，但它们没有描述后续的行动决策。本文提出了R2Act，一个用于诊断后事件响应的恢复行动评估框架。R2Act定义了一个事件模式、质量门、动作空间表示、恢复有效性指标、离线评估器和实时重放协议。我们将该框架实例化为一个基准数据集，包含来自\system的302个经过质量审计的Kubernetes事件。每个事件提供同步的多模态观测、根本原因标签、事件特定的动作空间以及注释的有效和无效恢复计划。我们评估了启发式、监督、RCA导向、深度日志和基于LLM的方法。最强的基于RAG的LLM达到了91.4%–99.7%的根本原因服务准确率，但其恢复有效性仅为36.8%–60.3%。即使根本原因服务和故障类型都正确，面向恢复的方法在39.5%–62.0%的正确诊断事件中仍然选择了无效动作。总体而言，这项工作揭示了许多恢复失败并非源于诊断知识的缺失，而是源于将诊断证据转化为有效恢复动作和可接受目标的困难。这项工作为研究和评估提供了一个可重复、简化的起点。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to interpret operational evidence and assist incident response in cloud-native microservice systems. However, recovery-oriented use cases require more than identifying a root cause. After observing symptoms and diagnosing a fault, an operator or agent must translate the diagnosis into a concrete recovery action, apply it to an admissible target, and verify that service health has been restored. Existing RCA and log-analysis evaluations are well-suited to diagnosis, but they do not characterize this subsequent action decision. This paper presents R2Act, a recovery-action evaluation framework for post-diagnosis incident response. R2Act defines an incident schema, quality gate, action-space representation, recovery-validity metrics, offline evaluator, and live-replay protocol. We instantiate the framework as a benchmark dataset of 302 quality-audited Kubernetes incidents from \system. Each incident provides synchronized multi-modal observations, root-cause labels, an incident-specific action space, and annotated valid and invalid recovery plans. We evaluate heuristic, supervised, RCA-oriented, deep log, and LLM-based methods. The strongest RAG-based LLMs reach 91.4\%--99.7\% root-cause service accuracy, yet their recovery validity remains only 36.8\%--60.3\%. Even when both the root-cause service and fault type are correct, recovery-oriented methods still choose invalid actions for 39.5\%--62.0\% of correctly diagnosed incidents. Overall, this work reveals that many recovery failures arise not from missing diagnostic knowledge, but from the difficulty of translating diagnostic evidence into valid recovery actions and admissible targets. This work provides a reproducible, simplified starting point for research and evaluation.

</details>


### [5] [Correctness, confidence, and context: Framing software assurance in the AI age](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04667v2)
*Mary Shaw*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文批判了软件工程对形式化正确性的追求，指出生成式AI带来的概率性保障要求我们重新思考保障技术，特别是隐性知识的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软件工程长期陷入形式化正确性思维，而生成式AI的统计本质迫使我们需要系统性地理解各种保障方法的优劣，尤其是处理隐性知识和AI挑战。

Method: 通过挑战现有思维模式，提出系统思考保障技术，特别是关注隐藏上下文和AI的独特问题，并呼吁做出工程化的成本效益决策。

Result: 指出传统保障方法忽视隐性知识和系统目的，生成式AI的近似正确性限制了形式保证，且我们对各种方法缺乏系统性比较。

Conclusion: 我们需要像工程师一样行事，系统性地选择和组合保障方法，以建立对系统的信心，而非执着于形式化正确性。

中文摘要：软件工程与“正确性”有着复杂的关系。我们认识到完全形式化严谨性的挑战，以及除功能正确性之外的许多所需属性。尽管在实践中我们采取满意原则，但我们仍然固守着一种思维模式，即只要拥有足够的信息，我们就能够推理出正确性。不幸的是，对于我们对形式化严谨性的期望，我们的期望是由个人、主观、定性和基本上不可用的隐性知识所塑造的。生成式AI为保障引入了一个新的维度：其基础是统计性的而非形式化的。传统软件工程通过严格的推理、领域知识和专家判断来建立信心。相比之下，生成式AI的结果是复杂的预测，“可能近似正确”。这从根本上将关于结果的保证限制在概率性断言上。此外，指导人类判断的细微差别通常是隐性的或隐含的。这些知识在数字记录中只留下微弱的影子，因此在AI模型中，这一关键知识来源仅得到微弱的体现。我们有许多方法为软件系统按预期运行提供保障，尽管大多数方法关注代码规范而非系统需求，更不用说系统对其目的的适用性了。我们未能对各种保障方法的相对优点建立系统性的理解。我希望生成式AI最终将迫使我们解决这个问题。为此，我将挑战我们系统地思考我们的保障技术，特别是隐藏上下文的作用以及AI的挑战。我们需要方法来做出明智的、有理由的选择，以成本效益高的组合方式建立对系统的信心。我们自称为软件工程师。让我们像工程师一样行事。

Original abstract: Software engineering has a complicated relationship with "correctness". We recognize the challenges of full formal rigor as well as many required properties beyond functional correctness. Although we satisfice in practice, we are still stuck in the mindset that we could reason our way to correctness, if only we had enough information. Unfortunately for our hopes of formal rigor, our expectations are shaped by unspoken knowledge that is personal, subjective, qualitative, and largely unavailable. Generative AI has introduced a new dimension to assurance: its foundation is statistical rather than formal. Traditional software engineering establishes confidence through rigorous reasoning, domain knowledge and expert judgment. In contrast, generative AI results are sophisticated predictions, "probably approximately correct". This inherently limits assurances about the results to probabilistic assertions. Further, the nuances that guide human judgment are often tacit or implicit. This knowledge casts only scant shadows into the digital record, so that critical source of knowledge is only faintly represented in AI models. We have many approaches for developing assurances that a software system does what it's expected to do, though most of them focus on code specifications rather than system requirements, let alone the system's fitness for its purpose. We have failed to develop a systematic understanding of the relative merits of the various approaches to assurance. I hope that generative AI will finally force us to tackle this. To that end, I will challenge us to think systematically about our assurance techniques, especially the role of hidden context and the challenges of AI. We need ways to make informed, reasoned choices about cost-effective combinations of approaches to developing confidence in our systems. We call ourselves software engineers. Let's act like engineers.

</details>


### [6] [AI Agent Pull Requests on GitHub: Frequency, Structure, and Merge Conflict Rates](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04697v2)
*George Xu,Arjun Subramanian,Nithilan Karthik*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 该文首次实证分析AI编码智能体并发提交PR的现象，发现多数共现PR来自同一智能体，但跨智能体PR的合并冲突率更高（41.7% vs 19.8%），且大部分冲突源于源代码文件的修改。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺乏对AI编码智能体向同一仓库并发提交PR程度的经验研究。

Method: 使用AIDev-pop数据集（33,596个PR，2,807个仓库），分析PR的时间重叠、冲突比例及类型，并对747个共现对进行git合并重放与冲突分类。

Result: 40.2%的仓库存在共现智能体PR对，占所有AI生成PR的79.4%（精确时间重叠）；一周窗口内升至53.4%和95.0%。共现对中99.5%为同一智能体生成，跨智能体仅占0.5%。跨智能体对文本冲突率41.7%，显著高于同一智能体对的19.8%。冲突文件中84.4%为源代码文件，42%为结构性冲突。

Conclusion: AI编码智能体并发提交PR现象普遍，且跨智能体协作时合并冲突更严重，需进一步研究减少冲突的策略。

中文摘要：AI编码智能体可能同时生成并向同一仓库提交拉取请求（PR）。然而，关于AI编码智能体向公共仓库并发提交程度的研究尚不存在。本文使用AIDev-pop数据集（包含2,807个仓库中的33,596个PR），首次实证考察了由智能体编写的PR的并发提交普遍性。我们报告，在考虑精确时间重叠时，40.2%的仓库包含共现的智能体编写的PR对；此外，共现对占所有AI智能体生成PR的79.4%。当我们检查一周协作窗口内的共现活动时，百分比分别增加到53.4%和95.0%。对于大多数共现PR对（其中绝大多数是同一智能体编写的），两个PR由同一智能体编写，而只有0.5%的共现对是跨智能体的，并且仅出现在2,807个检查仓库中的122个（约4.3%）。此外，我们对747个唯一的共现对（每个仓库一个）进行了实际的三方git合并重放，并计算了合并每个对中两个PR时遇到的文本冲突百分比。我们观察到，跨智能体对相比同一智能体对遇到的文本冲突百分比显著更高：分别为41.7% vs. 19.8%，且95%置信区间不重叠。最后，我们开发了一个基于git检测冲突的分类系统，并确定大多数冲突源于对源代码文件的修改（占冲突文件的84.4%），而非依赖清单文件；此外，我们观察到的近42%冲突是结构性的（即修改/删除或添加/添加）。

Original abstract: AI coding agents may generate and submit Pull Requests (PRs) to the same repository at the same time. However, research concerning the extent of concurrent submission by AI coding agents to a common repository does not exist. This paper uses the AIDev-pop dataset (33,596 PRs in 2,807 repositories) to provide the first empirical examination of the prevalence of concurrent submission using PRs authored by agents. We report that when considering exact temporal overlap, 40.2% of repositories contain co-active agent-authored PR pairs; further, the co-active pairs account for 79.4% of all PRs generated by an AI agent. When we examine co-activity within a one week collaboration window, the percentages are increased to 53.4% and 95.0%, respectively. For the majority of the co-active PR pairs (underlying the vast majority of which are intra-agent authored), both PRs were authored by the same agent, while only 0.5% of co-active pairs were cross-agent, and occurred in only 122 out of 2807 total repositories examined (or approximately 4.3%). Additionally, we replayed actual three way git merges on 747 unique co-active pairs (one per repository), and computed the percentage of textual conflict encountered during the merge operation to combine the two PRs in each pair. We observed that the percentage of textual conflict encountered was significantly higher for cross-agent pairs compared to intra-agent pairs: 41.7% vs. 19.8%, respectively, with non-overlapping 95% confidence intervals. Lastly, we developed a classification system based on the detection of conflict reported by git, and determined that the majority of conflicts resulted from modifications to source code files (84.4% of conflicted files) and not dependency manifest files; further, nearly 42% of conflicts we observed were structural (i.e., modify/delete or add/add).

</details>


### [7] [Dashboard2Code: Evaluating Multimodal Models on Reconstructing Interactive Dashboards](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04727v1)
*Tianhao Niu,Ziyu Han,Qiguang Chen,Shiqi Zhou,Baocai Shan,Hengjie Fang,Qingfu Zhu,Wanxiang Che*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Dashboard2Code任务和DashboardMimic基准，用于从交互式仪表板生成代码，并发现当前模型在高复杂度场景下表现不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动可视化生成主要针对静态图表，忽略了交互式仪表板，而后者在数据探索中更为常见。

Method: 引入Dashboard2Code任务，要求模型通过交互探索生成仪表板代码；构建DashboardMimic基准（180个仪表板-代码对，三个难度等级，八种交互模式）；提出结合代码语义与动态交互测试的自动化评估框架。

Result: 最强模型在高复杂度仪表板上仍表现困难，开源与闭源模型间存在显著性能差距。

Conclusion: Dashboard2Code任务具有挑战性，现有模型需进一步改进以处理交互式仪表板的复杂性。

中文摘要：随着多模态大语言模型的发展，自动数据可视化生成取得了显著进展，然而现有的工作主要关注静态图表，忽略了现实世界数据探索中常用的交互式仪表板。我们引入了Dashboard2Code，这是一个新颖的任务，要求模型主动探索交互式仪表板，获取并整合来自自身交互（如点击和过滤）的反馈，并生成能够复现目标仪表板的代码。为了支持全面评估，我们提出了DashboardMimic，这是首个针对Dashboard2Code的Plotly+Dash基准测试，包含180个精心设计并手动验证的仪表板-代码对，涵盖三个难度级别和八种常见的现实世界交互模式。我们还进一步提出了一种针对仪表板的自适应评估框架，该框架结合代码语义分析与基于动态交互的测试，以评估视觉和交互一致性，并与人工判断高度一致。在多个开源和闭源多模态模型上的实验表明，即使是最强的系统在高复杂度仪表板上也表现困难，并且在Dashboard2Code任务上，开源模型与闭源模型之间仍存在显著的性能差距。

Original abstract: Automatic data visualization generation has advanced rapidly with multi-modal large language models, yet existing efforts largely focus on static charts and overlook the interactive dashboards commonly used for real-world data exploration. We introduce Dashboard2Code, a novel task that requires a model to proactively explore an interactive dashboard, acquire and integrate feedback from its own interactions (e.g., clicking and filtering), and generate code that reproduces the target dashboard. To support comprehensive evaluation, we present DashboardMimic, the first Plotly+Dash benchmark for Dashboard2Code, comprising 180 carefully designed and manually verified dashboard-code pairs spanning three difficulty levels and covering eight common real-world interaction patterns. We further propose an automated evaluation framework tailored to dashboards that combines code semantic analysis with dynamic interaction-based testing to assess visual and interaction consistency, showing strong agreement with human judgments. Experiments across a range of open- and closed-source multi-modal models reveal that even the strongest systems struggle on high-complexity dashboards and that a substantial performance gap remains between open-source and closed-source models on the Dashboard2Code task.

### [8] [Cam2Sim: Neural Scenario Reconstruction for Closed-Loop Autonomous Driving Simulation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04770v1)
*Davide Jannussi,Stefano Carlo Lambertenghi,Constantin Carste,Andrea Stocco*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Cam2Sim通过将真实驾驶记录转化为CARLA仿真场景，利用高斯泼溅渲染缩小仿真与真实世界的视觉差距，提升闭环行为相似性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仿真测试面临合成与真实视觉差距大的问题，限制评估有效性。

Method: 从相机图像和位姿重建场景，结合高斯泼溅增强渲染，支持ROS数据提取、车辆检测、地图生成、场景构建、训练、轨迹重放和闭环测试。

Result: 在真实城市驾驶场景验证，高斯泼溅渲染缩小了视觉差距，提升了行为相似性。

Conclusion: Cam2Sim有效缩小仿真与现实的差距，提供更真实的评估环境。

中文摘要：基于仿真的测试能够安全且可重复地评估自动驾驶系统，但其有效性受到合成仿真器输出与现实相机观测之间差距的限制。为解决这一问题，我们提出了Cam2Sim，一个将真实世界驾驶记录转化为可玩的CARLA仿真场景的工具。从相机图像和位姿出发，Cam2Sim重建道路几何、自车轨迹、停放的车辆以及仿真资产，并通过高斯泼溅（Gaussian Splatting）增强重建环境，以渲染出类似原始记录的相机观测。该框架支持基于ROS的数据提取、停放车辆检测、基于OpenStreetMap的地图生成、CARLA场景构建、高斯泼溅训练、轨迹重放以及与待测系统的闭环执行。我们在一个基于相机的端到端驾驶模型的真实城市驾驶场景上验证了Cam2Sim，比较了重建质量、图像生成质量以及闭环行为，分别与纯仿真基线和真实世界目标进行了对比。结果表明，基于高斯泼溅的渲染缩小了与标准仿真渲染的视觉差距，并提高了与真实世界参考运行的行为相似性。该工件公开于https://github.com/ast-fortiss-tum/cam2sim，演示视频见https://youtu.be/KmZ74l1__lI。

Original abstract: Simulation-based testing enables safe and repeatable evaluation of autonomous driving systems, but its effectiveness is limited by the gap between synthetic simulator outputs and real-world camera observations. To address this problem, we present Cam2Sim, a tool that transforms real-world driving recordings into playable CARLA simulation scenarios. Starting from camera images and poses, Cam2Sim reconstructs road geometry, ego trajectories, parked vehicles, and simulation assets, and augments the reconstructed environment with Gaussian Splatting to render camera observations that resemble the original recording. The framework supports ROS-based data extraction, parked-vehicle detection, OpenStreetMap-based map generation, CARLA scenario construction, Gaussian Splatting training, trajectory replay, and closed-loop execution with a system under test. We validate Cam2Sim on a real-world urban-driving scenario with a camera-based end-to-end driving model, comparing reconstruction quality, image-generation quality, and closed-loop behavior against both a simulation-only baseline and the real-world target. Results show that Gaussian-Splatting-based rendering reduces the visual gap with respect to standard simulator rendering and improves behavioral similarity to the real-world reference runs. The artifact is publicly available at https: //github.com/ast-fortiss-tum/cam2sim, and a screencast showing the tool is available at https://youtu.be/KmZ74l1__lI

### [9] [KAT-Coder-V2.5 Technical Report](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05471v1)
*Bo Huang,Fengxiang Li,Hao Xu,Haoyang Huang,Hongyi Fu,Jinhua Hao,Kun Yuan,Minglei Zhang,Pengcheng Xu,Shiyang Liu,Wenhao Zhuang,Yuze Shi,Zongxian Feng,Chao Wang,Cheng He,Chongling Rao,Deyu Cao,Fan Yang,Gang Xiong,Haochen Liu,Jiabao Li,Jian Liang,Jinghui Jia,Jingwen Chang,Jun Du,Junyu Shi,Min Li,Mingqi Wu,Qiang Gao,Shangpeng Yan,Shaotong Qi,Shu Xu,Shuo Zhou,Tiankuo Xu,Tong Zheng,Weilun Zhao,Xiancheng Meng,Xianda Sun,Xiaoyu Jiang,Xunhao Jia,Yao Xia,Yimeng Xu,Yinghan Cui,Yingpeng Chen,Yiwen Ning,Yong Wang,Yuxuan Sun,Zhongsheng Liu,Ming Sun,Cheng Luo,Chen Yang,Han Li,Kun Gai*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了KAT-Coder-V2.5，一种在真实代码仓库中自主行动的智能体模型，通过端到端后训练框架解决环境、奖励和轨迹稀缺问题，在多个基准上取得领先结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码生成模型局限于单轮生成，缺乏在真实可执行环境中自主行动的能力，且受限于可复现环境、可验证奖励和高价值轨迹的稀缺性。

Method: 采用端到端智能体后训练框架，包括AutoBuilder重构多语言仓库并生成验证任务、KwaiClawEnv合成工具使用轨迹，结合引导随机化、可靠性沙盒、非对称PPO与事后价值估计、面向引导的奖励框架，并通过多教师在线策略蒸馏统一多个专家模型。

Result: 在六个基准测试中，KAT-Coder-V2.5在PinchBench上获得最佳工具使用结果，在仓库级软件工程中仅次于Opus 4.8。

Conclusion: KAT-Coder-V2.5通过创新的后训练框架和强化学习扩展，有效解决了智能体模型在真实环境中的训练瓶颈，取得了可与前沿模型媲美的性能。

中文摘要：我们提出了KAT-Coder-V2.5，这是一个以编码为中心的智能体模型，旨在真实、可执行的代码仓库中自主行动，而非作为单轮代码生成器。其能力瓶颈更多在于可复现环境、可验证奖励和高价值轨迹的稀缺性，而非模型规模本身，我们通过一个端到端的智能体后训练框架来解决这些问题。AutoBuilder将多语言代码仓库重构为沙盒环境，并大规模地进行失败到通过和通过到通过的验证，从中我们重新生成自包含的任务规范、恢复近命中轨迹，并通过基于过程的过滤提取监督信息，而KwaiClawEnv则从可执行服务和真实任务种子中合成大规模工具使用轨迹。我们进一步通过引导随机化、可靠性增强的沙盒、带有事后增强价值估计的非对称Actor-Critic PPO以及面向引导的奖励框架来扩展强化学习，并通过多教师在线策略蒸馏统一了SWE、Agent-Claw和WebCoding专家。在六个软件工程和智能体基准测试中，KAT-Coder-V2.5在PinchBench上取得了最佳智能体工具使用结果，并在仓库级软件工程中仅次于前沿的Opus 4.8。我们的服务可在https://streamlake.com/product/kat-coder获取。

Original abstract: We present KAT-Coder-V2.5, a coding-focused agentic model trained to act autonomously inside real, executable repositories rather than as a single-turn code generator. Its capability is bottlenecked less by model scale than by the scarcity of reproducible environments, verifiable rewards, and high-value trajectories, which we address with an end-to-end agentic post-training framework. AutoBuilder reconstructs multilingual repositories into sandboxed environments with fail-to-pass and pass-to-pass verification at scale, from which we regenerate self-contained task specifications, recover near-miss trajectories, and distill supervision through process-aware filtering, while KwaiClawEnv synthesizes large-scale tool-use trajectories from executable services and real task seeds. We further scale reinforcement learning with harness randomization, a reliability-hardened sandbox, an asymmetric actor--critic PPO with hindsight-augmented value estimation, and a harness-oriented reward framework, and unify SWE, Agent-Claw, and WebCoding experts via Multi-Teacher On-Policy Distillation. Across six software-engineering and agentic benchmarks, KAT-Coder-V2.5 delivers the best agentic tool-use result on PinchBench and ranks second only to the frontier Opus 4.8 on repository-level software engineering. Our service is available at https://streamlake.com/product/kat-coder.

### [10] [A Temporal Reasoning Benchmarking Framework for LRMs via Difficulty-controlled and Dynamic Test Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04784v1)
*Shide Zhou,Kailong Wang,Ling Shi,Haoyu Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出TRACE框架和TRACEBench基准，通过约束满足问题建模时间推理，发现模型性能与难度负相关，并揭示中型模型高虚假猜测率和不同规模模型的失败模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准存在数据污染、难度控制不足及仅关注结果忽视推理过程的问题，需更可靠的评估方法。

Method: 利用Allen区间代数将时间推理建模为约束满足问题，构建含1200个实例的TRACEBench基准，并引入基于轨迹的验证预言机。

Result: 模型性能与难度强负相关（r≈-0.96），中型模型虚假猜测率约28%，且发现小模型退化循环和先进架构推理爆炸等失败模式。

Conclusion: TRACE为评估LRMs的时间推理能力提供了鲁棒自动化的平台，可暴露忽略推理过程的评估缺陷。

中文摘要：定义大型推理模型（LRMs）的推理边界并确保其可靠性仍然是一个关键挑战。当前的基准测试主要依赖易受数据污染的静态数据集或缺乏细粒度难度控制的合成任务。此外，基于结果的标准评估往往忽略推理过程，从而掩盖推理缺陷。为了解决这些局限性，我们引入了TRACE，一个通过Allen区间代数将时间推理建模为约束满足问题的测试框架。该方法能够精确控制逻辑复杂度，并集成了基于轨迹的验证预言机来验证推理的忠实性。利用该框架，我们构建了TRACEBench，一个包含1200个跨梯度难度级别的合成测试实例的广泛基准。我们使用TRACE在TRACEBench上评估了八个广泛使用的LRMs。结果证实模型性能与我们的难度度量之间存在强负相关（Pearson r约-0.96），验证了我们的难度控制机制的有效性。此外，我们的基于轨迹的分析揭示了推理正确性与最终答案之间的显著差异，暴露出中型模型中约28%的高虚假猜测率。此外，我们诊断了规模相关的失败模式，从小模型中的退化循环到先进架构中的推理爆炸。因此，TRACE为基准测试LRMs的真实时间推理能力提供了一个稳健的自动化平台。

Original abstract: Defining the reasoning boundaries and ensuring the reliability of Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) remains a critical challenge. Current benchmarks primarily rely on static datasets susceptible to data contamination or synthetic tasks lacking fine-grained difficulty control. Furthermore, standard outcome-based evaluations often conceal reasoning flaws by neglecting the reasoning process.
  To address these limitations, we introduce TRACE, a testing framework that models temporal reasoning as constraint satisfaction problems via Allen's Interval Algebra. This approach enables precise regulation of logical complexity and incorporates a Trace-Based Verification Oracle to validate reasoning faithfulness. Using this framework, we construct TRACEBench, an extensive benchmark comprising 1,200 synthesized test instances across graded difficulty levels. We employ TRACE to evaluate eight widely used LRMs on TRACEBench. The results confirm a strong negative correlation between model performance and our difficulty metric (Pearson's r approximately -0.96), validating the effectiveness of our difficulty control mechanism. Moreover, our trace-based analysis exposes significant discrepancies between reasoning validity and final answers, revealing a high spurious guessing rate of approximately 28% in mid-sized models. In addition, we diagnose scale-dependent failure modes, ranging from Degenerative Loops in small models to Reasoning Explosion in advanced architectures. TRACE thus provides a robust, automated platform for benchmarking the true temporal reasoning capabilities of LRMs.

</details>


### [11] [An Exploration of Agentic Information Fusion for Test Maintenance Prediction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04786v1)
*Jingxiong Liu,Nasser Mohammadiha,Gregory Gay*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: MAST是一个多智能体框架，通过融合静态、词汇和语义分析，预测生产代码变更后需要维护的测试用例，在工业Java仓库上取得更高精确度、F1和F2分数，仅召回率略有损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测试维护成本高昂且具有挑战性，尤其是生产代码与测试代码关系复杂，现有方法难以准确识别需要维护的测试用例。

Method: 提出MAST多智能体框架，集成静态、词汇和语义分析，通过智能融合和后检查程序，在仓库级别推断测试与生产工件的关系，使用标准化输入格式。

Result: 在21个Ericsson AB工业Java仓库上评估，MAST在精确度、F1和F2分数上优于基线，召回率略有损失；消融实验验证了每种分析的价值。

Conclusion: MAST展示了多智能体系统融合多源信息在软件测试任务中的潜力，能有效预测需要维护的测试用例，降低维护成本。

中文摘要：测试维护是一项关键但成本高昂的活动——尤其是在代码库快速演变的背景下。为此，我们提出了MAST，一个多智能体框架，用于预测哪些测试用例需要在生产代码更改后进行维护。这一识别任务是任何后续维护活动的前提，但由于生产代码与测试代码之间的复杂关系，仍然具有挑战性。MAST通过集成多种分析（包括静态分析、词汇分析和语义分析），通过智能融合和后检查程序，并关注实际使用和评估设置（即标准化输入格式、仓库级分析，以及能够推断测试与生产工件之间的关系而不是假设预先存在的映射），推动了技术发展。我们在来自Ericsson AB的21个工业Java仓库上评估了MAST，考虑了实际情况中测试维护既需要又不需要的情况。MAST在精确度上优于现有技术基线——从而获得更高的准确率、F1和F2分数——仅召回率略有损失。我们的消融研究证明了每种分析在生成最终建议中的价值。MAST展示了多智能体系统在执行软件测试任务时融合多种信息源的潜力。

Original abstract: Test maintenance is a critical, yet costly, activity - particularly as codebases rapidly evolve. To assist, we present MAST, a multi-agent framework that predicts which test cases require maintenance following changes to the production code. This identification task is necessary as a precondition to any subsequent maintenance activities, but remains challenging due to the complex relationships between production and test code. MAST advances the state-of-the-art by integrating multiple analyses -- including static, lexical, and semantic analyses - through an intelligent fusion and post-check procedure and by focusing on a realistic use and evaluation setting - i.e., standardized input formats, repository-level analyses, and the ability to infer relations between test and production artifacts rather than assuming a pre-existing mapping.
  We evaluated MAST on 21 industrial Java repositories from Ericsson AB, considering situations where test maintenance both was and was not required in the ground truth. MAST yielded superior precision to a state-of-the-art baseline - resulting in a higher accuracy, F1, and F2 score - with only some loss in recall. Our ablation study demonstrates the value of each analysis in producing the final recommendations. MAST illustrates the potential of multi-agent systems that can fuse multiple information sources when performing software testing tasks.

</details>


### [12] [E-CoDrive: A Co-Simulation Framework for Testing Energy-Critical Driving Scenarios](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04803v1)

Original abstract: Autonomous driving research has largely focused on safety while giving limited attention to non-functional aspects such as energy consumption and sustainability. As Autonomous Electric Vehicles (AEVs) become increasingly common in urban traffic, understanding how complex traffic dynamics influence their energy consumption is paramount to test whether AEVs can complete trips before battery depletion. To support energy-aware scenario-based testing of AEVs, we present E-CoDrive, a framework for reproducible closed-loop driving co-simulations that integrates an energy consumption model, a micro-traffic simulator, and a high-fidelity driving simulator to test AEV software stacks in urban scenarios. This tool paper describes the architecture of E-CoDrive and demonstrates its applicability by testing an Autoware-based AEV stack. Our evaluation shows that varying traffic conditions produce substantial differences in vehicle energy consumption. The artifact is publicly available at https://doi.org/10.6084/m9.figshare.32244783, and a screencast showing the tool is available at https://youtu.be/yX9fWHqCvgc.

*Kilian Kier,Alessandro Giagnorio,Omar AbedelKader,Oleksandr Zaitsev,Robert Peharz,Romain Robbes,Gabriele Bavota,Stéphane Ducasse*

TL;DR: 本文报告了将LLM代码补全引入低资源语言Pharo的经验，通过数据整理、持续预训练和微调，使小型模型在Pharo补全上显著优于大型模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Pharo等低资源语言缺乏LLM代码补全支持，现有IDE仅提供简单补全。

Method: 构建端到端流水线：Pharo数据整理、持续预训练和微调开源代码LLM；设计Pharo代码补全基准测试。

Conclusion: 将强LLM代码补全引入低资源编程语言是可行的，且可用小型模型实现实时IDE支持。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在自动化代码编写方面开辟了新的可能性，成为大多数代码补全工具的支柱。尽管LLMs在主流语言上表现出色，但它们往往缺乏对所谓低资源语言的支持，因为这些语言的训练数据稀缺。因此，这些语言在可供其社区使用的代码补全工具质量上落后。一个具体例子是Pharo，一种受Smalltalk启发的语言，其IDE目前仅提供单令牌补全。在这项工作中，我们报告了将基于LLM的代码补全引入Pharo的经验。首先，我们描述了一个端到端流水线，该流水线结合了Pharo特定的数据整理、开放代码LLM的持续预训练和微调。其次，我们介绍了一套Pharo代码补全基准测试，旨在评估模型是否（i）学习Pharo语法以及（ii）准确补全来自真实GitHub仓库的掩码Pharo代码。第三，我们通过实证表明，专门针对Pharo的模型在Pharo补全上显著优于其原始基础检查点，并且也超过了规模大得多的代码LLM的准确率。总体而言，我们的案例研究证明了将强大的基于LLM的代码补全引入低资源编程语言的可行性，且模型足够小以提供“实时”的IDE内支持。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) unlocked new possibilities in automated code writing, becoming the backbone of most code completion tools. While LLMs excel in mainstream languages, they often lack support for the so-called low-resource languages where training data is scarce. As a result, these languages lag behind in the quality of code completion tooling available to their communities. A concrete example is Pharo, a Smalltalk-inspired language whose IDE currently offers only single-token completion. In this work, we report on our experience bringing LLM-based code completion to Pharo. First, we describe an end-to-end pipeline that combines Pharo-specific data curation, continued pre-training and fine-tuning of open code LLMs. Second, we introduce a set of Pharo code completion benchmarks designed to evaluate whether models (i) learn Pharo's syntax and (ii) accurately complete masked Pharo code from real-world GitHub repositories. Third, we show empirically that Pharo-specialized models substantially outperform their original base checkpoints and also exceed the accuracy of substantially larger code LLMs on Pharo completion. Overall, our case study demonstrates the feasibility of bringing strong LLM-based code completion to low-resource programming languages, with models small enough to provide ``real-time'' in-IDE support.

### [14] [Using Process Mining to Generate AI Agents from Software Engineering Process Records](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04948v1)

TL;DR: 通过结合多种流程挖掘技术，从软件仓库事件日志中自动发现项目特定的代理角色并生成相应规范与实现，在开源项目中验证了与人类期望的一致性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在成熟开源项目上进行了功能测试和探索性用户研究，生成的代理规范与人类期望具有良好的一致性。

Original abstract: Integrating AI agents into Software Engineering (SE) raises an important challenge: how can we specify and realize AI agents that work effectively alongside humans in hybrid SE teams? Determining the right granularity and separation of concerns for such agents is non-trivial. Coarse-grained agents may introduce unmanageable complexity, whereas micro-agents may create severe coordination overhead. Moreover, existing multi-agent SE frameworks typically rely on predefined role structures and do not account for project-specific characteristics or process adaptations. We address this by combining object-centric, imperative, and declarative process mining. Using event logs extracted from software repositories, our approach discovers project-specific agent roles using a predefined SE role vocabulary grounded in repository behavior and generates matching agent specifications and implementations. As proof-of-concept, we applied our approach to a well-established open-source project. We performed functional tests and an exploratory user study to determine how well the generated AI agent specifications are aligned with human expectations.

### [15] [Real-World Perturbation Testing of Autonomous Driving Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04953v1)
*Stefano Carlo Lambertenghi,Matthias Weil,Andrea Stocco*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 一项大规模研究揭示了扰动测试在离线与实际驾驶之间的差距，表明模型级指标不足以评估真实世界鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究扰动测试结果从离线/仿真到真实驾驶的迁移性问题，因为大多数研究忽略了实际部署中的差异。

Method: 对72种相机和LiDAR扰动在三种测试模态（离线模型级、硬件在环、全尺寸自动驾驶车闭环系统级）上进行评估，覆盖端到端视觉模型和模块化LiDAR系统。

Result: 相机系统离线影响小的扰动仍能导致真实世界故障；LiDAR系统感知退化一致但不易预测系统级故障；模型级指标不足以识别最有害扰动；实时可行性是关键约束；记录数据的鲁棒性不能可靠迁移到物理车辆闭环行为。

Conclusion: 强调了互补的实际世界系统级评估的重要性。

中文摘要：自动驾驶系统（ADS）必须在多种条件下可靠运行，然而针对罕见或不利场景的代表性数据难以获取。基于扰动的测试被广泛用于评估鲁棒性，但大多数研究集中在离线数据集或仿真上，留下了关于这些结果如何转化为真实驾驶的疑问。我们提出了一项大规模研究，涵盖72种相机和LiDAR扰动，并通过三种测试模态进行评估：离线模型级分析、硬件在环执行以及在全尺寸自动驾驶车辆上的闭环系统级测试。该研究涵盖了端到端的基于视觉的驾驶模型和模块化的基于LiDAR的感知与规划堆栈。我们的结果揭示了测试级别之间的明显差距。对于基于相机的系统，离线影响有限的扰动仍可能在实际驾驶中导致不稳定的控制和故障。对于基于LiDAR的系统，退化在感知层面更为一致，但对系统级故障的预测能力较弱。在两种模态中，仅凭模型级指标不足以识别最有害的扰动。我们进一步表明，实时可行性是实际测试中的关键约束，并且从记录数据中获得的鲁棒性观察结果并不一致地转化为物理车辆上的闭环行为，强调了互补的实际世界系统级评估的重要性。

Original abstract: Autonomous Driving Systems (ADS) must operate reliably under diverse conditions, yet representative data for rare or adverse scenarios is difficult to obtain. Perturbation-based testing is widely used to assess robustness, but most studies focus on offline datasets or simulation, leaving open questions about how such results translate to real-world driving. We present a large-scale study of 72 camera and LiDAR perturbations, evaluated across three testing modalities: offline model-level analysis, hardware-in-the-loop execution, and closed-loop system-level testing on a full-scale autonomous vehicle. The study covers both an end-to-end vision-based driving model and a modular LiDAR-based perception and planning stack. Our results reveal a clear gap between testing levels. For camera-based systems, perturbations with limited offline impact can still induce unstable control and failures in real-world driving. For LiDAR-based systems, degradation is more consistent at the perception level but weakly predictive of system-level failures. Across both modalities, model-level metrics alone are insufficient to identify the most harmful perturbations. We further show that real-time feasibility is a key constraint in real-world testing, and that robustness observations obtained from recorded data do not consistently transfer to closed-loop behavior on a physical vehicle, highlighting the importance of complementary real-world, system-level evaluation.

</details>


### [16] [A Comprehensive Study of Implementation Bugs in Multi-modal Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04974v1)
*Suwan Li,Lei Bu,Shangqing Liu,Yile Wang,Guangdong Bai,Fuman Xie,Kai Chen,Chang Yue*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 首个针对多模态智能体实现错误的系统性研究，构建了错误分类法并开发了自动错误识别工具MATester。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态智能体在复杂场景中应用广泛，但其实现错误缺乏系统性研究，导致交通事故和财务损失等风险。

Method: 收集34个代表性M-agent，从1268个问题报告中筛选158个特定错误，采用自上而下策略构建基于症状和根因的分类法，并开发MATester通过分析运行时组件间输出自动识别错误。

Result: MATester在12个额外M-agent上覆盖61.4%已知问题并发现31个新错误。

Conclusion: 研究提供了M-agent错误的全面分类法及实用工具，为错误分类、预防和修复提供指导。

中文摘要：多模态智能体（M-agents）由大型语言模型（LLMs）赋能，在自动驾驶、机器人等复杂、开放世界场景中表现出色。然而，它们与动态、多样的多模态环境交互的独特需求引入了传统智能体之外的新实现挑战。过时的感知、不可信的计划和不适当的执行可能导致交通事故和财务损失。尽管对智能体问题的研究日益增多，但尚未有系统性的研究聚焦于M-agent特定的实现错误。为填补这一空白，我们进行了首个M-agent实现错误的系统性研究。我们从不同来源收集了34个代表性M-agent，通过细致筛选，从1268个问题报告中识别出158个M-agent特定错误。采用自上而下策略，我们开发了一个全面的分类法，按全局症状、功能组件级症状和根本原因对错误进行分类。然后我们实现了MATester，一种通过分析运行时组件间输出来自动识别概念验证错误的工具。将其应用于12个额外的M-agent时，MATester成功覆盖了61.4%的已知未解决问题，并发现了31个额外错误，证明了我们研究的实际效用。我们的工作为M-agent错误的分类、预防和修复提供了全面的参考和指南。

Original abstract: Multi-Modal Agents (M-agents), empowered by Large Language Models (LLMs), excel in various complex, open-world scenarios such as autonomous driving and robotics. However, their unique requirements to interact with dynamic and diverse multi-modal environments introduce novel implementation challenges beyond those faced by traditional agents. Outdated perception, untrustworthy planning and inapplicable execution could cause traffic accident and financial loss. Despite growing study on agent issues, there has not been a systematic study focusing on M-agent-specific implementation bugs. To address this gap, we conducted the first systematic study of implementation bugs in M-agents. We collected 34 representative M-agents from diverse sources and, through meticulous filtering,identified 158 M-agent-specific bugs from 1,268 issue reports. Using a top-down strategy, we developed a comprehensive taxonomy that classifies bugs by global symptoms, functionality component-level symptoms, and root causes. We then implemented MATester, an automatic proof-of-concept bug identifier by analyzing runtime inter-component outputs. When applied to 12 extra M-agents, MATester successfully covered 61.4% of known open issues and discovered 31 additional bugs, demonstrating the practical usefulness of our study. Our work provides a comprehensive reference and guideline for classification, prevention and fix of M-agent bugs.

</details>


### [17] [LLM-Based Test Oracles: Source-of-Authority Taxonomy -- A Systematic Literature Review](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05031v1)
*Ali Hassaan Mughal,Muhammad Bilal*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 对LLM生成测试预言的系统文献综述，分析了54项研究，发现权威来源主要分为规范衍生（占一半）和无规范两类，且权威来源与裁决机制相互交叉，传统标签如“LLM作为法官”仅描述机制而非信任基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究按预言形式或LLM技术组织，但缺乏对预言权威来源的系统分析，无法解释裁决的可信度基础。

Method: 遵循PRISMA 2020指南，从2436条记录经LLM预过滤和双人独立筛选（Cohen's kappa=0.79）及全文评估，最终纳入54项研究，并按权威来源、形式、裁决机制三个轴进行分析。

Result: 规范衍生权威覆盖28/54项研究，其余26项无规范；权威来源与裁决机制呈交叉关系，同一来源可由多种机制检查；多数领域、语言、模型和适应策略被覆盖；预言评估和失败模式被报告。

Conclusion: LLM生成测试预言的权威来源主要分为有规范和无规范两类，且“LLM作为法官”等标签仅指示机制而非信任基础；分类法中稀疏区域为未来研究提供了方向。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被用于生成测试预言（test oracle），即测试中判断观察到的行为是否正确的那部分。然而，关于这些预言从何处获得权威的清晰描述仍然缺失。先前的二次研究按预言形式或LLM技术组织该领域，但没有任何研究按裁决权威的来源（即决定裁决可信度的属性）来组织。本文提出了一项系统文献综述，按照PRISMA 2020指南进行和报告。从2,436条记录中，经过LLM预过滤，随后独立双人筛选（审稿人一致性，Cohen's kappa为0.79）和全文评估，最终纳入54项研究。我们沿着三个轴分析这些研究：预言权威的来源、其采取的形式以及裁决它的机制。我们描述了领域、语言、模型和适应策略的格局。规范衍生权威虽然是最常见的单一来源，但仅覆盖约一半的研究（28/54）。其余26项研究在没有规范的情况下做出裁决。权威来源和裁决机制相互交叉：同一来源由多种机制检查，一种机制服务于多个来源，因此像“LLM作为法官”这样的标签命名了一种机制，而非信任基础。我们进一步报告了这些预言如何被评估以及它们如何失败，并将分类法中稀疏和空白的区域解读为研究议程。协议、搜索查询和每项研究的编码表作为补充材料发布。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to produce test oracles, the part of a test that decides whether observed behavior is correct. Yet a clear account of where these oracles draw their authority is missing. Prior secondary studies organize the area by oracle form or by LLM technique. None organizes it by the source of the verdict's authority, the property that governs how far a verdict can be trusted. This article presents a systematic literature review, conducted and reported under the PRISMA 2020 guidelines. From 2,436 records, an LLM pre-filter followed by independent dual human screening (reviewer agreement, a Cohen's kappa of 0.79) and full-text assessment yielded 54 included studies. We analyze these along three axes: the source of an oracle's authority, the form it takes, and the mechanism that adjudicates it. We characterize the landscape of domains, languages, models, and adaptation strategies. Specification-derived authority, though the most common single source, covers about half of the studies (28 of 54). The remaining 26 reach a verdict with no specification at all. The source of authority and the adjudication mechanism cross-cut: the same source is checked by several mechanisms and one mechanism serves several sources, so a label such as LLM-as-a-judge names a mechanism rather than a basis for trust. We further report how these oracles are evaluated and how they fail, and read the sparse and empty regions of the taxonomy as a research agenda. The protocol, search query, and per-study coding sheet are released as supplementary material.

</details>


### [18] [When AI Is Wrong on Purpose: How Students Respond to Buggy GenAI Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05068v1)
*Victor-Alexandru Pădurean,Kaitlin Riegel,Alkis Gotovos,Jyotika Mahapatra,Ahana Ghosh,Paul Denny,Juho Leinonen,James Prather,Adish Singla*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过注入错误和利用提示失败，让学生练习审查和修复GenAI生成代码，从而培养代码理解和调试技能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GenAI生成代码可能看似正确但有缺陷，CS1学生缺乏检查动力；需要调整活动来培养验证和修复实践。

Method: 在正确解决方案中注入可运行错误，分析学生行为（2,636个会话，917名学生），比较自然提示失败和注入错误的影响。

Result: 注入错误导致直接代码编辑和更高成功；提示失败导致完善提示。学生反思认为有助于代码理解、审查、调试和增强谨慎心态。

Conclusion: 提示失败和注入错误共同支持教学上有用的GenAI工作流程，结合提示细化和代码调试。

中文摘要：随着生成式人工智能（GenAI）在软件开发中变得越来越核心，计算机科学教育正在整合以提示（prompt）为中心的工作流程，学生用自然语言描述预期的程序行为以生成代码。然而，专业实践要求仔细审查和验证GenAI生成的代码，这些代码可能看似正确但包含细微缺陷。这给CS1级别的活动带来了挑战，因为当前模型通常能正确完成任务，从而降低了学生仔细检查生成输出的动力。我们研究了如何调整以提示为中心的编程活动以更好地培养这些实践。具体来说，我们探索了一种方法，即在其他正确的解决方案中注入现实的、可运行的错误，从而要求学生阅读和修复生成的输出。我们分析了来自917名学生的2,636个会话，并检查了每个会话中自然发生的与提示相关的失败和故意注入的错误的行为。我们的研究结果表明，学生对不同来源的错误反应不同。故意注入的错误更常导致直接的代码编辑和更高的下一次尝试成功率，表明对接近正确的解决方案进行局部修复。而与提示相关的失败则更常导致学生通过澄清约束、更新函数签名、添加边缘情况或重新定义任务来完善提示。学生的反思强化了对审查和修复的重视，描述了在代码理解、代码审查和调试方面的有用实践，以及更谨慎的验证心态和对GenAI限制的更大意识。最终，与提示相关的失败和注入的错误共同支持了一个在教学上有用的GenAI工作流程，学生在该流程中既通过提示练习规范细化，也通过代码编辑练习调试。

Original abstract: As Generative AI (GenAI) becomes increasingly central to software development, CS education is integrating prompt-centered workflows where students describe intended program behavior in natural language to elicit code. However, professional practice requires careful review and verification of GenAI-generated code that may appear correct while containing subtle faults. This creates a challenge for CS1-level activities, where current models often solve tasks correctly and reduce students' incentive to closely inspect generated outputs. We investigate how prompt-centered programming activities can be adapted to better foster these practices. Specifically, we explore an approach where realistic, runnable bugs are injected into otherwise correct solutions, thus requiring students to read and repair generated outputs. We analyzed 2,636 sessions from 917 students, and examined behavior across instances of naturally occurring prompt-related failures and deliberately injected bugs within each session. Our findings show that students responded differently across bug sources. Deliberately injected bugs more often led to direct code edits and higher next-attempt success, suggesting localized repair of near-miss solutions. Prompt-related failures instead more often led students to refine prompts by clarifying constraints, updating function signatures, adding edge cases, or reframing the task. Student reflections reinforce the emphasis on review and repair, describing useful practice in code understanding, code review, and debugging, as well as a more careful verification mindset and greater awareness of GenAI limitations. Ultimately, prompt-related failures and injected bugs together support a pedagogically useful GenAI workflow, where students practice both specification refinement through prompts and debugging through code editing.

</details>


### [19] [Can Code Specify a System Precisely Enough to Formally Verify It?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05076v1)
*Jean-Jacques Dubray*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文评估了大语言模型在生产软件（餐厅POS支付系统）上编写形式化规约的可靠性，发现规约契约的结构（而非语言）决定可靠性，并通过审计发现了七个故障处理缺口，其中三个被重现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 形式化验证很少用于生产软件，因为成本高；伴随研究提出低成本替代（基于轨迹的规约），但需在真实生产环境中评估其可靠性及LLM编写规约的能力。

Method: 对生产级POS系统的支付工作流进行形式化审计：构建手写模型，定义故障模型，使用LLM生成规约，并比较不同模型和契约结构的表现；同时测试了故障模型扩展（崩溃重启、脏读、两次尝试）和实时API探针。

Result: 核心协议在指定故障模型下正确，但发现七个故障处理缺口（三个被重现）；生产沙箱暴露了响应形状差异导致恢复不可达；复现了伴随研究结论：契约结构（而非语言）决定LLM规约可靠性，但最强模型才能达到语料库上限。

Conclusion: LLM编写生产软件规约的可靠性主要由规约契约的结构（而非语言）决定，但需要更强的模型才能达到高可靠性；基于模拟器的审计可能因相关预言机而遗漏实际API问题。

中文摘要：形式化验证很少应用于生产软件，因为历史上编写和维护模型的成本高于其回报。一项伴随研究[1]扩展了SysMoBench[4]，提出了一种低成本替代方案：根据从运行系统中捕获的轨迹对规约进行分级。该研究发现，当大型语言模型编写规约时，可靠性由规约契约的结构决定，而非语言本身。本文在生产软件上评估了这两者：一个运营中的餐厅销售点系统的支付工作流，该系统必须保持收银机、支付终端和支付处理器之间的一致性。我们报告三个结果。第一，相对于手工构建的、行级引用的模型，在精确陈述的故障模型下，核心协议是正确的。审计发现了七个故障处理缺口，几乎都有共同的根源；其中三个被重现为真实执行，一个修补程序在启用所有故障门的情况下重新检查后关闭了它们，随后一个后续修补程序关闭了重新检查本身暴露的缺陷。对故障模型的系统扩展（崩溃重启、脏读、两次尝试）各自找到了它们设计要探测的窗口。第二，对生产支付沙箱的一次探测暴露了一个响应形状差异，使得整个恢复阶梯对实时API不可达。基于模拟器的审计无法检测到这一点，因为代码和模拟器共享了相同的误读：相关预言机故障。第三，伴随研究的核心发现在来自两个供应商的七个模型上得到了复现：契约结构（而非语言）决定了LLM可靠地规约的内容。复现涉及契约的排序和故障分类，而非绝对水平：只有最强的模型达到了语料库上限，而更困难的任务恢复了基准已失去的区分能力。

Original abstract: Formal verification is seldom applied to production software, because writing and maintaining a model has historically cost more than it returns. A companion study [1] extended SysMoBench [4] with a lower-cost alternative: specifications are graded against traces captured from the running system. It found that when large language models write the specifications, reliability is governed by the structure of the specification contract, not the language. This paper evaluates both on production software: the payment workflow of an operational restaurant point-of-sale system, which must keep the register, payment terminal, and payment processor in agreement. We report three results. First, the core protocol is correct relative to a hand-built, line-cited model under a precisely stated failure model. The audit found seven failure-handling gaps, nearly all with a common root cause; three were reproduced as real executions, and a patch closing them was re-checked with all failure gates enabled, after which a follow-up patch closed a defect the re-check itself exposed. Systematic extensions of the failure model (crash-restart, stale reads, two attempts) each found the windows they were designed to probe. Second, a single probe of the production payment sandbox exposed a response-shape divergence that makes an entire recovery ladder unreachable against the live API. The emulator-based audit could not detect it, because code and emulator share the same misreading: a correlated-oracle failure. Third, the companion study's central finding replicates across seven models from two vendors: contract structure, not language, governs what LLMs specify reliably. The replication concerns the ordering of contracts and the failure taxonomy, not the absolute level: only the strongest models reached the corpus ceiling, and the harder task restores discriminating power the benchmark had lost.

</details>


### [20] [RepoTrace: Browser-Assisted Evidence Collection for GitHub Research Datasets](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05106v1)
*Xue Yao,Zehua Zhang,Jiatong Liu,Yongqiang Tian*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: RepoTrace是一个浏览器辅助工具，用于收集GitHub问题和PR证据到本地SQLite工作区，支持快照、注释、筛选等，验证显示能支持完整本地证据收集工作流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有手动构建GitHub数据集的流程中，证据、代码和决策理由分散在多处，导致溯源、更新和多人标记难以审计。

Method: RepoTrace结合Chrome侧面板扩展、Express后端和React仪表板，捕获页面快照、评论、标签、笔记、筛选/标记决策等，并存储到本地SQLite数据库。

Result: 验证收集了20个Matplotlib问题，产生22个快照、38条评论、20条笔记、98个注释、20个筛选等，模拟了4个未解决的共识冲突。

Conclusion: RepoTrace能够支持手动构建GitHub问题和PR数据集的完整本地证据收集工作流程。

中文摘要：经验软件工程研究经常从GitHub的问题和拉取请求中构建数据集。在许多项目中，研究人员在浏览器中检查页面，将选定的字段复制到电子表格中，在单独的文档中保留旁注，并随后运行脚本以规范化或导出数据。这种工作流程很灵活，但页面证据、研究代码以及每个决策背后的理由最终分散在标签页和文件中，这使得溯源、更新跟踪和多审查者标记难以审计。RepoTrace是一个浏览器辅助研究工具，它将GitHub问题和拉取请求证据收集到本地SQLite支持的工作空间中。它结合了Chrome侧面板扩展、Express后端和React仪表板，以捕获页面快照、评论、标签、笔记、筛选和标记决策、刷新历史以及范围导出，将源证据和研究解释联系在一起。一项验证过程收集并检查了两个研究项目中的20个Matplotlib问题。生成的数据集保留了22个快照、38条评论、20条研究笔记、98个注释、20个筛选评审、20个修复证据条目以及4个模拟的未解决共识冲突。结果表明，RepoTrace可以支持手动构建的GitHub问题和拉取请求数据集的完整本地证据收集工作流程。

Original abstract: Empirical software engineering studies frequently build datasets from GitHub issues and pull requests. In many projects, researchers inspect pages in a browser, copy selected fields into spreadsheets, keep side notes in separate documents, and later run scripts to normalize or export the data. This workflow is flexible, but the page evidence, the research codes, and the rationale behind each decision end up spread across tabs and files, which leaves provenance, update tracking, and multi-reviewer labeling hard to audit.
  RepoTrace is a browser-assisted research tool that collects GitHub issue and pull-request evidence into a local SQLite-backed workspace. It combines a Chrome side-panel extension, an Express backend, and a React dashboard to capture page snapshots, comments, labels, notes, screening and labeling decisions, refresh history, and scoped exports, keeping the source evidence and the research interpretation linked together.
  A validation pass collected and checked 20 Matplotlib issues across two study projects. The resulting dataset preserves 22 snapshots, 38 comments, 20 research notes, 98 annotations, 20 screening reviews, 20 fix-evidence entries, and 4 simulated unresolved consensus conflicts. The results show that RepoTrace can support a complete local evidence-collection workflow for manually constructed GitHub issue and pull-request datasets.

### [21] [From Failing to Passing: Evolving Natural Language Prompt Optimization Rules for LLM Code Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05121v1)
*Amal Akli,Melissa Akli,Cedric Richter,Mike Papadakis,Yves Le Traon*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出DUALFIX，通过演化自然语言转换规则并结合执行反馈修复，显著提升代码修复性能，规则可跨模型零样本迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型对提示措辞敏感，这种敏感性可能被利用来改善性能，且现有执行反馈修复存在局限性。

Method: 采用基于搜索的方法演化一组自然语言转换规则，并将其与执行反馈修复结合，构建分阶段修复流水线DUALFIX，同时处理规范级和实现级失败。

Result: 在LiveCodeBench和APPS上，DUALFIX修复10-30%的失败案例（其中12-17%无法被纯执行修复解决），恢复高达30%的基线失败，修复数量是Self-Fix的3-5倍，且规则可零样本迁移至其他模型。

Conclusion: DUALFIX是通用且有效的代码修复方法，其演化规则可跨问题重用、跨模型迁移，显著优于现有执行反馈修复基线。

中文摘要：大型语言模型已知对提示表述敏感。即使是措辞的微小变化也会显著降低性能。这种敏感性揭示了一个机会：如果提示措辞可能损害性能，那么它能被用来改善性能吗？为了研究这个问题，我们引入了一种基于搜索的方法，该方法识别并演化一组自然语言转换规则，这些规则对编码性能具有强大的下游影响。然后我们提出了DUALFIX，一个分阶段的修复流水线，将演化的转换规则与执行反馈修复相结合，处理规范级别和实现级别的失败。我们方法的一个关键优势在于其通用性：演化的规则与错误无关，可跨问题重用，并且可跨模型迁移。我们在三个模型上针对两个具有挑战性的基准（LiveCodeBench和APPS）评估了DUALFIX与执行反馈修复基线。我们的结果表明，演化的转换修复了10-30%的失败案例，其中包括12-17%的仅靠基于执行的修复无法解决的失败。总体而言，DualFix恢复了基线失败中高达30%的部分，并且在所有评估设置中修复的失败案例数量是Self-Fix的3-5倍。此外，我们还表明，在一个模型上演化的规则可以零样本迁移到其他模型，无需任何重新优化即优于执行反馈修复。

Original abstract: Large language models are known to be sensitive to prompt formulation. Even minor variations in wording can substantially degrade performance. This sensitivity reveals an opportunity: if prompt phrasing can harm performance, can it be used to improve it? To investigate this question, we introduce a search-based approach that identifies and evolves a set of natural language transformation rules with strong downstream effects on coding performance. We then propose DUALFIX, a staged repair pipeline that combines the evolved transformation rules with execution-feedback repair, addressing both specification-level and implementation-level failures. A key strength of our approach lies in its generality: the evolved rules are error-agnostic, reusable across problems, and transferable across models. We evaluate DUALFIX against execution-feedback repair baselines across three models on two challenging benchmarks, LiveCodeBench and APPS. Our results show that the evolved transformations fix from 10-30% of failing cases, including 12-17% of failures that execution-based repair alone cannot resolve. Overall, DualFix recovers up to 30% of baseline failures and fixes 3-5 times more failing cases than Self-Fix across all evaluated settings. Furthermore, we also show that rules evolved on one model transfer zero-shot to other models, outperforming execution-feedback repair without any re-optimization.

</details>


### [22] [Three-Phase Evaluation of AI-Assisted Software Development Life Cycle](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05125v1)
*Joshua Strubel,Professor Carrie Russell,Carson Crockett,Jason Ferraro,Nathan Londhe,Uzayr Syed,Jacob Viehe*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文评估了AI自主性水平对软件开发的影响，发现更高自主性减少工作量、改善需求遵循，但增加挫折感，且工具架构有独立影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索AI自主性水平如何影响软件开发的生产力、需求遵循度和开发者认知工作负荷。

Method: 四名开发者在三个连续阶段中重新实现相同的全栈Web应用：部分AI辅助（GitHub Copilot）、AI独占（GitHub Copilot）和AI独占（AWS Kiro），通过开发工作量、RITM分数、AI交互效率和NASA-TLX进行评估。

Result: 更高AI自主性关联减少开发工作量、改善需求遵循度和降低心理工作负荷，但开发者挫折感增加；AWS Kiro阶段在多数维度表现最佳。

Conclusion: 工具架构可能独立于AI自主性水平影响结果。

中文摘要：本文提出了一项探索性评估，研究AI自主性水平的提升如何影响软件开发生产力、需求遵循度和开发者认知工作负荷。一个由四名开发者组成的团队在三个连续阶段中重新实现了相同的全栈Web应用：使用GitHub Copilot的部分AI辅助开发、使用GitHub Copilot的AI独占工作流、以及使用AWS Kiro的AI独占工作流。评估指标包括开发工作量（小时）、需求遵循度（RITM分数）、AI交互效率以及NASA-TLX工作负荷测量。在各阶段中，更高的AI自主性水平与减少的开发工作量、改善的需求遵循度以及更低的自报心理工作负荷相关，而开发者挫折感略有增加。AWS Kiro阶段在大多数测量维度上取得了最强的整体表现，这表明工具架构可能独立于AI自主性水平影响结果。

Original abstract: This paper presents an exploratory evaluation of how increasing levels of AI autonomy affect software development productivity, requirement adherence, and developer cognitive workload. A team of four developers reimplemented the same full-stack web application across three sequential phases: partial AI-assisted development using GitHub Copilot, an AI-exclusive workflow using GitHub Copilot, and an AI-exclusive workflow using AWS Kiro. Evaluation metrics included development effort (hours), requirement adherence (RITM score), AI-interaction efficiency, and NASA-TLX workload measures. Across phases, higher levels of AI autonomy were associated with reduced development effort, improved requirement adherence, and lower self-reported mental workload, while developer frustration increased modestly. The AWS Kiro phase achieved the strongest overall performance on most measured dimensions, suggesting that tooling architecture may influence outcomes independently of AI autonomy level.

### [23] [On the risk of coding before testing: An empirical study on LLM-based test generation workflow](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05139v1)
*Michael Konstantinou,Florian Tambon,Mike Papadakis*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: LLM生成的代码会偏差后续测试生成，导致错误传播，使故障检测率从独立测试的25%降至14%，揭示当前工作流中缺乏独立性的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战“生成的测试是独立可靠预言”的假设，研究LLM生成代码是否偏差测试生成。

Method: 通过实验研究错误传播现象，比较独立生成测试与在错误代码后生成测试的故障检测率，使用不同提示策略和多步工作流。

Result: 错误代码后生成测试的故障检测率（14%）显著低于独立生成（25%），错误传播普遍且影响显著。

Conclusion: 当前工作流缺乏独立性，损害自动化测试可靠性；指出了耦合生成管道实证研究中的有效性威胁。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）日益被用于软件工程工作流程中，以生成源代码和测试套件。这种双重能力催生了新兴的开发范式，包括测试优先和代理工作流，其中单个模型同时产生和验证实现。然而，这些方法假设生成的测试作为独立且可靠的预言——这是有效软件测试的基本要求。在本文中，我们挑战这一假设，并研究LLM生成的代码是否会对后续测试的生成产生偏差。我们引入并实证研究了错误传播现象，即生成代码中的缺陷被系统地复制到相关的测试工件中。这导致错误实现和测试相互一致，掩盖缺陷而不是揭示缺陷。我们在一系列编程任务和代理工作流中评估了这一效应，分析了生成代码与测试断言之间的一致性，特别关注对齐失败的情景。我们的研究考察了（i）错误的代码工件是否会使测试生成产生偏差，（ii）这种偏差是否在不同的提示策略（包括思维链推理）下持续存在，以及（iii）错误如何在多步工作流中传播，其中中间输出被重用为上下文。结果表明，错误传播普遍且影响显著：与独立生成测试相比，在错误代码之后生成测试会显著降低故障检测有效性（14%对25%）。这些发现揭示了当前工作流的一个基本局限性，即生成工件之间缺乏独立性损害了自动化测试的可靠性。此外，我们的结果暴露了依赖耦合生成管道的实证研究中一个此前未被充分探索的有效性威胁。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used in software engineering workflows to generate both source code and test suites. This dual capability has enabled emerging development paradigms, including test-first and agentic workflows, where a single model is producing and validating implementations. However, these approaches assume that generated tests act as independent and reliable oracles - a fundamental requirement for effective software testing. In this paper, we challenge this assumption and investigate whether LLM-generated code biases the generation of subsequent tests. We introduce and empirically study the phenomenon of error propagation, where faults in generated code are systematically replicated in associated test artifacts. This leads to cases where incorrect implementations and tests are mutually consistent, masking defects rather than revealing them. We evaluate this effect across a range of programming tasks and agentic workflows, analyzing the consistency between generated code and test assertions, with particular focus on scenarios of aligned failures. Our study examines (i) whether erroneous code artifacts bias test generation, (ii) whether such bias persists under different prompting strategies, including chain-of-thought reasoning, and (iii) how errors propagate across multi-step workflows in which intermediate outputs are reused as context. The results show that error propagation is prevalent and impactful: generating tests after faulty code significantly reduces fault detection effectiveness compared to generating tests independently (14% vs. 25%). These findings highlight a fundamental limitation of current workflows, where lack of independence between generated artifacts undermines the reliability of automated testing. Furthermore, our results expose a previously underexplored threat to validity in empirical studies relying on coupled generation pipelines.

</details>


### [24] [Intent-Based Mutation Testing: From Naturally Written Programming Intents to Mutants](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05149v1)
*Asma Hamidi,Ahmed Khanfir,Mike Papadakis*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出基于意图的变异测试，通过改变编程意图而非语法来生成变异，利用LLM实现，实验表明其能覆盖传统变异未包含的55%变异，作为传统变异测试的补充。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统变异测试仅改变程序语法，无法捕获与编程意图相关的故障类别；意图变异通过改变意图可覆盖不同类别的故障，弥补传统方法不足。

Method: 使用大型语言模型（LLMs）对编程意图进行变异，生成实现不同意图的变异体，并转换为可执行程序。

Result: 在29个程序上评估，生成的变异语法复杂、语义多样，与传统变异语义差异大；55%的意图变异不被传统变异包含。

Conclusion: 基于意图的变异测试能有效补充传统变异测试，捕获更多故障类型，具有作为强大互补工具的潜力。

中文摘要：本文提出了一种基于意图的变异测试，这是一种通过改变被测试程序中实现的编程意图来生成变异的测试方法。与传统的改变（变异）程序编写方式的变异测试不同，意图变异通过生成实现与原始程序略有不同的意图的变异来改变（变异）程序的行为。编程意图的变异代表了程序行为的可能边界情况和误解，即程序规约，因此能够捕获与传统的（基于语法的）变异不同的故障类别。此外，由于编程意图可以以不同的方式实现，基于意图的变异测试可以生成多样且复杂的变异，这些变异接近于原始的编程意图（规约），从而将测试导向程序行为/规约的意图变体。我们使用大型语言模型（LLMs）实现基于意图的变异测试，这些模型对编程意图进行变异并将其转化为变异体。我们在29个程序上评估了基于意图的变异，并展示了它生成的变异在语法上复杂、语义上多样，并且在语义上与传统的变异有很大不同。我们还展示了55%的基于意图的变异没有被传统变异所包含。总体而言，我们的分析表明，基于意图的变异测试可以成为传统的（基于语法的）变异测试的有力补充。

Original abstract: This paper presents intent-based mutation testing, a testing approach that generates mutations by changing the programming intents that are implemented in the programs under test. In contrast to traditional mutation testing, which changes (mutates) the way programs are written, intent mutation changes (mutates) the behavior of the programs by producing mutations that implement (slightly) different intents than those implemented in the original program. The mutations of the programming intents represent possible corner cases and misunderstandings of the program behavior, i.e., program specifications, and thus can capture different classes of faults than traditional (syntax-based) mutation. Moreover, since programming intents can be implemented in different ways, intent-based mutation testing can generate diverse and complex mutations that are close to the original programming intents (specifications) and thus direct testing towards the intent variants of the program behavior/specifications. We implement intent-based mutation testing using Large Language Models (LLMs) that mutate programming intents and transform them into mutants. We evaluate intent-based mutation on 29 programs and show that it generates mutations that are syntactically complex, semantically diverse, and quite different (semantically) from the traditional ones. We also show that 55% of the intent-based mutations are not subsumed by traditional mutations. Overall, our analysis shows that intent-based mutation testing can be a powerful complement to traditional (syntax-based) mutation testing.

</details>


### [25] [Is Three the Magic Number? An Empirical Evaluation of LLM-Based Repair Loops](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05197v1)
*Tobias Kiecker,Eik Reichmann,Hosung Kang,Gabin An,Lars Grunske*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: LLM-based软件工程中的迭代修复存在收益递减，前3-4次迭代效果显著，后续改进有限，且修复行为更多受工作流和反馈设计影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对修复迭代次数的影响了解不足，常采用固定且任意的修复预算，缺乏系统分析。

Method: 在代码生成、测试生成和代码翻译等任务上，使用多个工作流、数据集和低成本LLM进行实验，观察修复迭代与性能的关系。

Result: 前三到四次修复迭代带来大部分收益，后续迭代改进微小；修复行为受工作流编排和反馈设计影响大于模型本身。

Conclusion: 修复预算应作为显式变量处理，因其直接影响评估结果、成本、运行时间和可重复性。

中文摘要：迭代修复循环已成为基于LLM的软件工程系统中的核心设计模式。这些工作流反复生成、验证和修复工件，使用诸如编译器错误或测试失败等反馈。尽管它们被广泛使用，但修复循环迭代限制的影响仍然知之甚少，因为大多数先前的工作采用固定的、通常是任意的修复预算。我们研究了跨多个软件工程任务（包括代码生成、测试生成和代码翻译）的修复循环有效性。在几个代表性的工作流、数据集和当代低成本LLM中，我们观察到一致的收益递减模式：前三到四次修复迭代贡献了大部分可实现的收益，而后续迭代仅带来边际改进。我们进一步发现，修复行为受工作流编排和反馈设计的影响比底层模型本身更强。这些结果表明，修复预算应被视为显式的实验变量，因为它们直接影响基于LLM的软件工程研究中的评估结果、计算成本、运行时间和可重复性。

Original abstract: Iterative repair loops have become a core design pattern in LLM-based software engineering systems. These workflows repeatedly generate, validate, and repair artifacts using feedback such as compiler errors or test failures. Despite their widespread use, the impact of repair-loop iteration limits remains poorly understood, as most prior work adopts fixed, often arbitrary, repair budgets. We study repair-loop effectiveness across multiple software engineering tasks, including code generation, test generation, and code translation. Across several representative workflows, datasets, and contemporary low-cost LLMs, we observe a consistent pattern of diminishing returns: the first three to four repair iterations account for most achievable gains, while later iterations contribute only marginal improvements. We further find that repair behavior is influenced more strongly by workflow orchestration and feedback design than by the underlying model itself. These results suggest that repair budgets should be treated as an explicit experimental variable, as they directly affect evaluation outcomes, computational cost, runtime, and reproducibility in LLM-based software engineering research.

*Bengt Haraldsson,Srijita Basu,Miroslaw Staron,Erika Mayer*

TL;DR: 研究了开发AUTOSAR Adaptive应用时的痛点，发现源于规范、实现和本地实践的混合因素，并提出了通过工具改进配置管理和减少培训时间的缓解建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用设计科学研究方法，开发了一个最小化的AUTOSAR Adaptive Platform作为实验原型，通过实践调查痛点来源。

Result: 痛点源于规范固有因素（架构选择和复用目标）、供应商实现以及本地使用实践的组合。

Conclusion: AUTOSAR规范存在固有痛点，开发组织需通过改进配置管理工具和降低培训时间来缓解，以帮助开发者理解自适应应用的运行时生命周期。

中文摘要：汽车行业对软件作为区分因素的依赖正在增加。在同时依赖供应商提供的软件和成本效益实现的情况下，AUTOSAR联盟成立，旨在提供标准化平台规范以实现复用。具体来说，AUTOSAR自适应平台（AP）规范旨在提供高性能的服务导向架构。
目的：本研究的目标是调查在开发AUTOSAR自适应应用程序时出现的痛点，以及这些痛点是否源于平台规范、其供应商实现或其本地使用。方法：我们进行了一项设计科学研究，开发了一个最小的AP作为实验原型用于调查。

结论：我们得出结论，存在AUTOSAR规范固有的痛点原因，这些原因源于架构选择和复用目标。对开发组织而言，其含义是需要通过更好地支持配置文件管理和减少开发者理解自适应应用程序运行时生命周期所需的培训时间的工具来减轻这些影响。

Original abstract: The reliance on software as a distinguishing factor in the automotive industry is increasing. With a combined reliance on vendor-supplied software and cost-effective implementation, the AUTOSAR consortium was initialized to provide standardized platform specifications that enable re-use. Specifically, the AUTOSAR Adaptive Platform (AP) specification aims to provide a high-performance service-oriented architecture.
  Objective: The goal of this study is to investigate what pain-points emerge when developing AUTOSAR Adaptive applications and whether they originate from the platform specification, its vendor-implementation, or its local usage. Methods: We conduct a Design Science Research study, developing a minimal AP that serves as an experimental prototype for our investigation.
  Results: We find that a combination of specification-inherent, implementation-based, and local practices contributes to the emergence of pain-points.
  Conclusions: We conclude that there are AUTOSAR specification-inherent reasons for pain-points, resulting from architectural choices and re-use goals. The implication for development organizations is the need to mitigate these effects through tooling that better supports configuration file management and reduces developer training time to properly understand the adaptive application runtime life-cycle.

### [27] [TypeGo: An OS Runtime for Embodied Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05482v1)
*Guojun Chen,Alex Schott,Lin Zhong*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出TypeGo，一个操作系统风格运行时，通过异步循环、技能内核和推测性技能流，实现具身代理的低延迟LLM规划与并发任务执行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将LLM作为请求/响应预言机用于规划，无法满足具身代理的实时控制和并发目标。

Method: 设计操作系统风格运行时TypeGo，包括多时间尺度异步循环、技能内核仲裁类型化物理子系统、调度器抢占/恢复进程、推测性技能流隐藏延迟，以及快速首动路径。

Result: 在Kalos四足机器人上，每步延迟降低50%，首次动作时间减少73%，并支持低开销并发任务。

Conclusion: TypeGo的初步验证表明，该设计能有效提升LLM规划在具身代理中的实时性和并发能力。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）可以从自然语言规划具身代理的行为，但将LLM视为关键路径上的请求/响应预言机从根本上不符合实时控制和并发目标。我们论证了具身代理的操作系统风格运行时，并在早期原型TypeGo中实例化了这一想法。TypeGo将基于LLM的规划结构为多个时间尺度的异步循环，这些循环与执行重叠，并像操作系统管理硬件一样管理代理的物理身体：技能内核仲裁并发任务进程中的类型化物理子系统，调度器根据来源抢占、恢复或替换它们，推测性技能流将LLM延迟隐藏在持续运动背后，而快速首动路径在一秒内产生可见反馈。用户通过自然语言指令编程行为，TypeGo将其分派给基于LLM的规划器或编译为低延迟中断处理程序。我们对Kalos（Unitree Go2四足机器人）的原型提供了该设计的初步证据：在当前任务套件中，与逐步规划相比，它减少了50%的每步延迟，与整体规划相比，首次动作时间减少了73%，同时以低调度开销接纳并发任务。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can plan behavior for embodied agents from natural language, but treating the LLM as a request/response oracle on the critical path is fundamentally at odds with real-time control and concurrent goals. We argue for an operating-system-style runtime for embodied agents, and instantiate this idea in an early prototype, TypeGo. TypeGo structures LLM-based planning as asynchronous loops at multiple timescales that overlap with execution, and manages the agent's physical body like an OS manages hardware: the Skill Kernel arbitrates typed physical subsystems among concurrent per-task processes, a scheduler preempts them and resumes or replaces each by source, and speculative skill streaming hides LLM latency behind ongoing motion, while a fast first-action path yields visible feedback within a second. Users program behavior through natural language prescriptions that TypeGo dispatches to the LLM-based planners or compiles into low-latency interrupt handlers. Our prototype of Kalos, a Unitree Go2 quadruped, provides preliminary evidence for the design: in our current task suite, it cuts per-step delay by 50% over step-by-step planning and time-to-first-action by 73% over monolithic planning, while admitting concurrent tasks at low scheduling overhead.

</details>


### [28] [A Mechanistic Lens on Semantic Conflicts: Using Activation Patching to Understand LLM Behavior](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05587v1)
*Youssef Abdelsalam,Norman Peitek,Anna-Maria Maurer,Marvin Wyrich,Sven Apel*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 首次受控机制性研究LLM在语义冲突下的行为，发现语义冲突降低执行正确性，LLM常被误导性语义线索主导，且因果信号集中在少数残差流状态中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究LLM处理可执行代码与非可执行语义线索冲突时的行为，明确哪种来源主导输出以及冲突如何影响模型性能。

Method: 构建45个Python片段三元组隔离冲突，评估四个开源LLM在输出预测和单元测试生成任务上的行为，使用行为度量和残差流激活修补进行因果分析。

Result: 语义冲突显著降低两个任务的执行正确性，所有LLM倾向于跟随误导语义线索；因果信号集中在改变的线索/代码区域和少量中间标记，在输出聚合前可恢复。

Conclusion: 语义冲突影响LLM的程序理解和下游任务，关键信息集中在少数因果活跃的残差流状态，为理解LLM如何整合代码信息提供了机制性分析框架。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地用于处理可执行代码和非可执行语义线索（如注释或标识符）的软件工程任务。当语义线索暗示的程序行为与代码本身不同时，这两个来源可能发生冲突。目前尚不清楚这种语义冲突如何影响LLM的行为，以及哪个来源主导其输出。我们首次进行了受控的、机制性的LLM在语义冲突下行为的研究。为此，我们构建了45个Python片段三元组，通过改变语义线索或实现来隔离冲突，同时保留标记对齐的对用于因果干预。我们在四个开源LLM上评估了两个任务（输出预测和单元测试生成），使用行为性能度量和残差流激活修补来识别对对齐输入和冲突输入之间行为差异有因果贡献的标记层状态。我们的结果表明，语义冲突显著降低了两个任务中基于执行的正确性，并且所有测试的LLM经常遵循误导性的语义线索。残差流激活修补揭示了最终输出预测的一致模式：改变的线索/代码区域和一小部分中间标记携带了大部分可恢复的因果信号，然后在输出读取附近聚合。对于单元测试生成，这种模式扩展到提示之外，表明在生成预期值之前，冲突相关信息在生成位置是可恢复的。总体而言，我们的发现表明语义冲突影响程序理解和下游任务，相关信息集中在少数因果活跃的残差流状态中，并展示了一个框架，用于在受控语义变化下机制性地分析LLM如何整合代码相关信息。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used in software-engineering tasks processing executable code and non-executable semantic cues such as comments or identifiers. These two sources can conflict when semantic cues suggest different program behavior than the code itself. It remains unclear how such semantic conflicts affect LLM behavior and which source dominates their outputs.
  We present the first controlled, mechanistic study of LLM behavior under semantic conflicts. To this end, we construct 45 Python snippet triplets that isolate conflicts by varying either semantic cues or implementation while keeping token-aligned pairs for causal intervention. We evaluate four open-weight LLMs on two tasks (output prediction and unit-test generation) using behavioral performance measures and residual-stream activation patching to identify token-layer states that causally contribute to behavioral differences between aligned and conflicting inputs.
  Our results show that semantic conflicts significantly reduce execution-grounded correctness in both tasks and that all tested LLMs often follow misleading semantic cues. Residual-stream activation patching reveals a consistent pattern for final-output prediction: The changed cue/code region and a small set of intermediate tokens carry most of the recoverable causal signal before aggregation near the output readout. For unit-test generation, this pattern extends beyond the prompt, showing that conflict-related information is recoverable at generated sites before producing expected values. Overall, our findings show that semantic conflicts affect program comprehension and downstream tasks, with relevant information concentrated in a small number of causally active residual-stream states, and demonstrate a framework for mechanistically analyzing how LLMs integrate code-related information under controlled semantic variations.

</details>


### [29] [Bridging Stakeholder and Product Requirements: An Empirical Study of Requirement Engineering in the Automotive Industry](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05632v1)
*Zixu Wang,Shengcheng Yu,Zhenchang Xing,Tobias Wenzel,Chunyang Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 基于英飞凌工业数据集的大规模实证研究，分析了利益相关者需求和产品需求之间的结构差异与细化模式，发现细化复杂性主要受架构范围和缺失上下文信息驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然已有研究提出了改进需求质量的技术，但缺乏工业汽车实践中利益相关者级需求如何被评估、细化并转化为产品级需求的实证证据。

Method: 采用混合方法，对来自英飞凌的8,082个利益相关者需求和5,870个产品需求进行定量分析（需求结构、决策分布、映射模式）和定性分析（理由、引用规范、软件/硬件工件）。

Result: 揭示了不同抽象层次上的系统性差异，细化复杂性主要由架构范围和缺失上下文信息驱动，而非语言冗长；推导出利益相关者-产品映射模式的分类。

Conclusion: 为工业需求获取和细化实践提供了具体见解，并确定了改进获取验证、偏差管理和工具支持的上下文丰富化的可行机会，以支持更快且更可复用的汽车产品开发。

中文摘要：汽车行业向软件驱动系统的转变增加了系统复杂性，并提高了有效需求获取和细化对于正确性、合规性、开发速度和系统化复用的重要性。尽管先前的研究提出了改进需求质量的技术，但在工业汽车实践中，关于利益相关者级需求如何被评估、细化并转化为产品级需求的实证证据仍然有限。本文基于来自英飞凌的工业数据集进行了一项大规模实证研究，该数据集包含8,082个利益相关者需求和5,870个产品需求，并附有可追溯性链接、决策结果、偏差理由和领域引用。采用混合方法，我们将需求结构、决策分布和映射模式的定量分析与理由、引用规范以及软件和硬件相关工件的定性分析相结合。我们研究了利益相关者需求与产品需求之间的结构和上下文差异，影响接受、拒绝和有偏差批准的因素，以及利益相关者到产品细化的本质。结果揭示了不同抽象层次上的系统性差异，并表明细化复杂性主要由架构范围和缺失的上下文信息驱动，而不是语言冗长。我们进一步推导出利益相关者-产品映射模式的分类，并将这些模式与不同的细化工作相关联。这些发现为工业需求获取和细化实践提供了具体见解，并确定了改进获取验证、偏差管理和工具支持的上下文丰富化的可行机会，以支持更快且更可复用的汽车产品开发。

Original abstract: The automotive industry's shift toward software-driven systems has increased system complexity and raised the importance of effective requirement intake and refinement for correctness, compliance, development speed, and systematic reuse. Although prior research has proposed techniques for improving requirement quality, limited empirical evidence exists on how stakeholder-level requirements are evaluated, refined, and transformed into product-level requirements in industrial automotive practice. This paper presents a large-scale empirical study based on an industrial dataset from Infineon, comprising 8,082 stakeholder requirements and 5,870 product requirements enriched with traceability links, decision outcomes, deviation rationales, and domain references. Using a mixed-methods approach, we combine quantitative analyses of requirement structures, decision distributions, and mapping patterns with qualitative analyses of rationales, referenced specifications, and software- and hardware-related artifacts. We investigate structural and contextual differences between stakeholder and product requirements, factors influencing acceptance, rejection, and approval with deviation, and the nature of stakeholder-to-product refinement. The results reveal systematic differences across abstraction levels and show that refinement complexity is driven primarily by architectural scope and missing contextual information rather than linguistic verbosity. We further derive a taxonomy of stakeholder-product mapping patterns and relate these patterns to differing refinement effort. The findings provide concrete insight into industrial requirements intake and refinement practices and identify actionable opportunities for improving intake validation, deviation management, and tool-supported contextual enrichment to support faster and more reusable automotive product development.

### [30] [EvalLoop: A Methodology for Evaluation-Driven Iterative Improvement of Business AI Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05638v1)
*Kenneth Benavides,Josh Fleischer,Danti Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: EvalLoop是一种评估驱动的迭代改进方法，通过维度诊断和故障模式分类，显著提升LLM在商业场景中的表现，并减少人工审核负担。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估框架仅作为静态模型选择，忽略了诊断和指导改进的核心价值，导致迭代优化缺乏方向。

Method: 提出EvalLoop方法，包含三个机制：维度度量分组、故障模式分类、结构化迭代工作流。通过案例研究（销售情报简报生成）进行验证。

Result: 维度诊断发现69%幻觉源于提示错误，针对性修复将最佳模型从82.6%提升至94.6%；无诊断迭代产生零影响；维度画像支持部署选择，盲审减少94%负担。

Conclusion: EvalLoop通过评估驱动的迭代改进，有效诊断并提升LLM系统性能，且可复用，适用于商业部署场景。

中文摘要：在商业环境中部署大型语言模型的团队需要评估系统，但大多数团队将评估视为静态模型选择：运行基准测试、对模型进行排名、部署胜出者。这种框架忽略了评估对生产系统的主要价值——诊断系统为何表现不佳并指导修复什么。我们提出EvalLoop，一种评估驱动的迭代改进方法。EvalLoop围绕三种机制组织评估：（1）维度度量分组，将质量分解为业务相关维度，实现正交故障诊断；（2）故障模式分类，对弱维度内输出失败的原因进行分类，连接诊断与行动；（3）结构化迭代工作流，每次评估运行改变一个系统变量，并比较前后维度画像。我们通过销售情报简报生成案例研究（10个模型、3个提供商、18个指标、5个维度、3次迭代）验证EvalLoop。维度诊断发现69%的幻觉失败是由提示引起的解释错误——这在聚合评分中是不可见的。针对性的提示修复将最佳模型从82.6%提升到94.6%，改进集中在诊断维度（内容准确性+16.8个百分点，综合能力+26.4个百分点）。之前迭代中一次无定向的配置变更产生零影响，说明了无诊断迭代的成本。我们还证明了维度画像能够支持部署特定模型选择，并且对最终候选面板（4个模型、16个案例）进行一次性的盲人人工审核，在确认维度排名的同时解决多标准部署权衡——相比评估整个设计，审核负担减少了94%。EvalLoop被打包为可复用工件（手册、代理规范、模板仓库），供其他团队采用。

Original abstract: Teams deploying large language models in business contexts need evaluation systems, yet most treat evaluation as static model selection: run benchmarks, rank models, deploy the winner. This framing misses evaluation's primary value for production systems--diagnosing why a system underperforms and guiding what to fix. We present EvalLoop, a methodology for evaluation-driven iterative improvement. EvalLoop organizes evaluation around three mechanisms: (1) dimensional metric grouping that decomposes quality into business-relevant dimensions enabling orthogonal failure diagnosis; (2) failure mode classification that categorizes why outputs fail within weak dimensions, bridging diagnosis to action; and (3) a structured iteration workflow where each evaluation run varies one system variable and compares dimensional profiles before and after. We validate EvalLoop through a case study on sales intelligence briefing generation (10 models, 3 providers, 18 metrics, 5 dimensions, 3 iterations). Dimensional diagnosis identified that 69% of hallucination failures were prompt-induced interpretation errors--invisible in aggregate scoring. A targeted prompt fix improved the best model from 82.6% to 94.6% overall, with improvement concentrated in diagnosed dimensions (Content Accuracy +16.8pp, Synthesis Power +26.4pp). An undirected configuration change in a prior iteration produced zero impact, illustrating the cost of iterating without diagnosis. We additionally demonstrate that dimensional profiling enables deployment-specific model selection, and that a one-time blind human gate on a finalist panel (4 models, 16 cases) confirms dimensional rankings while resolving multi-criteria deployment trade-offs--a 94% reduction in review burden compared to evaluating the full design. EvalLoop is packaged as reusable artifacts (playbook, agent specification, template repository) for adoption by other teams.
