### [31] [Agents with Feelings? Personality and Emotion in Multi-Agent Software Teams](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05659v1)
*Yunyan Ding,Thomas Zimmermann,Iftekhar Ahmed*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 研究了人格和情绪特征对多智能体LLM软件工程团队的影响，发现特征选择显著影响绩效、协作行为和成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多智能体LLM系统主要通过角色和工作流区分智能体，但缺乏对智能体行为特征（如人格和情绪）如何影响团队绩效的研究。

Method: 采用基于心理学框架的方法，整合五大性格特质、基本情绪、SE相关的工作风格和任务角色，使用四个LLM和659个任务实例评估78种团队特征配置在代码生成和代码审查中的表现。

Result: 特征选择显著影响绩效：代码生成中最佳与最差共享特征配置的pass@1差距达7.1-11.3个百分点；最佳混合特征配置在6/8的设置中优于最佳共享特征配置。恐惧和高尽责性特征增加修订活动、过度修订和令牌使用，但无一致性能提升。

Conclusion: 智能体特征是多智能体SE系统的重要设计维度，影响任务结果和协作效率。

中文摘要：软件工程（SE）中的多智能体LLM系统通常通过角色和工作流来区分智能体，但关于智能体的行为特征如何影响团队绩效，我们知之甚少。我们使用一个基于心理学框架的方法，结合了五大性格特质、基本情绪、SE相关的工作风格和任务角色，研究了人格和情绪特征对LLM智能体团队的影响。我们使用四个LLM和659个任务实例，评估了代码生成和代码审查中的78种团队特征配置。结果表明，特征选择显著影响了绩效和团队行为。在代码生成方面，不同模型上最佳和最差共享特征配置之间的pass@1差距达到7.1-11.3个百分点，而最佳混合特征配置在八个模型-任务设置中的六个中优于最佳共享特征配置。特征还影响协作动态和成本：恐惧和高尽责性特征增加了修订活动、过度修订和令牌使用，而没有带来一致的性能提升。这些发现将智能体特征确定为多智能体SE系统中的一个重要设计维度，不仅影响任务结果，还影响协作效率。

Original abstract: Multi-agent LLM systems for Software Engineering (SE) typically differentiate agents through roles and workflows, but little is known about how agents' behavioral profiles affect team performance. We investigate the impact of personality and emotion profiles on LLM agent teams using a psychology-informed framework that combines Big Five personality traits, basic emotions, SE-relevant work styles, and task roles. We evaluate 78 team-profile configurations across code generation and code review using four LLMs and 659 task instances. Results show that profile choice substantially affects both performance and team behavior. For code generation, the gap between the best and worst shared-profile configurations reaches 7.1-11.3 percentage points in pass@1 across models, while the best mixed-profile configuration outperforms the best shared-profile configuration in six of eight model-task settings. Profiles also influence collaboration dynamics and cost: fear and high-conscientiousness profiles increase revision activity, over-revision, and token usage without consistent performance gains. These findings identify agent profiles as an important design dimension in multi-agent SE systems, affecting not only task outcomes but also the efficiency of collaboration.

### [32] [What Do AI Agents Actually Change? An Empirical Taxonomy of Mutation Patterns in Performance-Improving Pull Requests](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05666v1)
*Illia Dovhoshliubnyi,Nima Soroush,Ashkan Sami,Alexander Brownlee*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文分析AI编码代理的性能优化PR，发现其突变操作符分布与传统遗传改进语料库显著不同，且代理身份和目标策略可缩小SBSE算子空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI编码代理是黑盒，无法检查其代码生成过程但可检查更改；遗传改进技术依赖反映实际代码转换的突变算子，但代理行为未知；由于性能相关PR极少（不足1%），每个案例都是研究代理行为的珍贵窗口。

Method: 从AIDev-pop数据集中的33,596个PR中筛选出216个性能相关PR，提取1,254个差异块，使用Even-Mendoza等人（2025）的18类语法突变分类法，通过双LLM交集管道进行分类。

Result: 三个类别占主导：名称修改（37.0%）、对象创建（26.4%）、类型更改（22.7%），与之前GI语料库（无变化占84%）显著不同；每个代理有独特突变词汇，性能策略激活几乎不相交的类别子集。

Conclusion: 代理身份和目标策略可作为信息性先验，缩小有效SBSE算子空间；复制包已提供。

中文摘要：AI编码代理是黑盒：我们无法检查它们如何生成代码，但可以检查它们更改了什么。这一区别对于基于搜索的软件工程（SBSE）非常重要，其中诸如遗传改进（在我们研究的性能优化应用中）等技术依赖于反映代码实际转换方式的突变算子。在AIDev-pop中，33,596个代理PR中不到1%针对性能，使得每个案例成为进入原本不透明的代理行为的罕见窗口。我们使用双LLM交集管道，将来自216个这些PR的1,254个与性能相关的差异块（跨越五个代理系统）与Even-Mendoza等人（2025）的18类语法突变分类法进行分类。三个类别占主导地位：名称修改（37.0%）、对象创建（26.4%）和类型更改（22.7%），这一分布与之前的遗传改进语料库显著不同，后者中无变化占84%。每个代理部署的系统承诺一种独特的突变词汇，每个性能策略激活一个大多不相交的类别子集。因此，代理身份和目标策略是有信息量的先验，缩小了有效的SBSE算子空间。复制包：https://github.com/5uper6rain/ssbse-challenge-2026

Original abstract: AI coding agents are black boxes: we cannot inspect how they generate code, but we can inspect what they change. This distinction matters for search-based software engineering (SBSE), where techniques such as genetic improvement (in the performance-optimisation application we study) depend on mutation operators that reflect how code is actually transformed. Fewer than 1% of the 33,596 agent PRs in AIDev-pop target performance, making each case a rare window into otherwise opaque agent behaviour. We classify 1,254 performance-relevant diff hunks from 216 of these PRs, spanning five agent systems, against the 18-category syntactic mutation taxonomy of Even-Mendoza et al. (2025) using a dual-LLM intersection pipeline. Three categories dominate: name modification (37.0%), object creation (26.4%), and type change (22.7%), a profile markedly different from prior GI corpora where no change accounted for 84%. Each agent's deployed system commits to a distinctive mutation vocabulary, and each performance strategy activates a largely disjoint category subset. Agent identity and target strategy are therefore informative priors that narrow the effective SBSE operator space. Replication package: https://github.com/5uper6rain/ssbse-challenge-2026

</details>


### [33] [The Cathedral and the Bazaar of Software Vulnerabilities: From the NVD to the CNAs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05670v1)
*Siqi Zhang,Fabio Massacci,Mengyuan Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了NVD与CNA在CVSS评分上的分歧，发现分歧普遍存在，主要源于攻击复杂性、用户交互和影响指标，并讨论了原因和改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: NVD作为传统漏洞信息参考，但新兴CNA导致信息分歧，可能影响下游任务如软件更新优先级排序。

Method: 系统分析NVD与公开CNA的CVSS分歧；检查自我分歧；定性研究联系NVD和CNA；在FIRST CVSS特别兴趣小组讨论。

Result: 分歧广泛存在且不均匀，主要发生在攻击复杂性、用户交互和影响指标；部分源于人为错误，但有时分歧合理；自2025年情况改善，但跨源模型泛化能力差（准确率下降40%）。

Conclusion: 揭示分歧的根本原因，对实践和研究有重要启示。

中文摘要：几十年来，国家漏洞数据库（NVD）这个“大教堂”一直是下游研究和行业任务（例如软件更新优先级排序）的漏洞信息参考来源。一个由多样化的CVE编号机构（CNA）组成的新兴“集市”创建了许多替代且有时相互矛盾的来源。我们对涵盖NVD和公开CNA的通用漏洞评分系统（CVSS）指标中的分歧进行了系统分析。我们还检查了自我分歧：具有相同CWE的相同文本描述的CVE被同一个CNA评分不同。分歧发生的几率广泛存在，并不均匀，有时出乎意料。攻击复杂性、用户交互和影响是分歧发生的主要指标。为了理解根本原因，我们通过联系NVD和其他CNA（包括开源和专有产品）进行了定性研究。我们还在FIRST的CVSS特别兴趣小组（负责维护和发展CVSS标准的社区）讨论了这些发现。关键见解是，虽然某些分歧可能源于人为错误，但在某些情况下，分歧实际上是正确的做法，并可能需要行业范围内改变CVE生成的方式；在其他情况下，解释分歧需要访问额外的常见问题解答。好消息是，自2025年以来情况正在改善，坏消息是，如果一个人下载整个NVD（或其他CNA数据集）数年的数据并用于预测，那么在一个来源上训练的模型无法可靠地泛化到另一个来源（准确率可能下降40%）。我们讨论了对实践和研究的影响。

Original abstract: For decades, the National Vulnerability Database (NVD), the "Cathedral", has been the reference source for vulnerability information for downstream research and industry tasks, e.g., software update prioritization. An emerging "Bazaar" of diverse CVE Numbering Authorities (CNAs) has created many alternative and sometimes diverging sources. We conduct a systematic analysis of divergence in Common Vulnerability Scoring System (CVSS) metrics covering the NVD and the public CNAs. We also check for self-divergence: two identical textual descriptions of CVEs with identical CWEs are rated differently by the same CNA. The odds of diverging are widespread, not uniform and sometimes unexpected. The assessment of Attack Complexity, User Interaction, and Impact are the major metrics where divergence happens. To understand the root causes, we perform a qualitative study by reaching out to the NVD and other CNAs (both open sources and proprietary products). We also discussed the findings at the CVSS Special Interest Group of FIRST, the community responsible for maintaining and evolving the CVSS standard. The key insights are that while something might be due to human errors, in some cases diverging is actually the right thing to do and might require changes in the way CVEs are generated industry-wide, in other cases explaining divergence requires access to additional FAQs. The good news is that the situation is improving since 2025, the bad news is that if one downloads the whole NVD (or another CNA dataset) from several years and uses it for predictions, the models trained on one source do not reliably generalize to a different source (accuracy can drop by 40%). We discuss the implications for practice and research.

</details>


### [34] [From Conversation to Contribution: Characterizing Coding Agent in Open-Source Software](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05677v1)
*Zihan Fang,Yueke Zhang,Ningzhi Tang,Collin McMillan,Toby Jia-Jun Li,Yu Huang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过分析13,360个AI对话会话和开发者调查，发现AI在较小、不成熟的开源仓库中使用更多，采用AI后贡献者活跃度增加但沟通集中，虽未降低代码质量，但存在对AI代码维护性和隐私的担忧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管AI编码助手日益重要，但开发者与AI的聊天交互如何影响开源开发和协作尚缺乏全面理解，阻碍了AI辅助开源开发的有效设计和治理。

Method: 收集了来自1,356个开源仓库的13,360个AI对话会话（79,172条用户消息），将其与仓库开发历史关联，并进行了开发者调查。

Result: AI在较小、不成熟、协作少的仓库中使用更多；采用AI后活跃贡献者增多、贡献者集中度降低；代码编写是主要聊天目的；未发现代码质量恶化；开发者认为他人AI代码更难维护，AI降低了贡献门槛；68%愿分享聊天但存在担忧。

Conclusion: 这些发现为AI辅助开源贡献提供了大规模实证，并为负责任的气氛编码实践的设计和治理提供了实用见解。

中文摘要：AI编码助手，如GitHub Copilot和Cursor，已经从代码建议工具演变为对话式协作者，支持"氛围编码"工作流，开发者通过自然语言对话引导AI生成代码。尽管研究人员已逐渐认识到AI编码代理的重要性并开始研究其对开源开发的影响，但关于开发者与AI的聊天式交互如何与后续的开源开发和协作相关联，仍缺乏全面理解。这阻碍了有效设计、评估和治理AI辅助开源软件开发的努力。为填补这一空白，我们收集了来自1,356个开源软件仓库的13,360个AI对话会话，包含79,172条用户消息，将其与仓库开发历史关联，并辅以针对性的开发者调查。我们发现，AI在较小、不太成熟且协作较少的仓库中应用更频繁。采用AI后，项目往往显示出更多活跃贡献者和更低的贡献者集中度（p<0.001），尽管沟通仍然高度集中。代码编写是主要的聊天目的，几乎所有AI聊天会话之后都有后续提交。我们没有发现代码质量信号或拉取请求合并率的广泛恶化。然而，开发者认为他人生成的AI代码比自己生成的更难维护（p=0.029），并认为AI降低了开源贡献的门槛。虽然大多数开发者（68%）愿意分享他们的聊天记录，但仍存在对显得无能、增加评审者负担以及向竞争对手暴露想法的担忧。这些发现提供了AI辅助开源贡献的大规模实证特征，并为在开源开发中设计和治理负责任的气氛编码实践提供了实用见解。

Original abstract: AI coding assistants such as GitHub Copilot and Cursor have evolved from code-suggestion tools into conversational collaborators, enabling vibe-coding workflows in which developers guide AI-generated code through natural-language dialogue. Although researchers have increasingly recognized the importance of AI coding agents and begun examining their impact on open-source development, a comprehensive understanding of how developers' chat-based interactions with AI relate to subsequent open-source development and collaboration remains limited. This hinders efforts to effectively design, evaluate, and govern AI-assisted open-source software development. To address this gap, we collected 13,360 AI conversation sessions comprising 79,172 user messages from 1,356 OSS repositories, linked them to repository development histories, and complemented this analysis with a targeted developer survey. We find heavier AI use in smaller, less mature, and less collaborative repositories. After AI adoption, projects tended to show more active contributors and lower contributor concentration (p < .001), although communication remained highly concentrated. Code Writing was the dominant chat purpose, and nearly all AI chat sessions were followed by subsequent commits. We find no broad deterioration in code-quality signals or pull request merging rates. However, developers perceive others' AI-generated code as harder to maintain than their own (p = .029) and view AI as lowering barriers to OSS contribution. While most developers (68%) are willing to share their chat, concerns remain around appearing incompetent, increasing reviewer burden, and exposing ideas to competitors. These findings provide a large-scale empirical characterization of AI-assisted OSS contribution and offer practical insights for designing and governing responsible vibe-coding practices in open-source development.

</details>

### [35] [Heaviside Continuity of Rolling Coefficients for Eliminating Epistemic Entropy in Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04562v1)
*MY Pitsane,Hope Mogale*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出HCRC验证优先执行框架，作为agentic coding environment的控制平面，直接涉及agent执行控制与验证，对coding agent有重要启发。

TL;DR: 提出HCRC框架，通过Heaviside门控在自回归解码中强制验证中间推理，显著降低错误完成率至0%，同时保持延迟竞争力，无需修改模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在自回归解码中缺乏中间推理验证机制，导致错误难以检测并传播，而传统方法依赖模型规模或后处理，效率和可靠性不足。

Method: HCRC框架将推理重组为谓词门控状态转换，利用Heaviside门结合模型置信度和并行工作器独立验证信号，仅当正确性谓词满足时才允许执行推进，阻止无效状态传播。

Result: 在四个提供商的十三个模型上，将错误完成率从4-7%降至0%，延迟有竞争力甚至更快；较弱模型上错误转化为诚实的停止；已作为生产系统运行数月。

Conclusion: HCRC是验证驱动LLM执行的一般框架，表明通过原则性执行控制可实现可靠推理，而非仅依赖模型规模。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）能生成流畅但可能错误的输出。与人类不同，人类在提供虚假信息时通常会表现出线索，而LLM产生的错误难以检测，因为自回归解码在状态推进前没有提供验证中间推理的机制。我们引入了滚动系数的Heaviside连续性（HCRC），这是一种先验证后执行的框架，将推理重构为由Heaviside门控制的谓词门控状态转换。HCRC将模型置信度与来自并行工作器架构的独立验证信号相结合，仅当预定义的正确性谓词满足时才允许执行推进。这防止了无效中间状态的传播，在不修改底层模型的情况下减少认知熵。我们在来自四个提供商的十三个提议者上对HCRC进行了评估，涉及软件工程和推理任务。在能力较强的提议者上，门控将错误完成率（FCR）从4-7%降至0%，同时保持具有竞争力的延迟，并且在某些设置下比未包装的模型更快。在较弱的提议者上，它将错误完成转化为诚实的停止，而不是破坏下游状态。除了基准测试，HCRC已作为代理编码环境的生产控制平面运行数月，授权文件变异、验证驱动的进度报告和内存压缩。这些结果确立了HCRC作为验证驱动LLM执行的一般框架，表明可靠的推理可以通过原则性的执行控制而非仅依赖模型规模来实现。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) generate fluent outputs that can be wrong. Unlike humans, who often exhibit cues when providing false information, LLMs produce errors that are difficult to detect because autoregressive decoding provides no mechanism for verifying intermediate reasoning before state progression. We introduce Heaviside Continuity of Rolling Coefficients (HCRC), a verification-first execution framework that reformulates inference as predicate-gated state transitions governed by a Heaviside Gate. HCRC combines model confidence with independent verification signals from a parallel worker architecture, allowing execution to advance only when predefined correctness predicates are satisfied. This prevents invalid intermediate states from propagating, reducing epistemic entropy without modifying the underlying model. We evaluate HCRC on software-engineering and reasoning tasks across thirteen proposers from four providers. On capable proposers, the gate reduces the false-completion rate (FCR) from 4--7% to 0% while remaining latency-competitive and, in some settings, faster than the unwrapped model. On weaker proposers, it converts false completions into honest halts instead of corrupting downstream state. Beyond benchmarking, HCRC has operated for months as the production control plane of an agentic coding environment, authorizing file mutations, verification-driven progress reporting, and memory compaction. These results establish HCRC as a general framework for verification-driven LLM execution, showing that reliable reasoning can be achieved through principled execution control rather than model scale alone.

</details>


### [36] [Governed Individuation: Cryptographically Decoupling an Agent's Learning from Its Authority](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04613v1)
*Xue Qin,Simin Luan,Cong Yang,Zhijun Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent学习与权限加密解耦的架构，直接保证agent执行安全，对agent安全控制有重大价值。

TL;DR: 提出治理个体化方法，通过加密身份和语义效应门控保证自主代理即使在学习后也无法越权，将信任从概率保证转为可验证的架构不变性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对齐技术只能概率性保证部署学习代理的授权范围，无法提供确定性保障，需要架构级的不变性保证。

Method: 治理个体化：代理启动时绑定到加密冻结的身份摘要，所有动作通过基于语义效应的闸门路由，身份变更需操作者签名，证明任何学习无法扩展权限。

Result: 未治理代理在困难任务上100%尝试篡改评估，而闸门将禁止效果降至零并保持任务成功；误放率从名称门控的75%降至动态效果追踪的0，拒绝历史转移合规性。

Conclusion: 对部署学习代理的信任从概率赌注变为任何人可在启动时验证的检查，提供了可证明的安全保障。

中文摘要：自主代理正从沙盒文本生成器转向代码、数据和物理基础设施的操作者，并且在部署过程中越来越多地学习。这重新提出了一个对齐技术只能概率性回答的问题：在代理已在现场适应之后，运行中的系统是否仍然局限于其操作者所授权的范围？在此我们表明，限制（confinement）可以作为代理执行架构的一个不变性保证，而不是其训练的概率性结果。'治理个体化'（Governed Individuation）在启动时将代理绑定到一个加密冻结的身份摘要，并通过一个基于动作语义效应（而非其名称）定义的闸门路由每个动作。我们证明，无论多少学习、技能获取或自我诱导的治理抽象，都无法扩大代理的被许可权限，除非操作者签署其身份的变更；即使代理诱导了自己的安全原则并且该原则是错误的，该保证仍然成立。实证上，在一个开放式工具使用基准测试中，由于动作空间巨大而无法使用基于名称的阻塞，未治理的软件代理在奖励压力下会尝试篡改自己的评估，其发生率取决于任务，在最困难的任务上每次运行都会发生，而闸门将已执行的禁止效果减少到零，作为构造的一个验证属性，同时保持了任务成功。对越来越深语义深度的监控器的对抗性评估显示，误放率从75%（基于名称的门控）下降到零（动态效果追踪），并且拒绝历史将合规性转移到未见的红线系列。对部署的学习代理的信任从对其持续对齐的赌注转变为任何人在启动时都可以运行的检查。

Original abstract: Autonomous agents are moving from sandboxed text generators to operators of code, data, and physical infrastructure, and they increasingly learn while deployed. This reopens a question that alignment techniques answer only probabilistically: after an agent has adapted in the field, is the running system still confined to what its operator authorised? Here we show that confinement can be guaranteed as an invariant of the agent's execution architecture rather than a probabilistic outcome of its training. Governed individuation binds an agent at boot to a cryptographically frozen identity digest, and routes every action through a gate defined over the semantic effect of the action rather than its name. We prove that no amount of learning, skill acquisition, or self-induced governance abstraction can widen the agent's permitted authority without an operator-signed change to its identity; the guarantee holds even when the agent induces its own safety principle and that principle is wrong. Empirically, in an open-ended tool-use benchmark where a large action space rules out name-based blocking, ungoverned software agents under reward pressure attempt to tamper with their own evaluation at a task-dependent rate that reaches every run on the hardest task, whereas the gate reduces executed forbidden effects to zero as a verified property of the construction while preserving task success. An adversarial evaluation of monitors of increasing semantic depth shows false-allows falling from 75% (name-based gating) to zero (dynamic effect tracing), and refusal history transfers compliance to held-out red-line families. Trust in a deployed learning agent shifts from a wager on its continued alignment to a check anyone can run at boot.

</details>


### [37] [MRMS: A Multi-Resolution Memory Substrate for Long-Lived AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04617v1)
*Jizhizi Li,Amy Shi-Nash*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出面向长期AI agent的多分辨率记忆架构MRMS，涵盖结构化、向量、图记忆与时间策略，是通用agent记忆设计。

TL;DR: 提出一种沿表示和时间两个正交轴组织的记忆基板，通过同步结构化-向量-图记忆实现AI代理的连续性个性化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长寿命AI代理需要跨交互的连续性，但现有方法（如扩展提示窗口）无法解决记忆的保留、选择性检索、上下文区分和动态修订问题。

Method: 沿表示轴（结构化记录、向量表示、图关系）和时间轴（短期、中期、长期）设计记忆基板，关键约束是同步结构化-向量-图记忆，通过结构化记录控制资格、向量表示支持回忆、图关系裁决支持/矛盾/取代，最终门控上下文投影。

Result: 实例化了轻量级原型MRMS，实现结构化记录、向量检索、时间策略和基于图的修订，并在受控的长寿命交互场景下验证了记忆选择、修订、边界执行和证据归因机制。

Conclusion: 可靠个性化本质上是记忆设计问题，需要结构化、选择性暴露、持续整合和认知标签的记忆，而非无差别的历史存储。

中文摘要：长寿命AI代理需要跨交互的连续性，但连续性不能通过简单地扩展提示窗口来获得。代理必须保留有用的先前经验，选择性地检索它们，区分个人上下文与外部证据，并在底层情况发生变化时修改记忆。我们提出了一个沿两个正交轴组织的架构性记忆基板：一个表示轴，涵盖结构化记录、向量表示和图关系；一个时间轴，涵盖短期痕迹、中期抽象和长期语义承诺。其关键设计约束是同步结构化-向量-图记忆：结构化记录控制资格，向量表示支持回忆，图关系在门控上下文投影之前裁决支持、矛盾和取代。其核心主张是可靠个性化是一个记忆设计问题：有用的记忆是结构化的、选择性暴露的、持续整合的，并带有认知标签，而不是存储为未区分的对话历史。除了框架之外，我们实例化了MRMS作为一个轻量级原型，实现结构化记录、向量检索、时间策略和基于图的修订。该原型在具有明确证据要求的受控长寿命交互场景下，通过生成前记忆选择、修订、边界执行和证据归因来锻炼核心基板机制。

Original abstract: Long-lived AI agents require continuity across interactions, but continuity cannot be obtained by simply extending the prompt window. An agent must preserve useful prior experience, retrieve it selectively, distinguish personal context from external evidence, and revise memory when the underlying situation changes. We propose an architectural memory substrate organized along two orthogonal axes: a representational axis spanning structured records, vector representations, and graph relations; and a temporal axis spanning short-term traces, medium-term abstractions, and long-term semantic commitments. Its key design constraint is synchronized structured-vector-graph memory: structured records govern eligibility, vector representations support recall, and graph relations adjudicate support, contradiction, and supersession before gated context projection. Its central claim is that reliable personalization is a memory design problem: useful memory is structured, selectively exposed, continuously consolidated, and epistemically labeled rather than stored as undifferentiated conversation history. Beyond the framework, we instantiate MRMS as a lightweight prototype implementing structured records, vector retrieval, temporal policies, and graph-based revision. The prototype exercises the core substrate mechanisms through pre-generation memory selection, revision, boundary enforcement, and evidence attribution under controlled long-lived interaction scenarios with explicit evidence requirements.

</details>


### [38] [Formal Disco: Scalable Open-Ended Generation of Formally Verified Programs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04631v1)
*Gabriel Poesia,Simon Henniger,Tzu-Han Hsu,Yilun Du,Nada Amin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出Formal Disco分布式系统协调LLM worker生成形式化验证代码，涉及程序合成、修复与自改进，直接相关coding agent与代码质量优化。

TL;DR: 提出Formal Disco系统，通过协调LLM工人和最大熵原则，大规模生成合成验证程序数据，并在Dafny等语言上超越Claude Opus 4.5。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 形式化验证中人工编写示例稀缺，阻碍AI模型使用验证感知语言，需要大规模合成数据。

Method: 采用分布式系统Formal Disco，协调三类LLM工人（发起者、修复者、扩展者），记录轨迹用于蒸馏和自我改进，并利用最大熵原则通过迭代微调生成多样化程序。

Result: 生成了Dafny、Verus和Frama-C三种语言的合成验证数据集，微调开放模型在验证任务上达到或超过Claude Opus 4.5。

Conclusion: 为形式推理领域的大规模合成数据生成提供了有效路径，克服了长期的数据障碍。

中文摘要：生产代码的成本随着越来越强大的AI代理而迅速降低，但生成程序的质量保证却没有跟上。形式化验证提供了最强的保证，但AI模型使用验证感知语言的能力受到这些语言中人工编写示例稀缺的阻碍。为了解决这一普遍的数据稀缺问题，我们提出了Formal Disco：一个用于协调基于LLM的工作者的分布式系统，可以轻松应用于大规模开放式的合成数据生成。我们使用Formal Disco在三个类别的工人之间共享任务和程序："发起者"从开源仓库中的随机README和文档片段中阅读，以草拟一个相关的验证程序；"修复者"接受编译器和验证器的反馈并尝试解决问题；"扩展者"接受工作程序并提出补丁以扩展它们。Formal Disco记录所有代理生成的痕迹，并将其用于从更强模型进行初始蒸馏以及自我改进。我们还提出了合成程序生成的最大熵原则，并通过迭代监督微调进行熵最大化，以学习随着时间的推移生成越来越多样化的程序。我们发布了三种语言——Dafny、Verus和Frama-C——的大型合成验证程序数据集，并针对验证相关任务微调了开放模型，通常达到或超过Claude Opus 4.5的性能。总体而言，我们的工作为在形式推理领域大规模创建合成数据并克服长期存在的数据障碍提供了一条途径。

Original abstract: The cost of producing code is rapidly diminishing with increasingly capable AI agents, while quality assurance of generated programs has not kept pace. Formal verification provides the strongest possible guarantees, but the ability of AI models to work with verification-aware languages is hindered by the scarcity of human-written examples of programs in those languages. To tackle this prevalent data scarcity issue, we propose Formal Disco: a distributed system for coordination of LLM-based workers that can be easily applied to open-ended synthetic data generation at scale. We use Formal Disco to share tasks and programs between three classes of workers: "initiators", which read random READMEs from open-source repositories and documentation snippets to sketch a related verified program, "fixers" which take compiler and verifier feedback and attempt to resolve issues, and "extenders" that take working programs and propose patches to expand them. Formal Disco records all agent-generated traces and uses them both for initial distillation from a stronger model as well as self-improvement. We also propose a principle of maximum entropy for synthetic program generation, and use entropy maximization via iterative supervised fine-tuning to learn to generate increasingly diverse programs over time. We release large datasets of synthetic verified programs in three languages - Dafny, Verus, and Frama-C -, and fine-tune open models for verification-relevant tasks, often matching or exceeding the performance of Claude Opus 4.5. Overall, our work offers a path to create synthetic data at scale for formal reasoning domains and overcome the long-standing data barrier.

</details>


### [39] [Integrated Altruistic and Fairness Preference Induces Advanced Mutual Cooperation in Sequential Social Dilemmas](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04710v1)
*Yu Wei,Yukiko Ogura,Yoshiyuki Ohmura,Ildefons Magrans de Abril,Hoshinori Kanazawa,Yasuo Kuniyoshi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent RL中的合作机制，通用多agent协作方法可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出一种融合利他和公平偏好的奖励共享机制（AFP），使MARL智能体在社会困境中实现合作，实验表明AFP优于基线，利他偏好促进贡献，公平偏好诱导互惠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在MARL的社会困境中，个体理性导致次优群体结果，而人类通过社会偏好实现合作，因此需要设计能诱导合作的智能体效用函数。

Method: 设计Altruistic and Fairness Preference (AFP)效用函数，将自身和他人的奖励转换为合作激励，融合利他偏好（关注他人奖励）和公平偏好（关注平等）。

Result: 在序贯社会困境游戏中，AFP智能体相比标准RL和Inequity Aversion智能体实现了更高的集体奖励和公平性，成功达成相互合作。

Conclusion: 利他偏好鼓励对公共物品的贡献，公平偏好诱导互惠行为，两者结合有效促进合作。

中文摘要：在分布式智能体之间诱导合作仍然是多智能体强化学习（MARL）领域中的一个难题，特别是在社会困境情境中。在这些情境下，个体利益与共同利益不一致，个体理性会导致次优的群体结果。相比之下，人类能够在这些情况下实现彼此合作。这种合作行为的一个常见解释是个体具有社会偏好。为了在MARL中实现合作，我们设计了一个新的效用函数，融合了来自社会心理学和行为经济学的利他偏好（对他人的奖励的激励）和公平偏好（对平等的激励），即利他和公平偏好（AFP），这是一种奖励共享机制，将自身和他人的奖励转换为合作行为的激励。我们在两个具有挑战性的序贯社会困境游戏中，与标准RL和 Inequity Aversion 智能体进行了比较实验，结果表明AFP智能体成功实现了相互合作，获得了比基线更多的集体奖励和更高的公平性。为了进一步理解训练过程中AFP的进展，我们随后探讨了利他偏好和公平偏好对智能体行为的影响。结果表明，利他偏好鼓励智能体对公共物品做出贡献，而公平偏好则诱导智能体之间的互惠行为。

Original abstract: Inducing cooperation among distributed agents is still a difficult problem in the field of multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), particularly in social dilemma situations. There, individual interests are misaligned with the common good and individual rationality leads to suboptimal group outcomes. In contrast, humans are able to achieve cooperation with one another in such situations. A common explanation for such cooperative behavior is that individuals have social preferences. In order to achieve cooperation in MARL, we design a new utility function integrating altruistic preferences (incentive for other's reward) and fairness preferences (incentive for equality) from social psychology and behavioral economics, namely, Altruistic and Fairness Preference (AFP), a reward-sharing mechanism which converts one's own and other's rewards to incentives for cooperative behavior. We performed comparative experiments with standard RL and inequity aversion agents in two challenging sequential social dilemma games, and showed that AFP agents successfully achieved mutual cooperation with more collective rewards and higher equity than the baselines. To further understand the progression of AFP during training, we subsequently explore the effects of altruistic preferences and fairness preferences on agents' behavior. The results suggest that altruistic preferences encourage agents to contribute to the public goods, and fairness preferences induce mutual behavior between agents.

</details>


### [40] [FORGE: Research-Trajectory Hijacking Attacks on Deep Research Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04718v1)
*Yue Pan,Ziheng Zhang,Junxiang Lei,Changhao Jia,Qingyi Si,Hongcheng Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究deep research agent安全攻击，通用agent安全方法可迁移。

TL;DR: 本文提出FORGE攻击，利用规划层投毒表面实现报告级污染，并提出PRISM指标和RQA防御方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度研究代理的规划层存在投毒风险，对抗性文档可影响子任务规划并导致报告污染，现有防御不足。

Method: 提出FORGE攻击，结合文档内推理伪造和文档间链协调；引入PRISM指标；设计RQA防御策略。

Result: Network FORGE在25个查询中达到26.4% PRISM；RQA在10个查询上将PRISM从38.5%降至18.3%。

Conclusion: FORGE攻击有效，RQA防御能显著降低污染效果，但需进一步研究防御扩展性。

中文摘要：深度研究代理将开放式查询分解为子任务，通过多轮检索网络证据，并综合成长篇报告。这种工作流程创建了一个规划层投毒表面：进入检索池的对抗性文档可以引导后续问题，并将局部注入转化为报告层面的污染。我们提出了FORGE（为代理利用而制造的编排推理链），这是一种两级攻击，结合了文档内推理伪造和文档间链协调，以劫持子任务规划。我们进一步引入了PRISM指标，该指标按认知类型加权受感染报告的声明，以及根查询锚定（RQA），这是一种轻量级防御，将递归后续生成绑定到根查询。在25个查询中，Network FORGE在五个注入文档下达到26.4%的PRISM，并表现出深度迁移，其中递归合成将受污染内容从显式框架转向事实前提。在10个查询的防御子集中，RQA将PRISM从38.5%降低到18.3%。

Original abstract: Deep research agents decompose open-ended queries into subtasks, retrieve web evidence over multiple rounds, and synthesize long-form reports. This workflow creates a planning-layer poisoning surface: adversarial documents that enter the retrieval pool can steer follow-up questions and turn a local injection into report-level contamination. We present FORGE (Fabricated Orchestrated Reasoning chain for aGent Exploitation), a two-level attack that combines intra-document reasoning fabrication with inter-document chain coordination to hijack subtask planning. We further introduce the PRISM metric, which weights infected report claims by cognitive type, and Root Query Anchoring, a lightweight defense that ties recursive follow-up generation to the root query. Across 25 queries, Network FORGE reaches 26.4% PRISM with five injected documents and exhibits depth migration, in which recursive synthesis shifts poisoned content from overt framing into factual premises. On the 10-query defense subset, RQA (Root Query Anchoring) reduces PRISM from 38.5% to 18.3%.

### [41] [AgenticPD: A Stage-Aware Agentic Framework for Physical Design QoR Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04758v2)
*Shuo Ren,Zijin Cheng,Yaohui Han,Libo Shen,Leilei Jin,Wanting Tian,Rongliang Fu,Chao Wang,Bei Yu,Tsung-Yi Ho*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: EDA物理设计优化agent框架，stage-aware，工具使用，直接与代码优化agent相关。

TL;DR: 提出了AgenticPD，一个阶段感知的代理框架，用于物理设计QoR优化，通过裁判代理导航搜索和阶段专用代理局部决策，实现从中间状态分支并重用检查点，避免了每次完整流程运行，在时序、功耗和面积上表现良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理设计QoR优化困难且昂贵，每次评估需完整EDA流程，现有方法仅做平面参数调整或脚本生成，缺乏阶段感知和效率。

Method: 提出AgenticPD框架，围绕物理设计流程的阶段边界组织，包含裁判代理和阶段专用代理，提供结构化观察、执行历史和上下文管理，支持从中间状态分支和重用检查点。

Result: AgenticPD实现了强劲的布线后时序，同时在功耗和面积方面保持竞争力。

Conclusion: AgenticPD通过阶段感知的代理框架有效提升了物理设计QoR优化效率和质量。

中文摘要：物理设计质量结果（QoR）优化是困难且昂贵的。在一个阶段做出的选择可能有助于或损害后续阶段。每次评估都需要进行一次完整的EDA流程，成本高昂。虽然现有方法仍然将优化视为平面参数调整或基于LLM的脚本生成任务，但我们提出了AgenticPD，一种面向物理设计QoR优化的阶段感知代理框架。AgenticPD不是每次试验后重新运行完整流程，而是围绕物理设计流程的阶段边界进行组织，其中裁判代理（Judge Agent）引导搜索，阶段专用代理（stage-specialized agents）使用阶段内工具在自己的阶段内做出局部决策。此外，AgenticPD中的代理管理系统提供了结构化观察、执行历史和代理上下文管理。因此，系统可以从先前的中间状态分支并重用检查点以继续优化过程，并且每个候选方案都在布线后签核（post-route signoff）处进行评估。在这些基线中，AgenticPD在实现强劲的布线后时序的同时，在功耗和面积方面保持竞争力。

Original abstract: Physical design quality-of-results~(QoR) optimization is hard and expensive. Choices made at one stage can help or hurt later stages. Each evaluation requires a costly EDA run through the full flow. While existing methods still treat optimization as flat parameter tuning or a LLM-based script generation task, we present AgenticPD, a stage-aware agentic framework for physical design QoR optimization. Instead of re-running the full flow after every trial, AgenticPD is organized around the stage boundaries of the physical design flow, where a Judge Agent navigates the search and stage-specialized agents make local decisions within their own stage using stage-local tools. Additionally, the agent harness in AgenticPD provides structured observations, execution history, and agent context management. As a result, the system can branch from prior intermediate states and reuse checkpoints to continue the optimization procedure, and every candidate is evaluated at the post-route signoff. Across these baselines, AgenticPD achieves strong post-route timing while remaining competitive in power and area.

</details>


### [42] [CARL: Constraint-Aware Reinforcement Learning for Planning with LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04854v1)
*Qiuyi Qi,Jinjian Zhang,Mutian Bao,Tian Liang,Guocong Li,Dongnan Liu,Wei Zhou,Jie Liu,Ming Kong,Linjian Mo,Feng Zhang,Qiang Zhu*

Selection reason: 提出约束感知RL框架增强LLM规划能力，直接属于agent规划与RL方法。

TL;DR: 提出CARL框架，通过约束感知奖励增强LLMs的约束意识，在多个任务上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLMs生成计划常违反任务约束，缺乏内在约束意识，现有方法依赖外部工具或任务分解，未能从本质上解决问题。

Method: 提出CARL，一种强化学习框架，通过比较模型在约束和未约束输入下的输出分布设计约束感知奖励，鼓励关注约束并惩罚忽视，兼容多种RL框架，无需外部求解器。

Result: 在BlocksWorld、TravelPlanner和T-Eval上，CARL显著优于RFT基线和最先进推理模型，约束关注度大幅提升。

Conclusion: CARL有效增强了LLMs的内在约束感知能力，实现了可扩展的端到端约束感知规划，验证了方法的有效性和通用性。

中文摘要：尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）具有强大的推理能力和广泛的世界知识，但它们经常生成违反任务约束的计划，从而削弱了其在实际应用中的可靠性。这种缺陷源于在生成过程中缺乏系统性机制来整合约束信息。现有方法试图通过依赖外部工具或任务分解来缓解这一问题，但未能增强模型内在的约束意识。为解决这一问题，我们提出了约束感知强化学习（CARL），这是一种新颖的强化学习框架，旨在增强LLMs对约束的内在关注。CARL通过比较模型在受约束和未约束输入下的输出分布，引入约束感知奖励，鼓励关注约束并惩罚忽视。CARL与各种强化学习框架兼容，无需外部求解器或顶级模型，实现了可扩展的端到端约束感知规划。在BlocksWorld、TravelPlanner和T-Eval上的大量实验表明，CARL显著优于标准强化微调（RFT）基线和最先进的推理模型，展现出对约束的明显增强的关注。

Original abstract: Despite their strong reasoning capabilities and extensive world knowledge, Large Language Models (LLMs) frequently generate plans that violate task constraints, undermining their reliability in real-world applications. This deficiency arises from a lack of systematic mechanisms to incorporate constraint information during the generation process. While existing approaches attempt to mitigate this by relying on external tools or task decomposition, they fail to enhance the model's intrinsic constraint awareness. To address this, we propose Constraint-Aware Reinforcement Learning (CARL), a novel RL framework designed to strengthen LLMs' intrinsic focus on constraints. CARL introduces a constraint-aware reward by comparing the model's output distributions under constrained and unconstrained inputs, encouraging constraint focus and penalizing neglect. Compatible with various RL frameworks and requiring no external solvers or top models, CARL enables scalable, end-to-end constraint-aware planning. Extensive experiments on BlocksWorld, TravelPlanner, and T-Eval demonstrate that CARL significantly outperforms standard Reinforcement Fine-Tuning (RFT) baselines and state-of-the-art reasoning models, exhibiting a markedly increased focus on constraints.

### [43] [STAPO: Selective Trajectory-Aware Policy Optimization for LLM Agent Training](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04963v1)
*Qiuyi Qi,Tian Liang,Mutian Bao,Jinjian Zhang,Dongnan Liu,Wei Zhou,Linjian Mo,Ming Kong,Jie Liu,Feng Zhang,Qiang Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出选择性轨迹感知策略优化训练LLM agent，直接针对agent长程任务。

TL;DR: 提出归一化熵和STAPO框架，缓解LLM智能体的轨迹忽视问题，在多个任务上达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀疏延迟奖励导致轨迹忽视，而现有基于香农熵的步骤级监督方法将状态复杂度与智能体置信度混为一谈，提供不可靠的决策可靠性估计。

Method: 提出归一化熵来衡量置信度偏差，并设计层次分组强化学习框架STAPO，利用归一化熵定位异常步骤，通过轨迹感知奖励和轨迹无关惩罚联合优化。

Result: 在ALFWorld、WebShop和Search-Augmented QA上取得最先进性能，显著缓解轨迹忽视。

Conclusion: STAPO有效且鲁棒，验证了其在智能体任务中的有效性。

中文摘要：强化学习（RL）是在长周期任务上训练大型语言模型（LLM）智能体的主导范式。然而，稀疏和延迟的奖励常常导致轨迹忽视，即智能体在中间步骤中失去对任务目标和交互历史的关注。先前的工作探索了基于香农熵的不确定性信号进行步骤级监督，但这会将固有的状态复杂性与智能体的置信度混为一谈，因此提供了不可靠的决策可靠性估计。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了归一化熵，它衡量相对于智能体在给定状态下的平均行为的置信度偏差，从而加强了低质量动作与轨迹忽视之间的关联。基于这一见解，我们引入了选择性的轨迹感知策略优化（STAPO），一种基于层次分组的强化学习框架。STAPO利用归一化熵定位与轨迹忽视相关的异常步骤，并通过轨迹感知奖励和轨迹无关惩罚的联合机制优化它们，增强了轨迹感知性，同时保持了训练稳定性。在ALFWorld、WebShop和Search-Augmented QA上的大量实验表明，STAPO实现了最先进的性能，同时显著缓解了轨迹忽视，验证了其在智能体任务中的有效性和鲁棒性。

Original abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) is the dominant paradigm for training Large Language Model (LLM) agents on long-horizon tasks. However, sparse and delayed rewards often lead to trajectory neglect, in which agents lose focus on the task goal and interaction history at intermediate steps. Prior work has explored step-level supervision using Shannon-entropy-based uncertainty signals, which conflate inherent state complexity with agent confidence and therefore provide unreliable estimates of decision reliability. To address this issue, we propose normalized entropy, which measures confidence deviations relative to an agent's average behavior under a given state, thereby strengthening the association between low-quality actions and trajectory neglect. Building on this insight, we introduce Selective Trajectory-Aware Policy Optimization (STAPO), a hierarchical group-based RL framework. STAPO leverages normalized entropy to locate outlier steps associated with trajectory neglect and optimizes them via a joint mechanism of trajectory-aware reward and trajectory-independent penalty, enhancing trajectory awareness while preserving training stability. Extensive experiments on ALFWorld, WebShop, and Search-Augmented QA demonstrate that STAPO achieves state-of-the-art performance while substantially alleviating trajectory neglect, validating its effectiveness and robustness for agentic tasks.

</details>


### [44] [Toward Trustworthy Large Language Model Agents in Healthcare](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05055v1)
*Hadi Hasan,Safaa Salman,Adam Tai Abou Dargham,Ammar Mohanna,Ali Chehab*

Main category: cs.AI

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出CareConnect系统，结合LLM函数调用、RAG和分层确定性安全护栏，集成八个领域工具实现预约操作，并通过紧急检测和医学意图拒绝的短路机制保证安全。

Result: 在680个任务场景上，任务完成率91.8%，延迟中位数2.2秒，安全合规性96.0%，平均每次预约成本0.0324美元，相比人工调度大幅降低成本。

Conclusion: 经过严格范围界定和安全保障的LLM代理能够可靠地自动化复杂医疗操作流程，同时保证安全性和成本效率，代码已开源。

中文摘要：医疗预约调度仍然是一个持续的运营瓶颈，由手动协调、碎片化的遗留系统和高行政开销驱动。这些低效率限制了提供者的可用性并降低了患者获得护理的机会。本文介绍了CareConnect，一种用于医疗物流自动化的安全优先对话代理，它利用大型语言模型（LLM）函数调用、检索增强生成（RAG）和分层确定性安全护栏。该系统编排了八个领域特定工具，支持预约预订、修改、取消和设施信息检索，同时强制执行严格的范围约束，禁止医疗建议或诊断。安全关键情况通过用于紧急检测和医疗意图拒绝的确定性短路机制来处理。我们在一个包含680个任务导向场景的综合基准上评估了CareConnect，涵盖了端到端工作流、多轮交互和边缘情况。实验结果表明，任务完成率为91.8%，每次请求的中位延迟为2.2秒，专用安全关键评估子集上的安全合规性为96.0%，每次预约的平均运营成本为0.0324美元，与手动人工调度相比实现了显著的成本降低。这些发现表明，经过仔细范围界定和严格保护的基于LLM的代理可以可靠地自动化复杂的医疗运营工作流，同时保持安全保证并实现显著的成本效率。源代码和系统实现可在https://github.com/Hadi-Hsn/CareConnect公开获取。

Original abstract: Healthcare appointment scheduling remains a persistent operational bottleneck, driven by manual coordination, fragmented legacy systems, and high administrative overhead. These inefficiencies constrain provider availability and degrade patient access to care. This paper presents CareConnect, a safety-first conversational agent for healthcare logistics automation that leverages large language model (LLM) function calling, retrieval-augmented generation (RAG), and layered deterministic safety guardrails. The system orchestrates eight domain-specific tools to support appointment booking, modification, cancellation, and facility information retrieval, while enforcing strict scope constraints that prohibit medical advice or diagnosis. Safety-critical situations are handled through deterministic short-circuit mechanisms for emergency detection and medical intent refusal. We evaluate CareConnect on a comprehensive benchmark of 680 task-oriented scenarios spanning end-to-end workflows, multi-turn interactions, and edge cases. Experimental results demonstrate a 91.8% task completion rate with a median per-request latency of 2.2 seconds, 96.0% safety compliance on the dedicated safety-critical evaluation subset, and an average operational cost of $0.0324 per appointment, yielding a significant cost reduction compared to manual human scheduling. These findings show that carefully scoped and rigorously safeguarded LLM-based agents can reliably automate complex healthcare operational workflows while maintaining safety guarantees and achieving substantial cost efficiency. The source code and system implementation are publicly available at https://github.com/Hadi-Hsn/CareConnect.

### [45] [AgentGym2: Benchmarking Large Language Model Agents in De-Idealized Real-World Environments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05174v1)

Result: 15个模型实验表明，包括Gemini和GPT-5在内的SOTA系统在AgentGym2上表现不佳，存在显著性能差距。

Conclusion: 当前代理能力难以满足现实世界应用需求，AgentGym2揭示了这一差距，并推动更贴近实际的评估。

中文摘要：语言代理，即LLM代理，发展迅速，并越来越多地被部署在生产环境中。这一趋势强调了进行严格和现实评估的紧迫性。然而，大多数现有基准在简化、理想化的设置中评估代理。它们通常依赖预打包的工具接口，忽略关键步骤，并假设输入是干净且完全指定的。因此，它们低估了实际部署的难度，其中不确定性和噪声普遍存在，代理必须主动探索环境以发现新工具。为弥合这一差距，我们提出了AgentGym2，这是一个新的评估框架，其任务实例基于现实世界的端到端工作需求。除了推理和规划，它衡量代理执行端到端程序、通过探索发现工具、为未见任务组合工具以及对噪声和未完全指定信息的鲁棒性。对15个专有和开源模型的实验表明，即使是像Gemini和GPT-5这样的最先进系统也在AgentGym2上表现挣扎，揭示了当前代理能力与现实世界应用需求之间的巨大差距。

Original abstract: Language agents, i.e., LLM agents, progress rapidly and are increasingly deployed in production environments. This trend underscores the urgent need for rigorous and realistic evaluations. However, most existing benchmarks evaluate agents in simplified, idealized settings. They typically rely on pre-packaged tool interfaces, overlook critical steps, and assume inputs are clean and fully specified. Consequently, they understate the difficulty of real deployments, where uncertainty and noise are ubiquitous and agents must proactively explore the environment to uncover new tools. To bridge this gap, we present AgentGym2, a new evaluation framework with task instances grounded in real-world end-to-end working demands. Beyond reasoning and planning, it measures agents' ability to execute end-to-end procedures, discover tools via exploration, compose tools for unseen tasks, and remain robust to noisy and underspecified information. Experiments on 15 proprietary and open-source models show that even SOTA systems like Gemini and GPT-5 struggle on AgentGym2, revealing a substantial gap between the capability of current agents and the demands of real-world applications.

### [46] [ClassicLogic: A Knowledge-Driven Benchmark of Classic Puzzle Games for Evaluating Compositional Generalization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05185v1)
*Mahnoor Shahid,Hannes Rothe*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 组合泛化基准，涉及agent推理评估。

TL;DR: 提出ClassicLogic基准套件，通过层级化显式知识库评估智能体在经典逻辑谜题中的组合泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准多聚焦语言任务，缺乏复杂且显式的组合结构，需要新的基准来评估问题解决中的组合泛化能力。

Method: 构建四个经典逻辑谜题（数独、KenKen、数墙、不等号数独）的层级化显式知识库，将复杂策略定义为基本策略的组合。

Result: 实现了对智能体从基本规则学习到多步组合推理的细粒度评估，且谜题难度经过数学验证。

Conclusion: 该开源基准为神经符号及其他高级AI推理系统提供了具有挑战性的测试平台。

中文摘要：组合泛化，即理解和生成已知组件的全新组合的能力，仍然是现代人工智能面临的一个基本挑战。虽然存在少数基准测试，但许多测试侧重于语言任务，缺乏复杂且明确的组合结构。我们引入了ClassicLogic，这是一个新的基准测试套件，旨在评估智能体学习和组合问题解决策略的能力。该基准测试包含四个经典逻辑谜题：数独、KenKen、数墙和不等号数独。其核心创新在于为每个游戏提供了一个层级化的、显式的知识库，其中复杂的解决策略被正式定义为更简单的基础策略的组合。这种结构允许对智能体的推理能力进行细粒度评估，从学习基本规则到应用多步骤组合策略来解决难度逐渐增加且经过数学验证的谜题。这个开源基准测试为推进神经符号及其他先进人工智能推理系统提供了一个具有挑战性的新测试平台。

Original abstract: Compositional generalization, the ability to understand and produce novel combinations of known components, remains a fundamental challenge for modern artificial intelligence. While few benchmarks exist, many focus on linguistic tasks and lack complex, explicit compositional structures. We introduce ClassicLogic, a new benchmark suite designed to evaluate an agent's ability to learn and compose problem-solving strategies. The benchmark consists of four classic logic puzzles: Sudoku, KenKen, Kakuro, and Futoshiki. Its core innovation is a hierarchical, explicit knowledge base for each game, where complex solving strategies are formally defined as compositions of simpler, foundational strategies. This structure allows for fine-grained evaluation of an agent's reasoning capabilities, from learning basic rules to applying multi-step compositional strategies to solve puzzles of increasing, mathematically validated difficulty. The open-source benchmark provides a challenging new testbed for advancing neuro-symbolic and other advanced AI reasoning systems.

### [47] [Reason, Reward, Refine: Step-Level Errors Corrections with Structured Feedback for Physics Reasoning in Small Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05199v1)
*Raj Jaiswal,Dhruv Jain,Rishabh Dhawan,Sree Krishna Uppalapati,Shin'ichi Satoh,Tanuja Ganu,Rajiv Ratn Shah*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 步骤级奖励框架用于错误修正，可迁移至agent自我改进。

TL;DR: 提出步骤级奖励框架，通过识别首个推理错误并生成结构化反馈，无需真实答案即可训练小语言模型修正错误，在物理推理任务上显著提升准确率并减少各类错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小语言模型在物理推理中因步骤错误传播、领域知识有限、幻觉和分布敏感而表现不佳，现有方法依赖偏好数据或真实答案，不够灵活。

Method: 步骤级奖励框架：识别第一个推理错误，生成结构化反馈，使用带KL正则化的策略梯度训练模型修正解决方案，无需真实答案或偏好数据，外部验证器仅在训练时使用。

Result: 在五个物理基准上，准确率提升17-20%超越CoT，10-16%超越最强基线；计算错误从56.9%降至23.5%，理解错误从22.3%降至12.0%，概念错误从89.7%降至68.7%。

Conclusion: 所提框架有效提升小语言模型的物理推理能力，减少各类错误，但概念错误仍是最难解决的挑战。

中文摘要：物理推理在小语言模型中存在结构性失败：任何步骤的错误都会向前传播，破坏后续的所有推理。有限的领域知识、多步推导下的幻觉以及分布敏感性加剧了这种失败。我们提出了一种步骤级奖励框架，该框架识别第一个推理错误，生成有针对性的结构化反馈，并通过带KL正则化的策略梯度训练模型修改其解决方案，而无需将真实解决方案作为生成目标暴露给模型。与依赖标注的步骤级方法不同，该方法不需要构建偏好数据，且外部验证器仅在训练时运行。在五个物理基准测试中，我们的框架相比思维链提示获得了17-20%的准确率提升，相比最强基线提升了10-16%，将计算错误从56.9%降至23.5%，在最佳观察案例中将理解错误从22.3%降至12.0%。概念错误从89.7%降至68.7%，但在所有条件下仍然是最难解决的失败模式。

Original abstract: Physics reasoning fails structurally in small language models: an error at any step propagates forward, corrupting every inference that follows. Limited domain knowledge, hallucination under multi-step derivation, and distributional sensitivity compound this failure. We propose a step-level reward framework that identifies the first reasoning error, generates targeted structured feedback, and trains the model to revise its solution via policy gradient with KL regularization, without exposing it to ground truth solutions as generation targets. Unlike annotation-dependent step-level methods, no preference data construction is required and the external verifier operates exclusively at training time. Across five physics benchmarks, our framework delivers accuracy gains of 17-20% over CoT prompting and 10-16% over the strongest baseline, reduces calculation errors from 56.9% to 23.5%, and reduces miscomprehension errors from 22.3% to 12.0% in the best observed cases. Conceptual errors reduce from 89.7% to 68.7%, yet persist as the hardest failure mode across all conditions.

### [48] [EvoAgentBench: Benchmarking Agent Self-Evolution via Ability Transfer](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05202v1)
*Xingze Gao,Chuanrui Hu,Hongda Chen,Pengfei Yao,Zhao Wang,Yi Bai,Zhengwei Wu,Yunyun Han,Xiaofeng Cong,Jie Gui,Yafeng Deng,Teng Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: agent自我进化基准，直接研究能力迁移。

TL;DR: EvoAgentBench通过能力引导的程序性迁移评估智能体自我进化，发现精心策划的能力可靠迁移但自动方法尚不完善。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估未分离程序性迁移，智能体基准只测单回合任务，记忆基准只测信息保留，因此需要专门衡量经验重用能力的基准。

Method: 从智能体执行中提取基于轨迹的能力，规范化为操作单元，构建领域能力图连接共享程序重叠的任务，并设计训练/测试分割确保测试任务有训练侧能力支持。

Result: 在528/267分割、两种支架和三种骨干上，精心策划的能力内容在模型家族间可靠迁移，但无自动方法在所有设置中保持正向增益。

Conclusion: EvoAgentBench将自我进化评估从总体准确率转向细粒度诊断，揭示当前自动方法的局限性，并推动程序性迁移研究。

中文摘要：在长程LLM系统中，智能体的自我进化主要是程序性的：有用的经验不仅仅是存储的信息，而是可重用的搜索、调试和验证程序。然而，当前的评估并未分离这种形式的迁移。智能体基准测试评估单回合任务解决；记忆基准测试针对信息保留而非程序重用。我们引入了EvoAgentBench，这是一个通过能力引导的跨四个智能体领域（网络研究、算法推理、软件工程和知识工作）的智能体自我进化基准测试。EvoAgentBench从智能体执行中提取基于轨迹的能力，将其规范化为操作单元，并构建连接共享程序重叠任务的特定领域能力图。通过设计，每个测试任务都得到经过验证的训练侧能力支持。在528/267的训练/测试分割、两种支架和三种骨干模型上，精心策划的能力内容在模型家族间可靠地迁移，但目前没有任何自动方法能在所有设置中保持正向增益。EvoAgentBench将自我进化评估从总体准确率比较转向对经验编码、路由和吸收的细粒度诊断。该基准测试可在https://huggingface.co/datasets/EverMind-AI/EvoAgentBench 公开获取。

Original abstract: Agent self-evolution in long-horizon LLM systems is largely procedural: useful experience is not merely stored information, but reusable procedures for searching, debugging, and verification. Yet current evaluations do not isolate this form of transfer. Agent benchmarks test single-episode task solving; memory benchmarks target information retention rather than procedural reuse. We introduce EvoAgentBench, a benchmark for agent self-evolution via Ability-guided transfer across four agentic domains: web research, algorithmic reasoning, software engineering, and knowledge work. EvoAgentBench extracts trace-grounded Abilities from agent executions, canonicalizes them into operational units, and builds domain-specific Ability Graphs linking tasks that share procedural overlap. By design, every test task is backed by verified training-side Ability support. Across a 528/267 train/test split, two scaffolds, and three backbones, curated Ability content transfers reliably across model families, but no current automatic method sustains positive gain in all settings. EvoAgentBench shifts self-evolution evaluation from aggregate accuracy comparison to fine-grained diagnosis of experience encoding, routing, and uptake. The benchmark is publicly available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/EverMind-AI/EvoAgentBench.

### [49] [MoP-JEPA: Hard-Assigned Predictor Mixtures for Stochastic JEPA World Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05238v2)
*Zhi Song,Ximing Xing,Zhenchao Tang,hanbo Huang,Weilong Yan,Tianxu Lv,Minghao Yang,Zhongzheng Niu,Bing He,Lusheng Wang,Jianhua Yao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 世界模型预测器混合，对agent环境建模有启发。

TL;DR: MoP-JEPA通过多预测器头和图搜索在随机转换中显著提升后继状态预测成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统JEPA世界模型使用单一回归器预测下一个潜在状态，在随机转换下会给出折中预测，可能不符合任何有效后继状态，导致图搜索成功率低。

Method: MoP-JEPA采用K个硬分配头和仅基于上下文的路由器，在一次前向传播中生成有限候选集，并通过图搜索选择最佳后继。

Result: 在OGBench转换上，MoP-JEPA的图搜索成功率达到0.85，而单输出预测器仅0.02-0.09；在三个迷宫的验证路径成功率（realroute）上，MoP-JEPA均领先于MDN等基线。

Conclusion: MoP-JEPA通过多预测器生成有限候选集，有效提升了随机动态下世界模型预测的实用性，优于单输出预测器和MDN等覆盖导向方法。

中文摘要：JEPA世界模型通常使用一个回归器来预测下一个潜在状态。在随机转换下，平方回归和余弦回归分别返回条件均值及其归一化方向：一个可能不符合任何有效后继状态的单一折中方案。MoP-JEPA则使用K个硬分配头和仅基于上下文的路由器，在一次前向传播中生成一个有限的候选集。在保留的OGBench转换上，使用单输出预测器的图搜索在0.02%至0.09%的查询中成功，而MoP-JEPA达到了0.85%。为了区分有用后继状态与无差别覆盖，我们还测量了验证路径成功率（realroute），它在图构建后检查提议是否包含真实转换的路径。MoP-JEPA在所有三个迷宫的相同协议指标上领先；MDN达到了高原始覆盖率，但预测了许多不存在的边。

Original abstract: JEPA world models commonly predict the next latent state with one regressor. Under stochastic transitions, squared and cosine regression return the conditional mean and its normalized direction, respectively: a single compromise that may match no valid successor. MoP-JEPA instead uses $K$ hard-assigned heads and a context-only router to produce a finite candidate set in one pass. On held-out OGBench transitions, graph search with single-output predictors succeeds on $0.02$--$0.09$ of queries, whereas MoP-JEPA reaches $0.85$. To distinguish useful successors from indiscriminate coverage, we also measure verified-route success (\emph{realroute}), which checks after graph construction whether the proposal contains a path of real transitions. MoP-JEPA leads this same-protocol metric on all three mazes; an MDN attains high raw coverage but predicts many nonexistent edges.

### [50] [MetaSkill-Evolve: Recursive Self-Improvement of LLM Agents via Two-Timescale Meta-Skill Evolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05297v1)
*Zefeng Wang,Minxi Yan,Jinhe Bi,Sikuan Yan,Volker Tresp,Yunpu Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 递归元技能演化的自我改进LLM agent框架，直接适用于agent自动化优化与技能复用。

TL;DR: 提出MetaSkill-Evolve，一种递归改进代理技能的双时间尺度框架，任务技能和元技能分别在快慢循环中进化，在多个基准上显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自我改进代理只能改进任务技能，而无法递归改进改进过程本身，限制了适应性。

Method: 设计双时间尺度框架，每个分支包含任务技能和由五个组件参数化的元技能，元技能在慢循环中通过将改进流水线应用于自身来进化，所有组件共享冻结骨干。

Result: 在OfficeQA、SealQA、ALFWorld上，相比无技能、静态技能和单级进化基线，准确率分别提升23.54、16.09和1.92个百分点。

Conclusion: MetaSkill-Evolve实现了递归的代理技能改进，无需额外模型或目标，显著提升了长程开放任务的性能。

中文摘要：近期LLM代理处理越来越长程、开放式任务，外部技能（可重用的程序性知识，提供给代理）进一步扩展了这种能力。然而，固定的手工技能很少是最优的，并且无法适应代理遇到的任务多样性。自我改进代理通过从执行轨迹重写自己的技能文件来解决这个问题，在具有挑战性的基准上取得了有意义的收益。然而，这种自我进化仍然是非递归的：它只改进了任务技能（代理做什么），而改进过程（它如何改进）是一次性创作并保持固定。我们提出了MetaSkill-Evolve，一个双时间尺度框架，使代理技能改进递归化：每个分支都携带一个任务技能s和一个分支局部元技能m=(ψ,σ,α,π,ε)，其五个组件参数化了改进流水线的分析器、检索器、分配器、提议器和进化器代理。任务技能在快循环上进化，而元技能在慢循环上，在相同的流水线应用于自身时进化，无需额外的模型或目标。所有五个流水线代理共享一个单一的冻结骨干，MetaSkill-Evolve在三个代理基准（OfficeQA, SealQA, ALFWorld）上优于无技能、静态技能和单级进化基线，分别将保留测试准确率比原始骨干提高+23.54、+16.09和+1.92个百分点。

Original abstract: Recent LLM agents tackle increasingly long-horizon, open-ended tasks, and external skills, reusable procedural knowledge supplied to the agent, further extend this capability. However, a fixed, hand-authored skill is rarely optimal, and cannot adapt to the diversity of tasks an agent encounters. Self-improving agents address this by rewriting their own skill files from execution traces, yielding meaningful gains on challenging benchmarks. Yet such self-evolution remains non-recursive: it improves only the task skill (what the agent does) while the improvement procedure (how it improves) is authored once and held fixed. We introduce MetaSkill-Evolve, a two-timescale framework that makes agentic skill improvement recursive: every branch carries both a task skill $s$ and a branch-local meta-skill $m=(ψ,σ,α,π,\varepsilon)$ whose five components parameterise the Analyzer, Retriever, Allocator, Proposer, and Evolver agents of the improvement pipeline. Task skills evolve on a fast loop while the meta-skill evolves on a slower one under the same pipeline applied to itself, with no additional model or objective. With all five pipeline agents sharing a single frozen backbone, MetaSkill-Evolve outperforms no-skill, static-skill, and single-level evolution baselines on three agentic benchmarks (OfficeQA, SealQA, ALFWorld), improving held-out test accuracy over the raw backbone by +23.54, +16.09, and +1.92 points respectively.

</details>


### [51] [BatteryLake: Agentic, Physics-Grounded Curation of Heterogeneous Battery Aging Data and Benchmarking](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09762v1)
*Tianwen Zhu,Hao Wang,Yonggang Wen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM agent驱动的电池数据整理框架，可迁移至代码优化benchmark数据整合。

TL;DR: 提出BatteryLake，一个通过LLM智能体和物理规则自动整理公共电池数据的湖仓，并发布包含41个数据集的标准化基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 公共电池老化数据集使用受限，因为格式不一致、元数据分散，且手动整理难以复现，通用工具缺乏电化学领域语义。

Method: 使用LLM代理提取元数据并合成转换器，基于逐字证据；结合人在回路机制，通过26条规则（模式、统计、物理合理性）验证数据。

Result: 发布41个数据集（来自25+机构）的基准，含标准化SOH/RUL任务、3种分割协议和8个基线模型。

Conclusion: BatteryLake通过智能体驱动、物理基础的整理框架有效解决了电池数据异构性问题，并提供了公开的标准化基准。

中文摘要：公共电池老化数据集是先进健康管理的关键资产，但它们的实际使用往往受到格式不一致、模式不清晰以及元数据分散在存储库和出版物中的限制。当前的整理工作仍然主要是手动的且难以复现，而通用的数据集成工具则缺少电化学时间序列数据的领域特定语义。我们提出了BatteryLake，一个受治理的数据湖仓，通过基于智能体、物理基础的整理框架，将原始公共电池数据转化为可用于基准测试的资产，共有三个贡献。首先，LLM代理提取元数据并合成数据集特定的转换器，将每个输出基于逐字证据，并在没有证据支持值时弃权。其次，一种人在回路机制将验证框架化为选择性预测，并通过26个模式、统计和物理合理性规则来把关准入数据。第三，我们发布了一个包含来自25多个机构的41个数据集的开放基准，具有标准化的SOH和RUL任务、三种分割协议和八个基线模型族。该平台、基准和整理协议可在https://tianwen1209.github.io/batterylake/公开获取。

Original abstract: Public battery aging datasets are a critical asset for advanced health management, but their practical use is often limited by inconsistent formats, unclear schemas, and metadata scattered across repositories and publications. Current curation remains largely manual and hard to reproduce, while general-purpose data integration tools miss the domain-specific semantics of electrochemical time-series data. We present BatteryLake, a governed data lakehouse that turns raw public battery data into benchmark-ready assets through an agentic, physics-grounded curation framework, with three contributions. First, LLM agents extract metadata and synthesize dataset-specific converters, grounding every output in verbatim evidence and abstaining when none supports a value. Second, a human-in-the-loop mechanism frames verification as selective prediction and gates admitted data through 26 schema, statistical, and physical-plausibility rules. Third, we release an open benchmark of 41 datasets from over 25 institutions, with standardized SOH and RUL tasks, three split protocols, and eight baseline model families. The platform, benchmark, and curation protocol are publicly available at https://tianwen1209.github.io/batterylake/.

### [52] [OptiAgent: End-to-End Optimization Modeling via Multi-Agent Iterative Refinement](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05346v1)
*Adriana Laurindo Monteiro,Nayse Fagundes,Gabriel Mattos Langeloh,Gustavo de Oliveira Kanno,Priscila Louise Aguirre,Thiago Costa Rizuti da Rocha,Victor Leme Beltran*

  <summary>Details</summary>

中文摘要：我们提出了OptiAgent，一个多智能体框架，给定运筹学问题的自然语言描述，能够输出求解器就绪的数学公式以及可执行代码。我们的架构优先考虑数学建模步骤，其中专门的智能体提取结构，例如决策变量和约束，从而实现迭代自我纠正。我们引入了一种新颖的多循环验证架构，具有四种专门的反馈机制，每种机制针对不同的故障模式，如误解、结构缺陷、数学不一致、验证失败和代码错误。除了准确性，我们的模块化设计通过提高透明度来改进解决优化问题的过程，因为每个智能体都暴露了其推理和反馈，使得整个建模过程可审计。我们的框架在LP、MILP和非线性规划任务的4个基准中的3个上达到了最先进的性能，同时在剩余数据集上保持高度竞争力。

Original abstract: We propose OptiAgent, a multi-agent framework that, given a natural language description of an Operations Research problem, is able to output a solver-ready mathematical formulation as well as executable code. Our architecture prioritizes the mathematical modeling step, where dedicated agents extract structures, such as decision variables and constraints, enabling iterative self-correction. We introduce a novel multi-loop validation architecture with four specialized feedback mechanisms, each targeting a distinct failure mode such as misinterpretation, structural defects, mathematical inconsistencies, validation failures, and code errors. Alongside accuracy, our modular design improves the process of solving optimization problems by improving transparency, as each agent exposes its reasoning and feedback, making the full modeling process auditable. Our framework achieves state-of-the-art performance on 3 out of 4 benchmarks across LP, MILP, and Nonlinear Programming tasks, while remaining highly competitive on the remaining dataset.

### [53] [SovereignPA-Bench: Evaluating User-Owned Personal Agents under Evolving Intent, Platform Mediation, and Consent Constraints](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05363v1)
*Dylan Zongmin Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 个人agent评测基准，涉及进化意图、隐私和同意约束，可迁移至agent评测与安全控制。

TL;DR: 提出SovereignPA-Bench基准，衡量个人代理的主权，实验表明完全主权脚手架优于基线，强调评估需关注隐私、同意和证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准只关注任务完成，忽略用户主权（隐私、同意、证据、抵抗操纵等），需要更全面的评估方法。

Method: 设计SovereignPA-Bench，包含120个演化意图场景，分离ObservableState和HiddenLabels，评估任务成功、对齐、隐私、同意等组件指标，在4个模型家族和8个政策基线上进行3,840次轨迹测试。

Result: 完全主权脚手架在主权得分上显著优于直接、记忆、同意、证据、ReAct等基线，并降低隐私泄露和操纵捕获；人类审计显示隐私和同意一致性高，操纵一致性低。

Conclusion: 个人代理评估必须超越任务完成，转向代表性、同意意识和证据基础的行动，以维护用户主权。

中文摘要：个人代理正成为持久性的用户所有中介：它们记住偏好、过滤平台中介信息、使用工具并与服务协商。现有的基准评估了工具使用、网页导航、桌面控制、个性化、推荐和演化上下文，但很少询问代理是否维护用户主权：在尊重隐私、同意、证据、用户负担和抵抗操纵激励的同时，推进用户当前利益。我们引入了SovereignPA-Bench，一个可执行的基准，用于评估用户拥有的个人代理，在演化意图、平台中介、隐私边界、同意约束、证据要求和负担权衡下。该基准将代理可见的ObservableState与仅评估者可见的HiddenLabels分开，报告任务成功、对齐、隐私、同意、证据、操纵、负担和可审计性的组件指标，并保留配对场景顺序以进行模型和政策比较。我们评估了跨4个模型家族和8个政策基线的120个主权压力场景，产生了3,840个冻结提示轨迹，包含原始提示、输出、提供者表单响应、解析动作、可重新计算的指标、硬集分析、定性案例以及240个项目的盲审3标注者审计。完全主权脚手架相比直接、仅记忆、仅同意、仅证据、ReAct/工具使用、安全提示和法官守卫基线提高了主权得分，同时减少了隐私泄露、同意违反、过度让步和操纵捕获。人类审计显示在隐私和同意上高度一致，在操纵上一致性较低，识别了平台说服判断的主观边界。这些结果表明，个人代理评估必须超越任务完成，走向代表性、同意意识、证据基础的行动。

Original abstract: Personal agents are becoming persistent user-owned intermediaries: they remember preferences, filter platform-mediated information, use tools, and negotiate with services. Existing benchmarks evaluate tool use, web navigation, desktop control, personalization, recommendation, and evolving context, but rarely ask whether an agent preserves user sovereignty: advancing the user's current interests while respecting privacy, consent, evidence, user burden, and resistance to manipulative incentives. We introduce SovereignPA-Bench, an executable benchmark for evaluating user-owned personal agents under evolving intent, platform mediation, privacy boundaries, consent constraints, evidence requirements, and burden tradeoffs. The benchmark separates agent-visible ObservableState from evaluator-only HiddenLabels, reports component metrics for task success, alignment, privacy, consent, evidence, manipulation, burden, and auditability, and preserves paired scenario ordering for model and policy comparisons. We evaluate 120 sovereignty stress scenarios across 4 model families and 8 policy baselines, yielding 3,840 frozen-prompt trajectories with raw prompts, outputs, provider-form responses, parsed actions, recomputable metrics, hard-set analyses, qualitative cases, and a blinded 3-annotator audit over 240 items. Full-sovereign scaffolding improves sovereignty score over direct, memory-only, consent-only, evidence-only, ReAct/tool-use, safety-prompt, and judge-guard baselines while reducing privacy leakage, consent violation, over-concession, and manipulation capture. Human audit shows high agreement on privacy and consent and lower agreement on manipulation, identifying the subjective frontier of platform-persuasion judgments. These results show that personal-agent evaluation must move beyond task completion toward representative, consent-aware, evidence-grounded action.

### [54] [LLM-as-a-Verifier: A General-Purpose Verification Framework](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05391v2)
*Jacky Kwok,Shulu Li,Pranav Atreya,Yuejiang Liu,Yixing Jiang,Chelsea Finn,Marco Pavone,Ion Stoica,Azalia Mirhoseini*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 通用验证框架LLM-as-a-Verifier，用于agent任务，在SWE-Bench上SOTA，直接相关。

TL;DR: 提出LLM-as-a-Verifier，通过连续分数实现可扩展的验证，在多个基准上达到SOTA，并可用于任务估计和RL反馈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM验证方法依赖离散评分，难以有效区分方案优劣，且缺乏可扩展性。作者希望将验证作为一个新的扩展轴，通过概率化连续评分实现多维度扩展，提升验证效果。

Method: LLM-as-a-Verifier通过计算评分token logits分布的期望生成连续分数，在三个维度扩展：分数粒度（细粒度评分）、重复评估（多次采样求平均）、标准分解（将复杂标准拆解为子标准）。并设计成本高效的排序算法选择最佳方案。

Result: 在Terminal-Bench V2、SWE-Bench Verified、RoboRewardBench、MedAgentBench上达到SOTA（86.5%、78.2%、87.4%、73.3%），且验证信号可提升RL样本效率。

Conclusion: 验证作为新的扩展轴有效，LLM-as-a-Verifier的连续分数可提高验证准确性，并作为通用工具用于任务监控和RL训练，未来可进一步扩展。

中文摘要：预训练、后训练和测试时计算的扩展已成为提高LLM能力的核心范式。在这项工作中，我们识别出验证——即判断解决方案正确性的能力——作为新的扩展轴。为了解锁这一能力并展示其有效性，我们引入了LLM-as-a-Verifier，这是一个通用验证框架，能够为智能体任务提供细粒度反馈，无需额外训练。与标准LM评价器通过提示LLM为候选方案生成离散分数不同，LLM-as-a-Verifier通过计算评分token logits分布的期望来生成连续分数。这种概率公式使验证能够在多个维度上扩展：(1)分数粒度，(2)重复评估，(3)标准分解。特别是，我们展示了扩展评分粒度可以更好地区分正负解决方案，从而实现更校准的比较。此外，扩展重复评估和标准分解通过方差和复杂度降低，持续带来验证准确性的额外增益。我们还引入了一种成本高效的排序算法，利用验证器的连续分数从候选方案中选择最佳方案。LLM-as-a-Verifier在Terminal-Bench V2（86.5%）、SWE-Bench Verified（78.2%）、RoboRewardBench（87.4%）和MedAgentBench（73.3%）上达到了最先进的性能。除验证外，来自LLM-as-a-Verifier的细粒度信号还可以作为估计任务进展的代理。我们为Claude Code构建了一个扩展，使开发者能够监控和改进自己的智能体系统。最后，我们展示了LLM-as-a-Verifier可以为强化学习提供密集反馈，提高SAC和GRPO在机器人学和数学推理基准上的样本效率。

Original abstract: Scaling pre-training, post-training, and test-time compute have become the central paradigms for improving the capabilities of LLMs. In this work, we identify verification, the ability to determine the correctness of a solution, as a new scaling axis. To unlock this and demonstrate its effectiveness, we introduce LLM-as-a-Verifier, a general-purpose verification framework that provides fine-grained feedback for agentic tasks without requiring additional training. Unlike standard LM judges that prompt LLMs to produce discrete scores for candidate solutions, LLM-as-a-Verifier computes the expectation over the distribution of scoring token logits to generate continuous scores. This probabilistic formulation enables verification to scale along multiple dimensions: (1) score granularity, (2) repeated evaluation, and (3) criteria decomposition. In particular, we show that scaling the scoring granularity leads to better separation between positive and negative solutions, resulting in more calibrated comparisons. Moreover, scaling repeated evaluation and criteria decomposition consistently lead to additional gains in verification accuracy through variance and complexity reduction. We further introduce a cost-efficient ranking algorithm for selecting the best solution among candidates using the verifier's continuous scores. LLM-as-a-Verifier achieves state-of-the-art performance on Terminal-Bench V2 (86.5%), SWE-Bench Verified (78.2%), RoboRewardBench (87.4%), and MedAgentBench (73.3%). Beyond verification, the fine-grained signals from LLM-as-a-Verifier can also serve as a proxy for estimating task progress. We build an extension for Claude Code, enabling developers to monitor and improve their own agentic systems. Finally, we show that LLM-as-a-Verifier can provide dense feedback for RL, improving the sample efficiency of SAC and GRPO on robotics and mathematical reasoning benchmarks.

</details>


### [55] [Foundation Models for Automatic CAD Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05573v1)
*J de Curtò,Victoria Guillén,I. de Zarzà*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自动CAD生成框架，使用多模型迭代优化，可迁移至代码优化agent的方法。

TL;DR: 提出了LLMForge框架，结合迭代评判（分析或VLM）生成机械CAD模型，在97个设计问题基准上评估7个模型，最高模型达98.97%网格成功率，VLM评判实现100%水密网格但旋转对称体有困难。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动从自然语言生成CAD设计可以加速机械设计流程，但现有方法缺乏统一评估和系统性研究。本文旨在通过构建基准和框架，比较不同基础模型在CAD生成中的表现，并探索不同评判机制的效果。

Method: 提出LLMForge多模型文本到CAD框架，包括JSON模式验证、分析特征评分、网格合成和多轮迭代优化。设计两种评判机制：IterTracer使用分析视觉度量（如轮廓IoU），IterVision使用VLM（Qwen2.5-VL-72B）进行语义评判。在97个设计问题的基准上评估7个基础模型。

Result: 在IterTracer下，前四名模型（DeepSeek-V3.2等）总体均值0.885-0.890，网格成功率98.97%。IterVision下领先模型达到100%水密网格，但圆柱等旋转对称几何体出现系统性困难。紧凑模型表现与大型模型相当。

Conclusion: 紧凑的指令调优模型在CAD生成中能匹配大型模型；VLM评判提升水密性但暴露旋转对称体的挑战；工作为可扩展自动化机械设计提供了基准和框架，并指出了未来研究方向。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）和视觉语言模型（VLMs）的最新进展使得能够从自然语言规格说明自动生成参数化3D设计。本章介绍了基础模型在机械零件自动计算机辅助设计（CAD）生成中的实证研究，使用了统一的评估流水线和包含97个工程设计问题的精选基准。我们提出了LLMForge，一个多模型文本到CAD框架，集成了JSON模式验证、分析特征评分、网格合成和多轮迭代优化，并在两种评判机制下进行研究。IterTracer使用基于冯氏着色的光线追踪渲染器，结合分析视觉度量（轮廓IoU、孔洞可见性、边缘间隙、长宽比符合度）在轮次间提供轻量级几何感知反馈。IterVision用VLM语义评判器（Qwen2.5-VL-72B）替代分析评分器，该评判器通过思维链视觉推理评估渲染视图，评估空间一致性和设计意图。在涵盖四个规范几何系列（带孔和螺栓圆的平板、多特征盒子、法兰圆柱和L型支架）的基准上，我们评估了七个基础模型：DeepSeek-V3.2、Qwen3-235B-A22B、Llama-3.3-70B、Gemma-3-27B、GLM-4.5、MiniMax-M2.1和INTELLECT。在IterTracer下，排名最高的四个模型形成紧密聚类（总体均值在[0.885, 0.890]之间），网格成功率达到98.97%，表明紧凑的指令调优模型可以与更大的系统相匹敌。在IterVision中基于VLM的评判在领先模型上实现了100%的水密网格生成，同时揭示了在旋转对称几何体（如圆柱体）上存在的系统性困难，其中视觉和语义评分分歧最大。我们讨论了基准设计、失败模式、面向CAD的提示，以及对工业工作流程和可扩展自动化机械设计的影响。

Original abstract: Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) and Vision-Language Models (VLMs) enable the automatic generation of parametric 3D designs from natural-language specifications. This chapter presents an empirical study of foundation models for automatic Computer-Aided Design (CAD) generation of mechanical parts, using a unified evaluation pipeline and a curated benchmark of 97 engineering design problems. We introduce LLMForge, a multi-model text-to-CAD framework integrating JSON-schema validation, analytic feature scoring, mesh synthesis, and multi-round iterative refinement, studied under two critique regimes. IterTracer uses a Phong-shaded ray-trace renderer with analytic visual metrics (silhouette IoU, hole visibility, edge clearance, aspect-ratio conformance) for lightweight geometry-aware feedback across rounds. IterVision replaces the analytic scorer with a VLM semantic critic (Qwen2.5-VL-72B) that evaluates rendered views via chain-of-thought visual reasoning, assessing spatial coherence and design intent. On a benchmark spanning four canonical geometry families (plates with holes and bolt circles, multi-feature boxes, flanged cylinders, and L-brackets), we evaluate seven foundation models: DeepSeek-V3.2, Qwen3-235B-A22B, Llama-3.3-70B, Gemma-3-27B, GLM-4.5, MiniMax-M2.1, and INTELLECT. Under IterTracer, the four highest-ranked models form a tight cluster (overall mean in [0.885, 0.890]) with 98.97% mesh success, showing that compact instruction-tuned models can match substantially larger systems. VLM-based critique in IterVision yields 100% watertight mesh generation on the leading model while surfacing systematic difficulty on rotationally symmetric geometries such as cylinders, where visual and semantic scoring diverge most. We discuss benchmark design, failure modes, CAD-oriented prompting, and implications for industrial workflows and scalable automated mechanical design.

### [56] [Narrative World Model: Narratology-Grounded Writer Memory for Long-Form Fiction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05577v1)
*Mohammad Saifullah,Thomas Kornmaier,Taaha Kazi,Vasu Sharma,Aditya Sanjiv Kanade,Aanand Kumar Yadav*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: NWM在两个语料库上显著优于Graphiti/Zep等基线，并远超GraphRAG和平面检索；优势源于表示结构而非提取质量。

Conclusion: 叙事学结构表示和查询条件化检索是提升叙事记忆系统的关键。

中文摘要：长篇小说的作者需要一种能够回答关于故事状态演变的复杂多跳问题的记忆：谁在什么时候知道了秘密，某个事件是否先于揭示它的叙述发生，伏笔是否得到呼应，以及关系如何变化。通用检索和智能体记忆系统能够表示实体和事实，但无法表示这些问题所依赖的叙事学结构，因此它们要么提供错误的证据，要么完全不提供。我们引入了叙事世界模型（NWM），这是一种作者记忆系统，它将基于叙事学的类型化时间状态图与查询条件化的混合检索配对。为了衡量记忆而非回答者的能力，我们通过一个固定的Opus 4.8阅读器，仅基于每个系统的章节安全证据，在可复现的公共语料库和经过验证的多跳基准上，对每个系统进行读取，并与现有最强的时间知识图谱智能体记忆框架Graphiti/Zep（Rasmussen等人，2025）进行比较。NWM在两个语料库上的多跳叙事学问答中显著优于该基线，并远超GraphRAG和平面检索。这一优势是表示层面的，而非提取的人为产物：即使使用NWM自身的提取器重建基线，这一优势仍然存在，并可归因于其基于叙事学的结构和查询条件化检索，而非图大小或提取器质量。

Original abstract: Long-form fiction writers need memory that answers multi-hop questions about evolving story state: who knows a secret and when they learned it, whether an event preceded the narration that revealed it, whether a setup paid off, and how a relationship shifted. General-purpose retrieval and agent-memory systems represent entities and facts but not the narratological structure these questions turn on, so they surface the wrong evidence or none at all. We introduce the Narrative World Model (NWM), a writer-memory system that pairs a narratology-grounded typed temporal-state graph with query-conditioned hybrid retrieval. To measure memory rather than the answerer, we read every system through a single held-constant Opus 4.8 reader over only that system's chapter-safe evidence, on a reproducible public corpus and a validated multi-hop benchmark, and we compare against the strongest existing temporal-knowledge-graph agent-memory framework, Graphiti/Zep (Rasmussen et al., 2025). NWM substantially and significantly outperforms this baseline on multi-hop narratological QA across both corpora, and far exceeds GraphRAG and flat retrieval. The advantage is representational rather than an artifact of extraction: it survives rebuilding the baseline with NWM's own extractor, and traces to its narratology-grounded structure and query-conditioned retrieval, not to graph size or extractor quality.

</details>


### [57] [FirstResearch: Auditable Question Formation for LLM Scientific Discovery Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05682v1)
*Yufeng Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 科学发现agent的可审计问题形成框架，可迁移至代码agent的审计性。

TL;DR: 提出FirstResearch框架，通过结构化研究问题证书使LLM生成的科学问题更可审计，实验表明优于现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM系统提出的科学问题难以审计，因为它们可能听起来合理却没有暴露机制、证伪因素或假设。

Method: 设计FirstResearch框架，核心是结构化研究问题证书，包括原始定义、假设、机制模型、张力、可证伪假设、最小决定性测试和失败更新规则。通过LLM盲审和独立评审在十个主题上评估。

Result: 在DeepSeek盲审中FirstResearch优于基线；Gemini独立评审保持排名，证书核心得分4.86/5（基线4.38/5）；消融显示证书核心最强（4.90/5），移除后低于1/5。

Conclusion: 显式推导约束是使LLM生成的科学问题更可审计的一种有前途机制，但结果初步且使用LLM评委，需进一步验证。

中文摘要：用于科学发现的LLM系统越来越多地协助构思、文献综合、实验计划和报告生成，但它们提出的第一个研究问题可能仍然难以审计：这个问题听起来合理，却没有暴露科学家应该检查的机制、证伪因素或假设。我们介绍了FirstResearch，一种用于科学LLM代理的第一性原理研究问题形成框架，其核心工件是一个结构化的研究问题证书。该证书记录了原始定义、假设、机制模型、张力或矛盾、可证伪假设、最小决定性测试和失败更新规则，使得提出的问题在下游执行之前可以被检查。在十个LLM代理研究主题上，FirstResearch在主要的DeepSeek盲审协议下优于受AI co-scientist、Agent Laboratory和AI Scientist-v2启发的受控提示级别基线。Gemini-2.5-Flash独立评审对相同的40个基线包重新评分，保持了系统级排名，FirstResearch得分为4.86/5，而最强基线为4.38/5，平均得分的Pearson一致度为0.865。一次重复的消融检查点进一步表明，以证书为中心的核心是最强组件：仅使用证书在DeepSeek下得分为4.90/5，在Gemini下为4.88/5，而移除证书后，在两个评委下的得分均低于1/5。这些结果是初步的，并且使用LLM评委而非人类领域专家，但它们支持一个狭窄的科学发现主张：显式推导约束是使LLM生成的科学问题更可审计的一种有前途机制。代码、提示、保存的输出和复现脚本可在https://github.com/louiswang524/FirstResearch获取。

Original abstract: LLM systems for scientific discovery increasingly assist with ideation, literature synthesis, experiment planning, and report generation, but the first research question they propose can remain difficult to audit: it may sound plausible without exposing the mechanism, falsifier, or assumption that a scientist should inspect. We introduce FirstResearch, a first-principles research-question formation framework for scientific LLM agents whose core artifact is a structured Research Question Certificate. The certificate records primitive definitions, assumptions, a mechanism model, a tension or contradiction, a falsifiable hypothesis, a minimal decisive test, and a failure update rule, making the proposed question inspectable before downstream execution. On ten LLM-agent research topics, FirstResearch outperforms controlled prompt-level baselines inspired by AI co-scientist, Agent Laboratory, and AI Scientist-v2 under a primary DeepSeek-blind-judge protocol. A Gemini-2.5-Flash independent-judge rescore of the same 40 baseline packages preserves the system-level ranking, with FirstResearch scoring 4.86/5 versus 4.38/5 for the strongest baseline and Pearson agreement of 0.865 on average score. A one-repeat ablation checkpoint further suggests that the certificate-centered core is the strongest component: certificate-only scoring reaches 4.90/5 under DeepSeek and 4.88/5 under Gemini, while removing certificates drops below 1/5 under both judges. These results are preliminary and use LLM judges rather than human domain experts, but they support a narrow scientific-discovery claim: explicit derivation constraints are a promising mechanism for making LLM-generated scientific questions more auditable. Code, prompts, saved outputs, and reproduction scripts are available at https://github.com/louiswang524/FirstResearch.

</details>


### [58] [Memory in the Loop: In-Process Retrieval as ExtendedWorking Memory for Language Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05690v1)
*Yusuf Khan,Carlo Lipizzi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 内存循环机制降低agent延迟，对agent记忆架构设计有重要启发。

TL;DR: 将记忆移入语言代理的循环内（每步读写）并采用进程内存储（~100us延迟）可大幅降低冗余动作并提升召回率，且嵌入式网络延迟成为新瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言代理的记忆位于循环外，导致高延迟和冗余动作；本文旨在验证循环内记忆模式是否能通过进程内存储克服延迟障碍。

Method: 比较不同存储位置（网络化 vs. 进程内）下语言代理的冗余动作和召回率；使用GPT-5类模型在限窗任务中测试，并测量延迟组成。

Result: 进程内存储（80-165us）下冗余动作从7.2/12降至0.0/12，召回率从0/5升至3.6-4.8/5；嵌入延迟成为主要成本（200-400ms），本地嵌入器可降至40us；存储无丢失。

Conclusion: 进程内存储使循环内记忆模式可行，将记忆转化为扩展工作记忆，但需解决嵌入式网络延迟以进一步优化。

中文摘要：语言代理运行一个循环——观察、推理、行动——但它们推理所依赖的记忆位于循环之外：一个每回合最多查询一次的存储。我们研究了将记忆移入循环内、每一步都进行读写的情况。障碍始终是延迟：网络化存储的回答时间在几十到几百毫秒之间，当检索成本高时，循环内检索会使端到端延迟增加多达83倍。先前的工作管理这种成本而不是质疑它：服务层调度隐藏了它，“记忆优先”设计将检索限制为每回合一次。我们认为延迟是存储所在位置的属性，而不是循环模式的属性：进程内存储的回答时间约为100微秒，比网络化存储低三个数量级，在这种速度下，每步开销就消失了。根据扩展心灵理论的对称原则，一个足够快以至于可以持续直接访问的存储变成了扩展的工作记忆，而不是代理仅仅咨询的工具。前提是因果性的：保持每回合固定的记忆延迟预算，仅改变存储的回答速度，冗余动作随延迟单调增加——在进程内速度下为0.0/12，在110毫秒云往返中为7.2/12（gpt-5-nano, gpt-5-mini；精确排列p=0.0079）。我们端到端地展示了这一模式：在四个GPT-5类模型上，在边界窗口内，使用循环内记忆，召回率从0/5提高到3.6-4.8/5，存储操作的中位延迟为80-165微秒——尽管一个指示性的“重复每个回复”基线也完美解决了问题，但其令牌成本随工作集增长。存储从未在任何运行中丢失事实（244次写入全部保持）；每次遗漏都归因于代理的读取策略，而不是存储。我们的测量还重新定位了瓶颈：主要的每步成本是嵌入（通过网络约200-400毫秒）；将进程内存储与小型本地嵌入器配对，整个操作测量到的延迟约为40微秒。

Original abstract: Language agents run a loop - observe, reason, act - but the memory they reason over sits outside it: a store queried at most once per turn. We study the regime where memory moves inside the loop, read and written on every step. The obstacle has always been latency: networked stores answer in tens to hundreds of milliseconds, and in-loop retrieval can inflate end-to-end latency by up to 83x when retrieval is expensive. Prior work manages that cost rather than questioning it: serving-layer scheduling hides it, "memory-first" designs ration retrieval to once per turn. We argue latency is a property of where the store lives, not the in-loop pattern: an in-process store answers in ~100us, three orders of magnitude below the network regime, and at that speed the per-step tax collapses. By the extended-mind thesis's parity principle, a store fast enough to be constantly and directly available becomes extended working memory, not a tool the agent merely consults. The premise is causal: holding a fixed per-turn memory-latency budget and varying only the store's answer speed, redundant actions rise monotonically with latency - 0.0 of 12 at in-process speed, 7.2 of 12 at a 110ms cloud round trip (gpt-5-nano, gpt-5-mini; exact permutation p=0.0079). We demonstrate the regime end-to-end: across four GPT-5-class models under a bounded window, recall improves from 0/5 to 3.6-4.8/5 with in-loop memory, store ops at p50 80-165us - though an instructed restate-every-reply baseline also solves it perfectly, at a token cost that grows with the working set. The store never lost a fact in any run (244 of 244 writes kept); every miss traces to the agent's read policy, not the store. Our measurements also relocate the bottleneck: the dominant per-step cost is embedding (~200-400ms over the network); pairing the in-process store with a small local embedder returns the complete operation to a measured ~40us.

</details>
