### [59] [A Few Teacher Steps Go a Long Way: Cost-Efficient On-Policy Data Augmentation for Agent Post-Training](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04574v1)
*Junze Ye,Jiayi Cheng,Miao Lu,Michal Mankowski,Jose Blanchet,Mohsen Bayati*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 研究LLM agent后训练中按策略数据增强的成本效益分配，直接在多种agent任务上验证，是通用的agent训练机制。

TL;DR: 纯行为克隆存在训练与测试上下文不一致的问题。本文将其视为预算分配问题，提出在学习者诱导的上下文中使用有限步数的教师延续，发现这种策略在匹配预算下优于更长的或过滤的教师完成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的监督微调方法存在上下文不匹配问题，纯粹行为克隆使用完整演示，而最近工作通过过滤教师延续来缓解，但成本高。本文旨在寻找更高效的监督资源分配方式。

Method: 将在线策略数据构建形式化为预算分配问题，涉及推出策略、切换时间、延续视界、过滤规则和两种成本。通过实验比较不同策略的性能。

Result: 在HotpotQA、ALFWorld和Terminal-Bench-Dev上，在学习者诱导上下文中使用有限步数未过滤教师延续优于纯行为克隆，且几步延续匹配或超过过滤替代方案。

Conclusion: 在学习者诱导上下文中放置少量教师步骤是比更长或更精心策划的教师完成更成本高效的监督分配方式。

中文摘要：对于LLM智能体，监督微调不仅关乎教师标签的质量，还关乎这些标签所条件化的交互上下文。纯粹的行为克隆使用完整的教师演示，造成了训练中看到的教师诱导上下文与测试时遇到的学生诱导上下文之间的不匹配。最近的工作通过查询学生达到的上下文处的教师来解决这种不匹配，通常伴随着对教师延续进行越来越精细的过滤。相反，我们将在线策略数据构建视为一个预算分配问题：在匹配的监督资源下，教师输出应该花在更多的从头到尾的演示、更长的延续、结果过滤还是更广泛地覆盖学习者诱导的上下文？我们通过推出策略、切换时间分布、延续视界、过滤规则以及两个互补成本（过滤前生成的教师推理和保留用于SFT的教师监督）来形式化这个设计空间。在HotpotQA、ALFWorld和Terminal-Bench-Dev上，在学习者诱导的上下文处的有界未过滤教师延续在匹配预算下优于纯粹的行为克隆。在HotpotQA和ALFWorld上，我们进行了完整比较，几步延续匹配或超过了成功过滤和关键上下文过滤的替代方案。我们的发现表明，在学习者诱导的上下文处放置少量的教师步骤可能比更长或更精心策划的教师完成更具成本效益的监督分配。

Original abstract: For LLM agents, supervised fine-tuning is not only about teacher labels' quality, but also about which interaction contexts those labels condition on. Pure behavioral cloning uses full teacher demonstrations, creating a mismatch between teacher-induced contexts seen in training and student-induced contexts encountered at test time. Recent work addresses this mismatch by querying a teacher at contexts reached by the student, often with increasingly elaborate filtering of the teacher's continuations. We instead frame on-policy data construction as a budget-allocation problem: under matched supervision resources, should teacher output be spent on more start-to-finish demos, longer continuations, outcome filtering, or broader coverage of learner-induced contexts? We formalize this design space through the rollout policy, switch-time distribution, continuation horizon, filtering rules, and two complementary costs: teacher inference generated before filtering and teacher supervision retained for SFT. Across HotpotQA, ALFWorld, and Terminal-Bench-Dev, bounded unfiltered teacher continuations at learner-induced contexts improve over pure behavioral cloning at matched budgets. On HotpotQA and ALFWorld, where we run the full comparison, few-step continuations match or exceed success-filtered and critical-context-filtered alternatives. Our findings suggest that a few teacher steps, placed at learner-induced contexts, can be a more cost-efficient supervision allocation than longer or more heavily curated teacher completions.

</details>


### [60] [Beyond the Need for Speed: Energy-Aware Code Generation via Simulation-Guided Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04577v1)
*Saurabhsingh Rajput,Tushar Sharma*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出用确定性仿真代替硬件测量来训练节能代码模型，构建Green Tea数据集，通过监督微调和强化学习训练能量感知模型，并引入CARET指标评估，在保留问题上取得显著能效提升，同时揭示IPC作为能效代理的不可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码模型只关注功能正确性，忽略能效；硬件测量因方差无法提供可重复反馈，需要可扩展的仿真方法。

Method: 使用确定性架构模拟构建Green Tea数据集（350万评估），通过能量对比对监督微调，再结合GRPO强化学习（仿真在环反馈）训练能量感知模型，并引入CARET指标惩罚牺牲功能换取效率的行为。

Result: 在143个保留问题上取得12.63% CARET，比单独微调提升近三倍，58.4%有效输出超越人类专家能效；分析发现IPC在67.8%问题上错误排序能效。

Conclusion: 直接能量模拟对训练节能代码模型至关重要，发布数据集和基础设施可促进社区研究，推动节能代码生成模型部署。

中文摘要：代码模型严格优先考虑功能正确性，将软件能效视为未优化的副产品。训练模型生成节能代码需要可扩展的可重复反馈，而由于硬件测量的方差，物理硬件测量无法可靠提供。在本文中，我们用确定性架构模拟框架替代硬件性能分析，构建了Green Tea，一个包含来自1,474个C++问题的350万次评估的数据集。我们通过在能量对比对上进行监督微调，然后使用仿真在环反馈进行闭环强化学习（GRPO），训练了一个能量感知的代码模型。为了严格评估部署准备程度，我们引入了正确性调整后的能量总减少量（CARET），该指标明确惩罚牺牲功能以换取效率的代码。在143个保留问题上，我们的仿真在环流程实现了12.63%的CARET，几乎将单独微调的增益提高了三倍，并且在其有效输出中成功击败了人类专家参考的能效，占58.4%。此外，我们的分析揭示了IPC陷阱：像每周期指令数（IPC）这样的标准吞吐量代理在67.8%的问题上主动错误排序真实能效，证明了直接能量模拟的绝对必要性。通过发布我们的数据集和基础设施，我们绕过了重现所需的263,000 CPU小时，从根本上赋能社区部署固有节能的代码生成模型。

Original abstract: Code models strictly prioritize functional correctness, leaving software energy efficiency as an unoptimized byproduct. Training models to generate energy-efficient code requires reproducible feedback at scale, which physical hardware measurement cannot reliably provide due to variance.
  In this paper, we replace hardware profiling with a deterministic architectural simulation harness to build Green Tea, a corpus of $3.5$ million evaluations across $1{,}474$ C++ problems. We train an energy-aware code model via supervised fine-tuning on energy-contrastive pairs, followed by closed-loop reinforcement learning (GRPO) using simulation-in-the-loop feedback. To rigorously evaluate deployment readiness, we introduce the Correctness-Adjusted Reduction in Energy Total (CARET), a metric that explicitly penalizes code that sacrifices functionality for efficiency.
  On $143$ held-out problems, our simulation-in-the-loop pipeline achieves $12.63\%$ CARET, nearly tripling the gain of fine-tuning alone, and successfully beats the energy efficiency of human-expert references on $58.4\%$ of its valid outputs. Furthermore, our analysis exposes the IPC trap: standard throughput proxies like Instructions-Per-Cycle (IPC) actively misrank true energy efficiency on $67.8\%$ of problems, proving the absolute necessity of direct energy simulation. By releasing our dataset and infrastructure, we bypass the $263{,}000$ CPU-hours required for reproduction, structurally empowering the community to deploy inherently energy-efficient code generation models.

</details>


### [61] [RSPO: Reward-Swap Policy Optimization for Multi-Turn LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04713v1)
*Qiang Liu,Taian Guo,Ruizhi Qiao,Xing Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出RSPO用于多轮LLM agent训练，解决奖励稀疏问题，直接适用于coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出奖励交换策略优化（RSPO），通过奖励交换机制结合过程奖励的丰富信息与结果奖励的真实性，提升多轮交互任务的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在长周期多轮任务中，直接使用稀疏结果奖励收敛慢且易错过未采样轨迹；而使用密集过程奖励可能因与真实结果奖励不一致而偏斜训练方向。需要一种方法兼顾两者优势。

Method: RSPO采用奖励交换机制，在训练过程中交替使用过程奖励和结果奖励，既利用过程奖励的密集信号增强采样多样性，又通过交换保证优化目标与结果奖励一致。

Result: 在WebShop和ALFWorld基准测试上，将RSPO应用于GRPO、PPO和GiGPO算法，均取得一致性能提升，证明了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: RSPO通过奖励交换有效解决了稀疏结果奖励和密集过程奖励之间的矛盾，提升了模型在复杂多轮任务中的性能上限。

中文摘要：强化学习在训练大型语言模型处理多轮交互任务方面具有重要潜力。然而，在具有稀疏结果奖励的长周期多轮任务中，直接使用结果奖励进行训练往往由于信号稀疏和缺乏细粒度反馈而导致收敛缓慢。此外，模型可能无法学习到训练期间未采样的成功轨迹，从而限制其性能。相反，虽然使用定制的密集过程奖励提供了更丰富的信号并加速收敛，但这些代理奖励可能与真实结果奖励存在潜在的不一致。这种不一致可能偏斜训练方向，最终降低模型的最终性能。在这项工作中，我们提出了奖励交换策略优化（RSPO），一种旨在利用密集过程奖励的丰富信息来促进结果奖励训练的方法。通过利用奖励交换机制，RSPO确保采样轨迹的多样性，同时保证优化目标与真实结果奖励之间的一致性，从而提升模型的性能上限。我们在两个具有挑战性的智能体基准测试WebShop和ALFWorld上进行了大量实验。通过将我们的方法应用于多种强化学习算法，包括GRPO、PPO和GiGPO，我们证明了RSPO在不同的基线和基准测试中均取得了持续的性能提升。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning holds significant potential for training large language models (LLMs) to handle multi-turn interactive tasks. However, in long-horizon, multi-turn tasks characterized by sparse outcome rewards, directly training with outcome rewards often results in slow convergence due to the sparsity of signals and the lack of fine-grained feedback. Furthermore, the model may fail to learn successful trajectories that are not sampled during training, thereby limiting its performance. Conversely, while employing customized dense process rewards provides richer signals and accelerates convergence, these surrogate rewards may exhibit potential misalignment with the ground-truth outcome rewards. This inconsistency can bias the training direction and ultimately degrade the model's final performance. In this work, we propose Reward-Swap Policy Optimization (RSPO), a method designed to leverage the rich information from dense process rewards to facilitate training with outcome rewards. By utilizing a reward-swap mechanism, RSPO ensures the diversity of sampled trajectories while guaranteeing consistency between the optimization objective and the true outcome rewards, thereby elevating the performance ceiling of the model. We conduct extensive experiments on two challenging agent benchmarks, WebShop and ALFWorld. By applying our method to various reinforcement learning algorithms, including GRPO, PPO, and GiGPO, we demonstrate that RSPO achieves consistent performance improvements across different baselines and benchmarks.

</details>


### [62] [Multi-Turn On-Policy Distillation with Prefix Replay](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04763v2)
*Baohao Liao,Hanze Dong,Christof Monz,Xinxing Xu,Li Dong,Furu Wei*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出ReOPD用于多轮LLM agent on-policy蒸馏，减少环境交互，直接适用于coding agent训练。

TL;DR: ReOPD proposes an off-environment distillation method that reuses teacher trajectories as prefixes, avoiding costly online rollouts and addressing the prefix trap via a step-decaying sampling schedule.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The high cost of fully online on-policy distillation for multi-turn agentic tasks, requiring fresh student rollouts and teacher queries.

Method: ReOPD reuses pre-collected teacher trajectories as replayed prefixes; student acts at selected steps while teacher provides per-step supervision. It treats multi-turn OPD as reliability-aware prefix design with a step-decaying sampling schedule to emphasize early, lower-shift prefixes.

Result: ReOPD preserves or improves OPD accuracy, uses zero tool calls during student training, and is at least 4x faster per rollout than OPD.

Conclusion: ReOPD turns expensive agent-environment interaction into a reusable offline resource, enabling scalable distillation across tools, tasks, and environments.

中文摘要：我们研究用于智能体任务的在线策略蒸馏（OPD），其中LLM智能体与环境进行多轮交互，学生在这多轮交互历史中模仿教师。完全在线的OPD成本高昂，因为每次更新都需要学生新的环境交互以及教师在所访问历史处的查询。我们提出重放前缀在线策略蒸馏（ReOPD），一种脱离环境的替代方案，它重用预收集的教师轨迹作为重放前缀：学生在选定步骤行动，而教师提供密集的逐步骤监督，无需执行新的环境交互。我们表明多轮OPD引入了一个前缀陷阱：使历史更符合学生在线策略提高了与学生相关性，但可能查询教师在目标不可靠的历史。这造成了学生占用与教师可靠性之间的双边分布偏移。ReOPD通过将多轮OPD视为可靠性感知的前缀分布设计来解决这一问题，并采用简单的逐步衰减采样调度实现，该调度强调早期、偏移较小的前缀。在涉及Python数学推理和搜索环境、多种教师和学生模型规模下，ReOPD保持或提高了OPD级别的准确率，在学生训练期间使用零工具调用，并且每次 rollout 至少比OPD快4倍。因此，ReOPD将昂贵的智能体-环境交互转变为可重用的离线资源，实现了跨工具、任务和环境可扩展的蒸馏。

Original abstract: We study on-policy distillation (OPD) for agentic tasks, where an LLM agent interacts with an environment over multiple turns and a student imitates a teacher over these multi-turn interaction histories. Fully online OPD is costly because each update requires fresh student rollouts through the environment and teacher queries at visited histories. We propose Replayed-Prefix On-Policy Distillation (ReOPD), an off-environment alternative that reuses pre-collected teacher trajectories as replayed prefixes: the student acts at selected steps, while the teacher provides dense per-step supervision without executing new environment interactions. We show that multi-turn OPD introduces a prefix trap: making histories more student-on-policy improves relevance to the student, but can query the teacher on histories where its target is unreliable. This creates a two-sided distribution shift between student occupancy and teacher reliability. ReOPD addresses this by treating multi-turn OPD as a reliability-aware prefix distribution design and implements it with a simple step-decaying sampling schedule that emphasizes early, lower-shift prefixes. Across mathematical reasoning with Python and search environments over multiple teacher and student model scales, ReOPD preserves or improves OPD-level accuracy, uses zero tool calls during student training, and is at least 4$\times$ faster per rollout than OPD. ReOPD therefore turns expensive agent-environment interaction into a reusable offline resource, enabling scalable distillation across tools, tasks, and environments.

</details>


### [63] [PDEFlow: Autonomous Agentic PDE Pipelines for Neural Operator Learning and Solver-Free Inference](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05134v1)
*Akshat Jani,Prathamesh Gadekar,Sakhinana Sagar Srinivas,Venkataramana Runkana*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 自治agent管道处理PDE，通用agent工作流架构有启发。

TL;DR: PDEFlow是一个自主框架，将ODE/PDE描述转化为求解器支持的神经算子流水线，实现规范、数据生成、训练和推理的自动化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 减少手动干预，自动化物理配置的规范、模拟、学习和查询过程，支持可重复的科学和工程工作流。

Method: 使用状态输入图处理自然语言输入和编辑，生成有效问题规范；数据生成模块通过FEniCSx有限元求解器采样参数并存储张量；基于注册表的接口支持不同神经算子，当前实例化为多分支贝叶斯DeepONet。

Result: 在基准ODE和PDE任务上，PDEFlow成功构建有效规范、生成求解器数据集、训练稳态和瞬态问题的神经算子，并能从保存的检查点进行无求解器预测。

Conclusion: 该框架适用于需要最少手动干预的可重复科学和工程工作流，能够高效处理大量相关物理配置。

中文摘要：我们提出了PDEFlow，一个自主智能体框架，将用户层面的ODE和PDE描述转化为求解器支持的神经算子流水线。该工作流链接了问题规范、数据生成、算子训练和基于检查点的推理。一个状态输入图将多轮自然语言输入和用户编辑转换为经过验证的问题规范。然后，数据生成模块对参数进行采样，使用FEniCSx有限元后端求解配置的控制方程，并将解存储为算子就绪的张量。训练和推理阶段使用基于注册表的接口，允许不同的神经算子进行训练和部署，而无需更改周围的流水线。在当前实现中，我们使用多分支贝叶斯DeepONet实例化该接口。在基准ODE和PDE任务上的实验表明，PDEFlow可以构建有效的规范，生成求解器支持的数据集，在稳态和瞬态问题类别上训练神经算子，并从保存的检查点提供无求解器的预测。该框架专为可重复的科学和工程工作流而设计，在这些工作流中，许多相关的物理配置必须用最少的手动干预进行规范、模拟、学习和查询。

Original abstract: We present PDEFlow, an autonomous agentic framework that turns user-level ODE and PDE descriptions into solver-backed neural-operator pipelines. The workflow links problem specification, data generation, operator training, and checkpoint-based inference. A stateful input graph converts multi-turn natural-language input and user edits into validated problem specifications. The data-generation module then samples parameters, solves the configured governing-equation with FEniCSx finite-element backend, and stores the solutions as operator-ready tensors. The training and inference stages use a registry-based interface, allowing different neural operators to be trained and deployed without changing the surrounding pipeline. In the current implementation, we instantiate this interface with a multi-branch Bayesian DeepONet. Experiments on benchmark ODE and PDE tasks show that PDEFlow can construct valid specifications, generate solver-backed datasets, train neural operators across steady and transient problem classes, and provide solver-free predictions from saved checkpoints. The framework is designed for repeatable scientific and engineering workflows where many related physics configurations must be specified, simulated, learned, and queried with minimal manual intervention.

### [64] [Latent Programming Horizons in Coding Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05188v1)
*André Silva,Han Tu,Martin Monperrus*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 编码代理中语言模型的残差流线性编码程序演化属性，且能提前约25步预测未来编辑结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编码代理在任务中执行复杂编辑，但对其内部程序理解机制缺乏了解。

Method: 在隐藏状态上训练逻辑回归探针，解码代码解析、测试通过、失败减少和回归等属性，并预测未来编辑结果。

Result: 探针正确性AUC达0.83，且能提前最多25步预测未来编辑，跨基准迁移无需重新训练。

Conclusion: 语言模型在编码代理中线性编码程序状态并提前预测，促进机制可解释性研究。

中文摘要：解决软件工程任务的编码代理会花费数十步进行推理、编辑代码和运行测试，然而我们对其底层语言模型内部关于所处理程序的表现知之甚少。我们表明，编码代理下的语言模型的残差流线性地编码了演化程序的性质：在隐藏状态上的逻辑回归探针能够解码当前代码是否解析、通过测试套件、减少失败测试数量以及引入回归，在两个模型和两个基准测试中正确性AUC达到0.83。我们的第二个发现更令人惊讶：这些表示领先于代理自身的编辑。训练用于预测未来编辑结果（在它们实现并写入磁盘之前）的探针能够在大约25步之前达到高于随机水平的性能。我们称之为代理的潜在编程视野。作为外部有效性的证明，我们展示了探针无需重新训练即可跨基准测试迁移。我们的积极结果呼吁对编码代理的机制可解释性进行更多研究。

Original abstract: A coding agent solving a software-engineering task spends dozens of steps reasoning, editing code, and running tests, yet little is known about what the underlying language model internally represents about the program it is working on. We show that the residual streams of language models under coding agents linearly encode properties of the evolving program: a logistic-regression probe on hidden states is able to decode whether the current code parses, passes its test suite, reduces the number of failing tests, and introduces regressions, reaching AUC up to 0.83 for correctness across two models and two benchmarks. Our second finding is more surprising: these representations run ahead of the agent's own edits. Probes trained to predict the outcome of future edits (before they are materialized and written on disk) achieve performance above chance up to roughly 25 steps in advance. We call this the agent's latent programming horizon. As a proof of external validity, we show that the probes transfer across benchmarks without retraining. Our positive results open calls for more research in mechanistic interpretability of coding agents.

</details>


### [65] [PatchOptic for Shared-State LLM Workflows with Projected Views and Verified Structured Updates](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05483v1)
*Zhaoyu Bai,Jiaqi Cai*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出共享状态LLM工作流的projected reads和verified patches，可迁移至coding agent的状态管理与验证。

TL;DR: PatchOptic为LLM工作流提供了一种基于光学的接口，通过投影读取和验证补丁确保局部更新的全局有效性，在减少泄漏和成本的同时保持输出质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法缺少局部更新与全局状态有效性之间的契约，导致无法验证局部修改是否破坏全局一致性。

Method: 提出PatchOptic，利用光学的双向访问器概念，实现投影读取和结构化补丁验证，包含声明投影视图、授权写入区域和补丁源区域，并提供路径级足迹支持组合与重排序。

Result: 在PatchBench上评估，投影读取减少泄漏和token成本，保留输出质量；运行时验证阻止契约违规，补丁读取拒绝隐藏源干扰。

Conclusion: PatchOptic通过声明式契约有效管理局部更新与全局状态的一致性，为LLM工作流提供可靠且高效的状态操作机制。

中文摘要：智能体工作流通常操作于共享的结构化状态。由于LLM上下文窗口有限，每个模型调用通常仅显示当前工作流步骤所需的状态片段，这种模式通常称为渐进式展示。现代系统使用类似grep的关键词搜索、检索增强生成（RAG）、抽象语法树（AST）查询和特定任务的智能体技能来构建此类模型视角的视图。这些方法使读取侧变得可管理，但它们未定义局部提议的重写在应用于完整状态后何时有效。缺失的部分是局部更新与全局有效性之间的契约。我们引入了PatchOptic，一种用于共享状态LLM工作流的、受光学启发的接口。光学是可组合的双向访问器，描述结构化数据的读取和更新方式。PatchOptic借鉴了这种视图/更新直觉，并通过投影读取和验证的结构化补丁来实现。每个工作流步骤声明一个投影读取视图、一个授权写入区域和一个补丁源区域。除了运行时强制之外，相同的声明还产生一个路径级足迹，支持委派、子工作流组合以及同一阶段内独立步骤重排序的静态证书。我们通过PatchBench（跨领域的46个案例）评估了此设计。结果表明，在强智能体下，投影读取减少了报告的泄漏和token成本，同时保持了接受的输出质量。运行时验证在提交前阻止声明的 workflow 契约违规，补丁读取强制拒绝使用隐藏源的受损补丁工件。

Original abstract: Agentic workflows often operate over shared, structured state. Because LLM context windows are limited, each model invocation is typically shown only the state fragment needed for the current workflow step, a pattern commonly known as progressive disclosure. Modern systems construct such model-facing views using grep-like keyword search, retrieval-augmented generation (RAG), abstract-syntax-tree (AST) queries, and task-specific agent skills. These methods make the read side manageable, but they do not define when a locally proposed rewrite is valid after it is applied back to the full state. The missing piece is a contract between local updates and global validity. We introduce PatchOptic, an optic-inspired interface for shared-state LLM workflows. Optics are compositional bidirectional accessors that describe how views of structured data are read and updated. PatchOptic borrows this view/update intuition and realizes it through projected reads and verified structured patches. Each workflow step declares a projected read view, an authorized write region, and a patch-source region. Beyond runtime enforcement, the same declaration yields a path-level footprint that supports delegation, sub-workflow composition, and static certificates for reordering independent steps within the same phase. We evaluate this design with PatchBench, a benchmark with 46 cases across domains. The results show that projected reads reduce reported leakage and token cost while preserving accepted-output quality under the strong actor. Runtime verification blocks declared workflow-contract violations before commit, and patch-read enforcement rejects compromised patch artifacts that use hidden sources.

</details>


### [66] [TREK: Distill to Explore, Reinforce to Refine](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05339v1)
*Yuanda Xu,Zhengze Zhou,Kayhan Behdin,Jelena Markovic-Voronov,Hejian Sang,Xiaomin Li,Wenhui Zhu,Xinchen Du,Aida Rahmattalabi,Ran He,Sen Na,Zhipeng Wang,Alborz Geramifard*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 通过蒸馏扩展支持提升GRPO，在agentic任务上显著提升，可迁移至agent训练方法。

TL;DR: 提出TREK方法，通过前向KL蒸馏扩展探索支持，解决GRPO在困难提示上的停滞问题，在数学推理和智能体任务上显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GRPO在困难提示上因学生策略的在线支持不足而停滞，需要扩展探索支持以覆盖正确的解题模式。

Method: TREK分阶段：先识别低通过率提示，利用教师生成验证候选解，按学生似然排序保留前r个，通过短暂前向KL阶段将验证模式拉入学生支持，再回到标准GRPO微调。

Result: 数学推理：Qwen3-8B在AIME 2025从36.9到40.3，AIME 2024从47.9到51.1；智能体：ALFWorld从75.8到82.8，ScienceWorld从12.5到26.7。

Conclusion: TREK通过蒸馏扩展支持，有效提升GRPO在困难任务上的表现，且通用性强，可适用不同教师类型。

中文摘要：Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) 在当前策略已经采样有用的推理轨迹时是有效的，但在困难提示上会停滞，因为正确的解题模式位于学生策略的在线支持之外。我们提出 TREK (Teacher-Routed Exploration via Forward KL)，一种简单的分阶段过程，它利用蒸馏不是为了模仿，而是为了扩展探索支持。TREK 的一个关键优势是其通用性：因为它只消耗验证过的输出轨迹，它可以使用外部黑盒教师、白盒教师，或者同一模型在额外推理时上下文下的自身，并且即使教师内部不可用，它也能高效识别哪些困难提示样本最值得巩固。TREK 首先识别那些未受助学生通过率非常低的提示，查询一个提案源以生成验证过的候选解，保留按当前学生似然排名的前 r 个提案，应用一个短暂的前向 KL 阶段将这些验证过的模式拉入学生的支持范围内，然后返回到标准的在线策略 GRPO 微调。在数学推理上，使用 DeepSeek-V4 提案的 TREK 在 AIME 2024 和 AIME 2025 上所有测试规模的 Qwen3 模型上都取得了改进；对于 Qwen3-8B，它在 AIME 2025 上从 36.9 提高到 40.3，在 AIME 2024 上从 47.9 提高到 51.1（avg@16），而自上下文变体在没有外部教师的情况下达到了 38.5 和 49.6。在智能体任务上，TREK 将 ALFWorld 成功率从 75.8 提高到 82.8，ScienceWorld 成功率从 12.5 提高到 26.7；值得注意的是，在最困难的任务类型上，TREK 在训练早期就达到了高成功率，而未受助的 GRPO 需要更多的优化步骤才能达到可比水平。

Original abstract: Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) is effective when the current policy already samples useful reasoning trajectories, but it stalls on hard prompts whose correct solution modes lie outside the student's on-policy support. We propose TREK (Teacher-Routed Exploration via Forward KL), a simple staged procedure that uses distillation not for imitation but for exploration support expansion. A key advantage of TREK is its generality: because it only consumes verified output trajectories, it can use an external black-box teacher, a white-box teacher, or the same model given additional inference-time context, and it can efficiently identify which hard-prompt samples are most worth consolidating even when teacher internals are unavailable. TREK first identifies prompts where the unaided student has very low pass rate, queries a proposal source to produce verified candidate solutions, keeps the top-$r$ proposals ranked by current student likelihood, applies a short forward-KL phase to pull those verified modes into the student's support, and then returns to standard on-policy GRPO refinement. On mathematical reasoning, TREK with DeepSeek-V4 proposals improves Qwen3 models across all tested scales on AIME 2024 and AIME 2025; for Qwen3-8B, it improves AIME 2025 from 36.9 to 40.3 and AIME 2024 from 47.9 to 51.1 (avg@16), while the self-context variant reaches 38.5 and 49.6 without an external teacher. On agentic tasks, TREK raises ALFWorld success rate from 75.8 to 82.8 and ScienceWorld success rate from 12.5 to 26.7; notably, on the hardest task types, TREK achieves high success rates early in training while unaided GRPO requires substantially more optimization steps to reach comparable levels.

</details>


### [67] [Self-Review Reinforcement Learning (SRRL) with Cross-Episode Memory and Policy Distillation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05541v1)
*Muhammad Zain Amin,Kibele Sebnem Yildirim*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 自我审查RL结合跨episode记忆与策略蒸馏，直接涉及agent反思、记忆与自我改进。

TL;DR: Self-Review Reinforcement Learning (SRRL) embeds a self-review step into RL episodes to improve learning from sparse feedback, outperforming standard RLVR on GSM8K.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Reinforcement learning for large language models faces challenges due to sparse or delayed environmental feedback, making it hard to identify which actions led to success or failure.

Method: SRRL adds an explicit self-review step in each RL episode: when a first attempt fails, the model generates a self-review explaining the error and conditions an improved second attempt. It optimizes self-review with policy gradients and internalizes improvements via selective distillation, with cross-episode memory for reusing successful self-reviews.

Result: SRRL consistently outperforms standard RLVR in final reward performance and achieves greater learning efficiency on GSM8K across two language models (Qwen 3-4B and OLMo-3-7B).

Conclusion: The framework effectively transforms feedback into behavioral improvement, demonstrating that explicit self-review and selective distillation enhance learning from sparse signals.

中文摘要：强化学习通常用于通过环境反馈来训练大型语言模型。在实际应用中，环境通常提供稀疏或延迟的反馈。这使得模型难以确定其推理中的哪些行为导致了成功或失败。因此，从这些信号中有效学习是困难的，因为模型必须确定每个失败应如何在后续迭代中转化为有意义的行为修正。我们引入了一个训练框架，即自我反思强化学习，它将明确的自我反思步骤嵌入到每个强化学习回合中。当首轮回答失败时，模型会生成自我反思以识别问题所在，从而为改进的第二轮回答创造条件。与推理时的反思方法（如Reflexion）不同，该框架通过策略梯度优化自我反思，并通过选择性蒸馏将改进内化到基础策略中，确保它们在未来的回合中持续存在。跨回合记忆在训练过程中保留成功的自我反思，以便在遇到类似任务时重复使用。我们使用GRPO优化器，在GSM8K基准上，针对两个语言模型（Qwen 3-4B和OLMo-3-7B），将SRRL与标准的RLVR基线进行了评估。SRRL在最终奖励性能上持续优于RLVR，并通过成功地将反馈转化为行为改进，实现了更高的学习效率。

Original abstract: Reinforcement Learning is commonly used to train large language models using environmental feedback. In applied settings, the environment usually provides sparse or delayed feedback. This makes it difficult for the model to pinpoint which actions in its reasoning led to success or failure. So, learning effectively from these signals is hard because the model must determine how each failure should inform meaningful behavioral corrections in subsequent iterations. We introduce a training framework, Self-Review Reinforcement Learning, that embeds an explicit self-review step into each RL episode. When a first-pass response fails, the model generates a self-review to identify what went wrong, which conditions an improved second attempt. Unlike inference-time reflection approaches, such as Reflexion, the framework optimizes self-review with policy gradients and internalizes improvements into the base policy via selective distillation, ensuring they persist across future episodes. A cross-episode memory keeps successful self-reviews for reuse when encountering similar tasks in future episodes during training. We evaluate SRRL against a standard RLVR baseline using the GRPO optimizer across two language models, Qwen 3-4B and OLMo-3- 7B, on GSM8K benchmark. SRRL consistently outperforms the RLVR in final reward performance and achieves greater learning efficiency by successfully transforming feedback into behavioral improvement.

</details>


### [68] [Safe Bayesian Optimization with Counterfactual Policies](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05620v1)
*Katherine Avery,Bruno Castro da Silva,David Jensen*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 安全贝叶斯优化，对agent安全决策有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 提出一种结合共形预测和安全贝叶斯优化的方法，在反事实基线策略下进行安全优化，保证约束违反率可控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多实际场景要求新干预措施不降低结果至阈值以下，而传统优化方法未考虑反事实基线的不确定性。

Method: 使用共形预测构建反事实基线结果的不确定性区间，并融入安全贝叶斯优化框架，同时适应协变量偏移。

Result: 提供了安全性证明、实验证据和敏感性分析，表明方法能有效控制约束违反率。

Conclusion: 该方法能在保证安全性的前提下优化目标，适用于临床医学等需要反事实基线评估的场景。

中文摘要：在许多决策制定场景中，只有当新干预措施不会将结果降低到某个既定阈值以下时，才可接受。例如，在临床医学中，新疗法通常仅当其不会相对于既定护理标准恶化结果时才可接受。安全贝叶斯优化在满足安全约束的条件下最大化目标函数。在我们考虑的场景中，安全性是相对于一个已知的基线策略定义的，该策略的结果是反事实的，因此未被观测到。因此，必须估计基线策略的反事实结果，并利用这些（不确定的）估计来安全地优化目标函数。我们通过使用共形预测为反事实基线结果构建有效的不确定性区间来解决这一估计问题，并展示了如何将这些区间整合到安全贝叶斯优化中，以确保约束违反率不高于用户指定的水平。我们还展示了如何使这些共形估计适应不同类型的协变量偏移。我们提供了安全性证明、实验证据和敏感性分析。

Original abstract: In many decision-making settings, new interventions are acceptable only if they do not reduce outcomes below some established threshold. For example, in clinical medicine, new treatments are often acceptable only if they do not worsen outcomes relative to an established standard of care. Safe Bayesian optimization maximizes an objective subject to safety constraints. In the setting that we consider here, safety is defined relative to a known baseline policy whose outcomes are counterfactual and therefore unobserved. Thus, the counterfactual outcomes of the baseline policy must be estimated and those (uncertain) estimates must be used to safely optimize the objective. We address this estimation problem by using conformal prediction to construct valid uncertainty intervals for counterfactual baseline outcomes, and we show how these intervals can be integrated into safe Bayesian optimization to ensure that constraint violations occur at or below a user-specified rate. We also show how to adapt these conformal estimates to different kinds of covariate shift. We provide a safety proof, experimental evidence, and a sensitivity analysis.

</details>

### [69] [Decision Protocols in Multi-Agent Large Language Model Conversations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05477v1)
*Lars Benedikt Kaesberg*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 研究多agent LLM对话中的决策协议，通用agent协作方法。

TL;DR: 本论文提出了MALLM框架，系统评估了投票、共识和裁判三种决策协议在不同类型任务上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLMs扩展面临收益递减和高成本，MAS通过分配任务可降低训练成本但增加测试时间，而决策协议作为关键组件缺乏系统研究。

Method: 构建MALLM框架，实现投票、共识和裁判三种决策协议，在知识型和逻辑型多个数据集上模拟多智能体讨论并评估其影响。

Result: 共识协议在知识密集型任务中表现更优，投票和裁判协议在逻辑任务中更有效；增加响应多样性提升决策质量，而信息访问变化影响较小。

Conclusion: 不同决策协议适用于不同任务类型，为多智能体系统的设计提供了指导，并揭示了响应多样性的重要性。

中文摘要：提升大型语言模型（LLMs）的任务性能至关重要，然而扩展这些模型面临着收益递减和高成本等重大挑战。多智能体系统（MAS）通过将任务分配给专门的智能体来提升整体任务性能，提供了一种有前景的解决方案。这可以降低训练成本，但代价是由于讨论和决策过程导致测试时间增加。决策协议是MAS的关键组成部分，因为它规定了多个智能体如何协作以生成最终解决方案。本文引入了多智能体LLM（MALLM）框架，该框架实现并评估了各种决策协议，即投票、共识和裁判决策机制，以模拟用于对话式任务解决的多智能体讨论。与以往使用单一决策协议或在有限数据集上进行测试的工作不同，本研究系统地考察了它们在多种任务上的影响，这些任务涵盖基于知识的数据集（MMLU、MMLU-Pro、GPQA）和基于逻辑的数据集（StrategyQA、MuSR、Math-lvl-5、SQuAD 2.0）。结果表明，共识协议在知识密集型领域表现优异，而投票和裁判协议在基于逻辑的任务中更为有效。通过独立解决方案生成来增加响应多样性可以提高决策质量，而决策过程中信息访问的变化影响微乎其微。

Original abstract: Improving the task performance of Large Language Models (LLMs) is essential, yet scaling these models faces significant challenges such as diminishing returns and high costs. Multi-Agent Systems (MAS) offer a promising solution by distributing tasks among specialized agents to improve the overall task performance. This can reduce training costs at the expense of increased test time due to the discussion and decision-making process. The decision protocol is a critical component of MAS because it specifies how multiple agents collaborate to create a final solution. This thesis introduces the Multi-Agent LLM (MALLM) framework, which implements and evaluates various decision protocols, namely voting, consensus, and judge decision mechanisms, to simulate multi-agent discussions for conversational task solving. Unlike previous work that used a single decision protocol or tested them on limited datasets, this study systematically examines their impact on a diverse set of tasks, ranging from knowledge-based datasets (MMLU, MMLU-Pro, GPQA) and logic-based datasets (StrategyQA, MuSR, Math-lvl-5, SQuAD 2.0). The results indicate that consensus protocols excel in knowledge-intensive domains while voting and judge protocols are more effective for logic-based tasks. Increasing response diversity through independent solution generation improves decision quality, while changes in information access during the decision process have minimal impact.

</details>


### [70] [Collective Intelligence with Foundation Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07729v1)
*J. de Curtò,I. de Zarzà*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent协作框架，包含生成、批评、聚合，通用agent方法。

TL;DR: 异质多智能体框架通过模型多样性显著提升推理准确率和逐步推理质量，优于同质和单个模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基础模型规模增长，需要协调多个模型实现更安全、更可靠的AI协作推理系统。

Method: 提出多智能体框架（求解器、批评者、聚合者、评分模块），在多个学科基准上通过消融研究比较四种配置（单个、同质框架、冗余同质、异质）。

Result: 异质配置逐步准确率0.64，比单个模型提升2.3倍，方差更小，逐步推理质量仅随模型多样性显著提升。

Conclusion: 模型异质性是性能提升的关键，支持透明、可审计、高置信度的跨领域决策。

中文摘要：随着基础模型在规模和多样性上的增长，将多个模型协调成协作推理系统为更安全、更可靠的AI提供了一条路径。本章提出了一个多智能体框架，其中求解器模型生成独立草稿，每个草稿都经过批评智能体的结构化批评和修订，然后聚合智能体综合出最终共识解决方案。评分模块在所有智能体上提供语义、数值和过程评估。通过在涵盖微积分、物理、化学、生物、经济、优化、统计和数学的基准上进行消融研究，我们分离了框架架构与模型多样性的贡献。我们比较了四种配置：（1）单个基线，（2）使用一个共享模型的同质框架，（3）使用同一模型的多个实例的冗余同质求解器，以及（4）具有多样化专业模型的异质框架。结果表明，虽然框架结构和冗余采样带来适度改进，但模型异质性是驱动显著性能提升的关键因素。异质配置在逐步准确率上取得了优越性能（0.64对比单个模型的0.54；比同质配置提升2.3倍），并且在不同类别和难度水平上方差更小。逐步推理质量（中间步骤的正确性，不仅仅是最终答案）仅在模型多样性下显著提高，表明异质智能体提供了互补的错误检测和推理细化，这对于可解释性和可审计性至关重要。我们讨论了架构原则、评估方法以及对全球应用AI的影响，展示了异质多智能体协调如何支持跨科学和工业领域的透明、可审计、高置信度决策。

Original abstract: As foundation models grow in scale and diversity, coordinating multiple models into cooperative reasoning systems offers a path toward safer, more reliable AI. This chapter presents a multi-agent framework where solver models generate independent drafts, each undergoes structured critique and revision by a critic agent, and an aggregator agent synthesizes a final consensus solution. A scoring module provides semantic, numerical, and procedural evaluation across all agents. Through ablation studies on a benchmark spanning calculus, physics, chemistry, biology, economics, optimization, statistics, and mathematics, we isolate the contributions of framework architecture versus model diversity. We compare four configurations: (1) Individual Baseline, (2) Homogeneous Framework using one shared model, (3) Redundant Homogeneous Solvers using multiple instances of the same model, and (4) Heterogeneous Framework with diverse specialized models. Results show that while framework structure and redundant sampling yield modest gains, model heterogeneity is the critical factor driving substantial performance improvements. The heterogeneous configuration achieves superior step-wise accuracy (0.64 vs. 0.54 for individual models; 2.3x improvement over homogeneous configurations) with reduced variance across categories and difficulty levels. Step-wise reasoning quality (correctness of intermediate steps, not just final answers) improves dramatically only with model diversity, showing that heterogeneous agents provide complementary error detection and reasoning refinement essential for explainability and auditability. We discuss architectural principles, evaluation methodology, and implications for Global Applied AI, showing how heterogeneous multi-agent coordination supports transparent, auditable, high-confidence decision-making across scientific and industrial domains.

</details>

### [71] [To Retain or to Adapt? Generalizing Continual Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05609v1)
*Giulia Lanzillotta,Mandana Samiei,Doina Precup,Razvan Pascanu,Claire Vernade*

Main category: stat.ML

Selection reason: 持续学习理论，可迁移至agent的持续学习和适应。

TL;DR: 挑战持续学习中的保留知识假设，提出转移效率和关键任务持续时间概念，并引入预测性持续学习算法，在非平稳环境下优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战持续学习中以保留所有知识为前提的默认假设，指出在非平稳环境中优先保留会阻碍实时适应，并形式化CL为在线优化问题。

Method: 引入转移效率度量不稳定性和瞬态误差之间的张力，推导关键任务持续时间闭式阈值；提出预测性持续学习算法，基于动态未来任务模型优化期望性能。

Result: 在持续图像分类和强化学习基准上验证理论预测；窗口算法在受控分布漂移下优于JTL和ITL。

Conclusion: JTL只是更广泛目标族的一个实例，预测性持续学习能通过显式建模未来任务分布实现更优的在线适应。

中文摘要：持续学习（CL）文献长期以来一直以缓解灾难性遗忘为目标。这一目标基于一个普遍且常常未明确说明的假设：终身学习者应该近似联合任务学习（JTL）的解决方案，并保留所有先前获得的知识。我们挑战这种以保留为中心的前提，认为在非平稳环境中，优先考虑保留会阻碍实时适应。将焦点转移到平均终身误差（ALE）上，我们将CL形式化为一个在线优化问题，受环境动态和学习动态之间的相互作用支配。我们引入转移效率作为衡量不稳定性（从冲突的过去经验中继承的偏差）和瞬态误差（从头学习新任务的优化成本）之间张力的定量度量。在温和的收敛条件下，适用于线性模型和神经网络模型，这种分解产生了一个关键任务持续时间：一个闭式阈值，超过该阈值，每当保留导致正平稳偏差时，历史知识就从热启动优势转变为优化负债。我们在持续图像分类和强化学习基准上验证了这些理论预测。最后，通过将持续学习与可预测序列的在线学习框架联系起来，我们表明JTL只是一个更广泛目标族的一个实例，并提出了一类新的通用持续学习算法，我们称之为预测性持续学习。预测性CL算法在显式、动态更新的未来任务模型下优化预期未来性能。作为概念验证，我们分析了一个窗口算法，该算法在JTL和独立任务学习（ITL）之间进行插值，在受控分布漂移下优于两者。

Original abstract: The Continual Learning (CL) literature has long been driven by the goal of mitigating catastrophic forgetting. This objective rests on a pervasive, often unstated assumption: that a lifelong learner should approximate the Joint-Task Learning (JTL) solution and retain all previously acquired knowledge. We challenge this retention-centered premise, arguing that in non-stationary environments prioritizing retention can impede real-time adaptation. Shifting the focus to the Average Lifelong Error (ALE), we formalize CL as an online optimization problem governed by the interaction between environmental and learning dynamics. We introduce Transfer Efficiency as a quantitative measure of the tension between Instability, the bias inherited from conflicting past experience, and Transient Error, the optimization cost of learning new tasks from scratch. Under mild convergence conditions, holding across linear and neural network models, this decomposition yields a Critical Task Duration: a closed-form threshold beyond which historical knowledge transitions from a warm-start advantage to an optimization liability whenever retention induces a positive stationary bias. We validate these theoretical predictions on continual image classification and reinforcement learning benchmarks. Finally, by connecting continual learning to the online learning framework of predictable sequences, we show that JTL is only one instance of a broader family of objectives, and we propose a new general class of continual learning algorithms, which we call Predictive Continual Learning. Predictive CL algorithms optimize expected future performance under an explicit, dynamically updated model of future tasks. As a proof of concept, we analyze a Window algorithm that interpolates between JTL and Independent-Task Learning (ITL), outperforming both under controlled distributional drift.

</details>

# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [72] [Hierarchical Evidence-Driven Reasoning for Long Document Understanding](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04625v1)
*Junyu Xiong,Yonghui Wang,Rongjian Gu,Chenyu Liu,Bing Yin,Wengang Zhou,Houqiang Li*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 提出HIEVI-RAG框架，包含层次分解、多页验证agent（EVIAGENT）和迭代生成，属于通用agent推理与检索方法。

TL;DR: 提出HIEVI-RAG，一种分层证据驱动的多模态RAG框架，通过四阶段流水线解决干扰页面和级联错误问题，在四个基准上平均准确率提升8.05%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG面临两个挑战：标准检索器获取主题重叠但无答案的干扰页面；刚性单次流水线依赖初始检索成功，遗漏核心证据导致级联错误。

Method: HIEVI-RAG包含四阶段：层次化问题分解、粗粒度视觉页面检索、基于EVIAGENT（用GRPO训练的多页面验证器）的细粒度验证、记忆引导的迭代生成。

Result: 在四个基准上，HIEVI-RAG显著优于现有开源基线，平均准确率超过最强基线8.05%。

Conclusion: HIEVI-RAG通过分层证据驱动方法有效缓解了干扰和级联错误，展现了强大效能与协同作用。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）通过利用检索机制将输入图像限制为高度精选的子集，从而简化了长文档理解。然而，现有的多模态RAG流水线主要面临两个关键挑战：首先，标准的语义相似性检索器经常获取主题重叠但缺乏答案的干扰页面，从而误导下游生成；其次，刚性的单次通过流水线严重依赖于初始检索成功，任何核心证据的遗漏都不可避免地导致级联错误。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了HIEVI-RAG，一种用于封闭域文档理解的分层、证据驱动的多模态RAG框架。HIEVI-RAG系统地将复杂查询分解为协作的四阶段流水线：（1）层次化问题分解，将多跳根查询分解为原子子问题；（2）粗粒度视觉页面检索，利用多模态检索器基于语义相似性获取候选页面；（3）通过EVIAGENT进行细粒度页面验证，EVIAGENT是一种专门的多页面验证器，使用GRPO进行训练，以在多图像块上执行跨页面推理；（4）记忆引导的迭代生成，利用累积的子问题上下文在优先序列上执行多轮动态推理。在四个基准上的广泛评估表明了我们框架的强大效能和协同作用，其显著优于现有的开源基线，并且平均准确率比最强报告的基线高出8.05%。

Original abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) streamlines long-document understanding by leveraging retrieval mechanisms to restrict input images to a highly curated subset. However, existing multimodal RAG pipelines primarily face two critical challenges: first, standard semantic similarity retrievers frequently fetch topically overlapping yet answer-void distractor pages that mislead downstream generation; second, rigid single-pass pipelines heavily depend on initial retrieval success, where any omission of core evidence inevitably causes cascading errors. To address these challenges, we introduce HIEVI-RAG, a hierarchical, evidence-driven multimodal RAG framework for closed-domain document understanding. HIEVI-RAG systematically factorizes complex queries into a cooperative four-stage pipeline: (1) hierarchical question decomposition to break multi-hop root queries into atomic child questions; (2) coarse visual page retrieval leveraging a multimodal retriever to fetch candidate pages based on semantic similarity; (3) fine-grained page verification via EVIAGENT, a specialized multi-page verifier trained with GRPO to execute cross-page reasoning over multi-image blocks; and (4) memory-guided iterative generation that leverages accumulated sub-question context to execute multi-round, dynamic reasoning over the prioritized sequence. Extensive evaluations across four benchmarks demonstrate the robust efficacy and synergy of our framework, which significantly outperforms existing open-source baselines and exceeds the strongest reported baseline by an average of 8.05% in accuracy.

</details>


### [73] [CanvasAgent: Enabling Complex Image Creation and Editing via Visual Tool Orchestration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05465v1)

Motivation: 现有多模态工具智能体主要针对感知和搜索优化，缺乏用于复杂图像创建的大规模可执行轨迹监督。

Original abstract: Complex image creation and editing often require more than a single generation or editing model. A user request may involve synthesizing images, localizing objects, segmenting regions, editing selected content, compositing intermediate assets, reading text, and enhancing the final result. Such tasks shift multimodal agents from perception-augmented reasoning to manipulation-centered visual creation, where tools must actively transform visual states rather than merely inspect them. However, existing multimodal tool-use agents are mostly optimized for perception, search, or domain-specific editing, and lack large-scale supervision for executable image-creation trajectories. In this paper, we introduce CanvasCraft, a large-scale multimodal tool-use dataset for complex image creation and editing, and \textbf{CanvasAgent}, a tool-augmented multimodal agent that learns to orchestrate heterogeneous visual tools through multi-turn interaction. CanvasCraft contains 140K fully annotated executable trajectories and 10K
  RL task specifications. CanvasAgent is first trained with SFT to learn executable reasoning-action trajectories, and is then optimized with GRPO using a hybrid reward that combines outcome- and process-level signals. During rollout, CanvasAgent inspects intermediate results, tracks visual assets, and adapts tool decisions to the evolving visual state. Experiments evaluate both final image quality and trajectory behavior, demonstrating the effectiveness of CanvasAgent and the proposed dataset for complex multi-tool image creation workflows.

### [74] [ReflectWorld-MM: An Entity-Oriented Multimodal Memory System for Open-Ended Video Streams](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09759v2)
*Xiaokang Ma,Yifan Sun,Zhihong Jin,Jie Gu,Yudong Luo,Shenyi Shao,Chu Tang,Jingmin Chen,Li Pu*

TL;DR: 提出了面向实体的多模态记忆系统 ReflectWorld-MM，在六个基准上达到最佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有系统将记忆限制在模型上下文或扁平特征存储中，且围绕帧而非实体组织，导致无法追踪持续出现的实体并处理无界视频流。

Method: 提出三部分结构：感知前端（将视听流转化为实体观察）、基于人类记忆理论的分层长期记忆（多尺度情景记忆、实体中心语义记忆、程序记忆）以及面向实际部署的完整实现。

Result: 在六个长视频和终身记忆基准上均取得最高准确率，超越现有记忆智能体和前沿模型。

Conclusion: 实体导向的分层记忆设计能有效支持开放视频流中持续学习与推理，为构建终身记忆助手提供新方案。

中文摘要：建立能够持续观察世界、记住所见内容并推理累积经验的助手是一个长期目标，最近，配备长期视频流记忆的多模态智能体引起了越来越多的兴趣。不幸的是，现有系统要么将记忆保留在模型上下文中，要么存放在扁平的特征存储中，并且围绕帧而非流真正关注的持久实体来组织记忆，这将其限制在有界视频中，并削弱了其追踪随时间重复出现的对象的能力。在本文中，我们提出了 ReflectWorld-MM，一种面向实体的开放视频流多模态记忆系统。它由三部分组成。第一部分是一个感知前端，它将视听流在有界短期记忆下转化为实体解析的观察。第二部分是基于人类记忆理论的分层长期记忆，它结合了多尺度情景记忆、演化的实体中心语义记忆和程序记忆。第三部分是一个完整的实现，为真实世界操作而构建，可以摄取任意流并插入现成的智能体。在六个长视频和终身记忆基准测试中，ReflectWorld-MM 在所有六个基准测试中均达到最佳准确率，优于强大的记忆智能体和前沿模型。

Original abstract: Building assistants that can continually watch the world, remember what they see, and reason over their accumulated experience is a long-standing goal, and recently multimodal agents equipped with long-term memory over video streams have attracted increasing interest. Unfortunately, existing systems either keep their memory inside the model context or in a flat feature store, and organize it around frames rather than around the persistent entities a stream is really about, which confines them to bounded videos and weakens their ability to track who and what reappears over time. In this paper, we propose ReflectWorld-MM, an entity-oriented multimodal memory system for open-ended video streams. It consists of three parts. The first is a perception front-end that turns an audiovisual stream into entity-resolved observations under a bounded short-term memory. The second is a hierarchical long-term memory, grounded in human memory theory, that couples a multi-scale episodic memory, an evolving entity-centric semantic memory, and a procedural memory. The third is a complete realization, built for real-world operation, that ingests arbitrary streams and plugs into off-the-shelf assistants. Across six long-video and lifelong-memory benchmarks, ReflectWorld-MM achieves the best accuracy on all six, outperforming strong memory agents and a frontier model.

### [75] [Search Beyond What Can Be Taught: Evolving the Knowledge Boundary in Agentic Visual Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05382v3)
*Haozhe Wang,Weijia Feng,Jinpeng Yu,Che Liu,Ping Nie,Fangzhen Lin,Jiaming Liu,Ruihua Huang,Jimmy Lin,Wenhu Chen,Cong Wei*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 视觉生成agent的知识边界方法，teach-then-search框架可迁移至agent工具使用。

TL;DR: 本文指出视觉生成器存在世界知识瓶颈，构建了SearchGen-20K等基准测试，发现现有生成器得分很低；提出“先教后搜索”协同训练框架可有效利用搜索工具改进生成，实现单调提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视觉生成器对未知内容会错误生成（幻觉），现有基准无法发现该问题，且简单搜索会引入噪声，因此需要更好的知识补充机制。

Method: 提出SearchGen-20K和SearchGen-Bench基准，包括多种失败类别；并采用“先教后搜索”协同训练框架，让生成器先学习内部化知识，再通过搜索获取外部知识，迭代提升。

Result: 在SearchGen-Bench上，前沿生成器得分仅21-28；协同训练框架产生单调改进，验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过可发现的生成器知识边界和协同训练，能够实现工具增强的视觉生成，满足基于世界知识的请求，并为递归自我改进提供基础。

中文摘要：视觉生成器擅长于渲染，但它们自信地编造它们不知道的内容。用户请求是无界的、不断演化的，并且深度长尾：新角色、流行实体、截止日期后的事件等等。这种世界知识瓶颈是结构性的：生成器在固定的语料库上训练，但视觉世界是开放式的。我们构建了SearchGen-20K和SearchGen-Bench，包含20,839个提示，涵盖十二个失败类别和二十二个领域，并配有一个预执行的多模态SearchGen-Corpus-1M，以支持离线、可重复的研究。在SearchGen-Bench上，前沿开放生成器得分仅为21到28分（满分100分），这是现有基准无法发现的40分崩塌。自然的补救措施是使用搜索工具，实现智能体视觉生成。然而，我们发现简单的搜索会失败：它不加区分地检索，将噪声注入生成器已经能够处理的提示中。我们将根本原因追溯到生成器特定的、不断演变的知识边界：即生成器通过训练可以内化的内容与必须保留在外部上下文中的内容之间的分界线。尽管这个边界难以预先指定，但我们表明它可以通过“先教后搜索”的协同训练框架来发现。即使是这个协同训练配方的最小版本也能产生单调改进，为视觉生成中的递归自我改进奠定了基础，从而能够满足基于世界知识的请求。我们发布了完整的数据集、协同训练语料库和搜索语料库，作为一个可重放的工具，用于工具增强的、基于世界知识的视觉生成。

Original abstract: Visual generators excel at rendering, but they confidently fabricate what they do not know. User requests are unbounded, evolving, and deeply long-tailed: new characters, trending entities, post-cutoff events, and more. This world-knowledge bottleneck is structural: generators are trained on fixed corpora, but the visual world is open-ended. We construct SearchGen-20K and SearchGen-Bench, with 20,839 prompts spanning twelve failure categories and twenty-two domains, paired with a pre-executed multimodal SearchGen-Corpus-1M to support offline, reproducible research. On SearchGen-Bench, frontier open generators score only 21 to 28 out of 100, a 40-point collapse invisible to existing benchmarks. The natural remedy is to employ search tools, enabling agentic visual generation. However, we find that naive search fails: it retrieves indiscriminately, injecting noise into prompts the generator already handles. We trace the root cause to a generator-specific, evolving knowledge boundary: the divide between what a generator can internalize through training and what must remain in external context. Although this boundary is hard to specify in advance, we show that it is discoverable through a teach-then-search co-training framework. Even a minimal version of this co-training recipe produces monotonic improvement, laying the foundation for recursive self-improvement in visual generation that can meet world-knowledge-grounded requests. We release the full dataset, co-training corpus, and search corpus as a replayable harness for tool-augmented, world-knowledge-grounded visual generation.

### [76] [EEG-SpikeAgent: Agentic Closed-Loop Program Synthesis for Automated EEG Spike Detection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04558v1)
*Sonali Santhosh,Kelly Shuhong Yu,Eugene Chang,Jonathan Kim,Kie Shidara,Danilo Bernardo*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出EEG-SpikeAgent，使用LLM agentic系统进行信号处理特征的程序合成与迭代优化，属于coding agent方法，可迁移至自动代码优化。

TL;DR: 提出EEG-SpikeAgent，利用LLM代理迭代生成可解释的EEG特征，在尖峰检测任务上达到高AUC且保持代码可审计性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习方法在EEG尖峰检测中准确性高但缺乏可解释性，临床场景需要透明、可审查的决策过程。

Method: 设计闭环程序合成框架，LLM代理迭代生成EEG信号处理特征模块，执行后提取表格特征，通过分类器评估并反馈诊断信息优化特征集。

Result: 在VEPISET数据集上，AUC达0.935，平衡准确率0.699，F1 0.557，灵敏度0.401，特异度0.996；高灵敏度设置下精度0.470，特异度0.900；伪影感知特征提升性能。

Conclusion: LLM驱动的程序合成能有效自动化EEG特征工程，生成可解释、可审计的代码级特征，支持临床和方法学审查。

中文摘要：自动检测头皮脑电图（EEG）中的发作间期癫痫样放电在临床上具有重要意义，但近期高性能的深度学习模型常常以牺牲可解释性为代价来提高准确性。我们介绍EEG-SpikeAgent，一种闭环程序合成框架，它使用大型语言模型（LLM）代理系统来生成用于头皮脑电尖峰检测的信号处理特征。该系统迭代地每次提出一个确定性EEG特征模块，在EEG上执行生成的代码以生成表格特征，通过表格分类器评估性能，汇总运行级指标，并将结构化诊断反馈回模型以进行改进。经过多次迭代，EEG-SpikeAgent根据模型性能提出并精炼候选信号特征和决策规则。我们在VEPISET数据集上评估了EEG-SpikeAgent，该数据集是一个包含29个通道、4秒时长的公开数据集，包含2,516个含放电的epoch和22,933个不含放电的epoch。在五折交叉验证中，使用梯度提升树分类器，代理生成的特征在默认操作点下实现了0.935的受试者工作特征曲线下面积、0.699的平衡准确率、0.557的F1分数、0.401的灵敏度和0.996的特异度。在灵敏度为0.80的操作点下，平均精确度为0.470，平均特异度为0.900。考虑伪影的特征生成相比仅尖峰特征搜索提高了平衡准确率和F1分数。这些结果表明，基于LLM的程序合成可以以可审计和可检查的代码驱动方式自动化EEG特征工程，便于临床和方法学审查。

Original abstract: Automated detection of interictal epileptiform discharges in scalp electroencephalography (EEG) is clinically important, but recent high-performing deep-learning models often trade interpretability for accuracy. We introduce EEG-SpikeAgent, a closed-loop program-synthesis framework that uses a large language model (LLM) agentic system to generate signal-processing features for spike detection in scalp EEG. The system iteratively proposes one deterministic EEG feature module at a time, executes the resulting code on EEG to generate tabular features, evaluates performance via a tabular classifier, summarizes run-level metrics, and feeds structured diagnostics back to the model for refinement. Across iterations, EEG-SpikeAgent proposes and refines candidate signal features and decision rules informed by model performance. We evaluated EEG-SpikeAgent on VEPISET, a public 29-channel dataset of 4-second epochs containing 2,516 discharge-containing and 22,933 non-discharge epochs. Across five-fold cross-validation with a gradient-boosted tree classifier, agent-generated features achieved an area under the receiver operating characteristic curve of 0.935, balanced accuracy of 0.699, F1 score of 0.557, sensitivity of 0.401, and specificity of 0.996 at the default operating point. At an operating point with sensitivity 0.80, mean precision was 0.470 and mean specificity was 0.900. Artifact-aware feature generation improved balanced accuracy and F1 score over spike-only feature search. These results indicate that LLM-based program synthesis can automate EEG feature engineering in auditable and inspectable code-driven manner for clinical and methodological review.

### [77] [ToolFailBench: Diagnosing Tool-Use Failures in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04686v1)
*Harsh Soni*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出ToolFailBench基准，用于诊断语言模型工具调用中的四种失败模式，发现最佳模型清洁使用率仅86.33%，且不同模型失败模式差异显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合基准分数无法揭示工具使用的失败细节，导致不同失败模式（如不调工具、忽略结果）在最终准确率上表现相似。

Method: 构建包含1000个任务的ToolFailBench，涵盖金融、医疗、法律等领域的工具必需任务和控制任务，通过规则分类器和两个LLM评判者的多数投票标注四种失败类型。

Result: 19个主流模型中最佳Clean Tool-Use Rate为86.33%，Llama-3.1模型表现出Always-Call模式，且相同参数规模下Llama-3.1-70B与Qwen2.5-72B控制任务准确率相差89个百分点。

Conclusion: 工具使用评估应同时关注是否调用工具、是否正确使用工具输出以及是否在不必要时避免调用工具。

中文摘要：工具调用是现代语言模型智能体的核心，但聚合基准分数常常掩盖了工具使用失败的地方。从不调用所需工具的模型与调用工具但忽略结果的模型在最终任务准确率上可能看起来相似。我们引入了ToolFailBench，这是一个诊断基准，用于衡量在金融、医疗、法律、网络安全和房地产领域1000个任务中的工具使用失败情况。需要工具的任务会返回模型无法猜测的值，迫使模型信任工具，而控制任务则附加相同的工具但应直接回答。我们使用规则分类器和两个LLM评判者（通过多数投票聚合）为每个轨迹标注工具跳过、忽略结果、输出捏造和不必要的工具使用。在19个主流模型中，最佳模型达到了86.33%的清洁工具使用率，表明忠实的工具使用尚未饱和。更重要的是，具有相似聚合分数的模型以不同方式失败：大多数在无工具控制任务上保持纪律，而Llama-3.1模型表现出始终调用的模式，并且在相同参数规模下，Llama-3.1-70B和Qwen2.5-72B在控制任务准确率上相差89个百分点。工具使用评估不仅应衡量智能体是否调用工具，还应衡量它们是否正确使用工具输出并在不需要时避免使用工具。

Original abstract: Tool calling is central to modern language model agents, but aggregate benchmark scores often hide where tool use fails. A model that never calls a needed tool and a model that calls the tool but ignores the result can look similar under final task accuracy. We introduce ToolFailBench, a diagnostic benchmark for measuring tool-use failures across 1,000 tasks in finance, medicine, law, cybersecurity, and real estate. Tool-required tasks return values the model wouldn't guess, forcing it to trust the tool while control tasks attach the same tools but should be answered directly. We label each trace with Tool-Skip, Result-Ignore, Output-Fabrication, and Unnecessary-Tool-Use, using a rule classifier and two LLM judges aggregated by majority vote. Across 19 headline models, the best reaches 86.33% Clean Tool-Use Rate, showing that faithful tool use is not saturated. More importantly, models with similar aggregate scores fail in different ways: most stay disciplined on no-tool controls, while Llama-3.1 models show an Always-Call pattern, and at the same parameter scale Llama-3.1-70B and Qwen2.5-72B differ by 89 percentage points on control-task accuracy. Tool-use evaluation should measure not only whether agents call tools, but whether they use tool outputs correctly and avoid tools when none is needed.

</details>

### [78] [Evaluating calibrated refusal and safe usefulness in dual-use biology settings](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05462v1)
*Edwin H. Wintermute,Harmon Bhasin,Christina M. Agapakis,Dianzhuo Wang,Evan Seeyave,Arjun Banerjee,Daniel Fulop,Matthew C. Watson,Adam J. Meyer,Sandrine Boissel,Jens H. Kuhn,Rishi Jain,Noah D. Taylor,Helena Shomar,Patrick M. Boyle,Kenny Workman*

TL;DR: 提出了BioSecBench-Refusal基准测试，用于评估AI智能体在生物研究任务中的拒绝行为，发现许多模型对合法任务的拒绝率高于对危险任务的拒绝率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI智能体在生命科学中的应用可能被滥用，需要基准测试来识别风险和评估拒绝行为。

Method: 构建包含61个常规任务和46个红队任务的基准测试，在16种模型-工具配置上测试拒绝率。

Result: 常规任务拒绝率7%-74%，红队任务拒绝率1%-62%，许多配置对常规任务拒绝率更高；拒绝主要由API过滤器触发，但模型推理可提升威胁识别。

Conclusion: BioSecBench-Refusal有助于模型开发者校准生物技术研发中的能力与谨慎度。

中文摘要：随着AI智能体被整合到生命科学工作流程中，加速发现的能力也可能被滥用。我们提出了BioSecBench-Refusal，这是一个用于生物研究任务的风险识别和拒绝行为的基准测试。该基准测试将61个常规任务（源自已发表文献的合法分析）与46个红队任务（类似真实研究但隐藏生物安全危害的虚构场景）配对。在16种模型-工具配置中，常规任务的拒绝率从7%到74%不等，红队任务的拒绝率从1%到62%不等，许多配置对合法常规工作的拒绝率与对隐藏危害的拒绝率相当或更高。拒绝最常由在智能体推理之前应用的提供商API过滤器触发。然而，给予推理空间的模型显示出识别更多真实威胁的潜力。我们发布BioSecBench-Refusal作为模型开发者校准能力与谨慎度的工具，用于智能生物技术研发。

Original abstract: As AI agents are incorporated into life science workflows, the capabilities that speed discovery might also enable misuse. We present BioSecBench-Refusal, a benchmark for risk identification and refusal behavior for biological research tasks. The benchmark pairs 61 Routine tasks, legitimate analyses adapted from the published literature, with 46 Red-Team tasks, fictional scenarios that resemble real research but conceal a biosecurity hazard. Across 16 model-harness configurations, refusal rates ranged from 7\% to 74\% on Routine tasks and 1\% to 62\% on Red-Team tasks, with many configurations refusing legitimate Routine work at comparable or higher rates than concealed hazards. Refusals were most often triggered by provider API filters applied prior to agentic reasoning. However, models given room to reason showed the potential to identify more real threats. We release BioSecBench-Refusal as a tool for model developers to calibrate capability and caution for agentic biotech R\&D.

### [79] [RustMizan: A Compilable, Contamination-Aware Benchmarking Framework for Rust Vulnerabilities](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04729v1)
*Tarek Elsayed,Shiping Yang,Eunsong Koh,Sanika Goyal,Vincent Huang,Paul Ngo,Nathan Young,Mohammad Omidvar Tehrani,Alvyn Kang,Arnell Kang,Zeyu Chen,Angélica Moreira,Xuan Feng,Angel X. Chang,Nick Sumner,Steven Y. Ko*

TL;DR: RustMizan是一个针对Rust漏洞分析的新型基准测试框架，通过可编译代码变体和突变测试，评估LLM智能体的漏洞检测能力，发现行级定位准确率低且易受对抗性影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建包含crate、文件和函数级别的可编译代码变体数据集，提供二元漏洞检测、CWE分类及函数级和行级定位注释；并采用配对突变框架生成保持语义的代码突变体进行污染测试和鲁棒性探测。

中文摘要：LLM智能体越来越多地应用于漏洞分析，但现有的基准测试没有跟上。它们通常依赖于小的不可编译的代码片段，侧重于二元分类（有漏洞或没有），并且没有考虑公开数据集可能成为模型训练语料库的风险。我们引入了RustMizan，一个针对Rust漏洞分析的基准测试框架，填补了这些空白。RustMizan包含在crate、文件和函数级别的可编译代码变体，并带有二元漏洞检测、CWE分类以及函数级和行级定位的注释。一个配对的突变框架产生保持语义的代码突变体，用于污染测试和鲁棒性探测。在具有命令行访问权限的智能体设置中，跨越四个前沿模型，二元分类在56-65%范围内，但行定位F1接近20%，对抗性线索使行F1下降约27%。

Original abstract: LLM agents are increasingly applied to vulnerability analysis, but existing benchmarks have not kept pace. They typically rely on small non-compilable snippets, focus on binary classification (vulnerable or not), and do not account for the risk that publicly-released datasets are part of model training corpora. We introduce RustMizan, a benchmarking framework for Rust vulnerability analysis that addresses these gaps. RustMizan contains compilable code variants at the crate, file, and function levels, with annotations for binary vulnerability detection, CWE classification, and function- and line-level localization. A paired mutation framework produces semantics-preserving code mutants for contamination testing and robustness probing. Across four frontier models in an agentic setup with command-line access, binary classification sits in the 56-65% range, but line localization F1 stays near 20%, and adversarial cues drop line F1 by about 27%.

### [80] [ShadowProbe: Language-Extensible Detection of Hidden Algorithmic Complexity Vulnerabilities](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05474v1)
*Yuanmin Xie,Xiangfan Wu,Wenhao Wu,Lingyun Ying,Puzhuo Liu,Haipeng Qu,Zhongyuan Chen,Min Zhou,Chengnian Sun*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出ShadowProbe框架，通过静态分析、上下文重构和LLM辅助测试生成，高效发现由于影子复杂度引起的算法复杂度漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ACV检测器语言特定、需手动构建且依赖运行时插桩，未能充分挖掘标准库中隐藏的影子复杂度漏洞。

Method: 采用多阶段流水线：静态筛选候选函数、从项目符号重构最小执行上下文、合成大小可控输入、基于执行时间统计验证。

Result: 在WISE基准上效率优于现有方法，并在CPython、JDK等大型系统中发现多个此前未知的ACVs，获维护者确认。

Conclusion: ShadowProbe能有效且可扩展地识别跨语言真实代码库中的隐藏算法风险。

中文摘要：算法复杂度漏洞（ACVs）是指当对抗性输入触发最坏情况执行行为时，导致严重性能下降或拒绝服务条件的情况。一个关键但未充分探索的来源是影子复杂度：隐藏在看似良性的标准库API内部的非平凡计算成本。由于这些成本在调用点不可见，攻击者可以利用它们诱发意外的超线性运行时行为。现有的ACV检测器通常依赖于模糊测试、符号执行或混合分析，但它们通常是特定于语言的，需要大量手动工作来构建测试框架，并且依赖于繁重的运行时插桩。我们提出ShadowProbe，一个可扩展且语言无关的框架，通过轻量级静态分析、自动重构执行上下文和大语言模型（LLM）辅助的测试生成来发现ACVs。ShadowProbe使用结构化的多阶段流水线：它通过影子复杂度信号静态筛选候选函数，从项目级符号重构最小可执行上下文，并合成大小可控的输入以探查最坏情况行为。然后，它使用执行时间测量和稳健的统计增长推断来验证候选者，将真正的算法爆炸与运行时噪声（如垃圾回收和JIT编译效应）分离。我们在WISE基准上评估ShadowProbe，它持续提高了分析效率。我们进一步将其应用于大规模系统，包括CPython、JDK、Zig、Rustc和vLLM，发现了许多以前未知的ACVs，其中许多已被维护者确认并部分修复。这些结果表明ShadowProbe能够在多样化的真实代码库中识别隐藏的算法风险。

Original abstract: Algorithmic Complexity Vulnerabilities (ACVs) arise when adversarial inputs trigger worst-case execution behavior, causing severe performance degradation or Denial-of-Service conditions. A key but underexplored source is shadow complexity: non-trivial computational costs hidden inside seemingly benign standard library APIs. Because these costs are invisible at call sites, attackers can exploit them to induce unexpected superlinear runtime behavior. Existing ACV detectors often rely on fuzzing, symbolic execution, or hybrid analysis, but they are usually language-specific, require substantial manual effort to construct harnesses, and depend on heavy runtime instrumentation.
  We present ShadowProbe, a scalable and language-extensible framework for discovering ACVs through lightweight static analysis, automated reconstruction of execution contexts, and Large Language Model (LLM) assisted test generation. ShadowProbe uses a structured multi-stage pipeline: it statically screens for candidate functions guided by shadow-complexity signals, reconstructs minimal executable contexts from project-level symbols, and synthesizes size-controlled inputs to probe worst-case behavior. It then validates candidates using execution-time measurements and robust statistical growth inference, separating true algorithmic blowups from runtime noise such as garbage collection and JIT compilation effects.
  We evaluate ShadowProbe on the WISE benchmark, where it consistently improves analysis efficiency over existing approaches. We further apply it to large-scale systems including CPython, the JDK, Zig, Rustc, and vLLM, uncovering many previously unknown ACVs, many of which have been confirmed and partially remediated by maintainers. These results show that ShadowProbe can identify hidden algorithmic risks across diverse real-world codebases.

### [81] [Look-Ahead-Freedom as Temporal Non-Interference: A Verifiable Correctness Property for Backtesting and Agentic Trading Pipelines](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04958v1)
*Xavier Fonseca*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过将无前瞻性形式化为时间非干扰性，提出了一种管道演算和类型系统，在线性时间内判定值无关片段的无前瞻性，并验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有管理前瞻偏差的方法针对特定构造且不完整，需要一种形式化方法来确保回测和机器学习评估的可信度。

Method: 将无前瞻性识别为时间非干扰性，开发了管道演算分离数据可用性与参考时间，并提出值无关片段上的类型-效果系统。

Result: 系统可靠且在线性时间内可判定，实验证明能检测所有植入泄漏且无误报。

Conclusion: 该形式化方法为无前瞻性提供了严格的保证，并揭示了值依赖情况下问题的不可判定性边界。

中文摘要：前瞻偏差（在决策时刻之后使用信息来做出该时刻的决策）是回测或机器学习评估中过度美化系统性能的主要原因，导致系统在实际部署中令人失望。业界通过针对特定构造的配方和经验检测器来管理该问题，这些方法仅在各个通道上有效，且不能通过沉默来证明任何问题。我们表明，无前瞻性实际上是一个形式化性质：固定一个时刻，要求未来不影响当前是一种时间索引信息格上的时间非干扰性。基于这一识别，我们开发了一个管道演算，将数据的可用性与其参考时间分离，并界定了问题的边界。当可用性可能依赖于数据值时，无前瞻性是不可判定的（实际上是Pi-0-1-hard）：泄漏是递归可枚举的，但无泄漏性则不是。在值无关片段（涵盖窗口化、重采样、连接、时间点和历史读取以及代理检索）上，我们给出了一个类型-效果系统，它是可靠且可在线性时间内判定的。一个实验验证了该理论：检查器线性地扩展，独立的预言机证明没有任何接受管道存在泄漏，并且检查器捕捉到了所有差分检测器和分块检测器遗漏的植入泄漏。

Original abstract: Look-ahead bias (using information from after a decision epoch to make the decision at that epoch) is the dominant way a backtest or a machine-learning evaluation flatters a system that will disappoint in deployment. The field manages it with construct-specific recipes and empirical detectors, which are sound only channel by channel and certify nothing by their silence. We show that look-ahead-freedom is a formal property in disguise: fixing an epoch, the demand that the future not influence the present is temporal non-interference over a time-indexed information lattice. From this identification we develop a pipeline calculus separating a datum's availability from its reference time, and settle the problem's boundary. Where availability may depend on data values, look-ahead-freedom is undecidable (indeed Pi-0-1-hard): leakage is recursively enumerable but freedom is not. On the value-independent fragment (covering windowing, resampling, joins, point-in-time and vintage reads, and agentic retrieval) we give a type-and-effect system that is sound and decidable in linear time. An artifact confirms the theory: the check scales linearly, an independent oracle witnesses no leak in any accepted pipeline, and the checker catches every planted leak that differential and tiling detectors miss.

</details>

*Mouhamed Amine Bouchiha,Gregory Blanc*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖单一大型语言模型进行端到端抽取，存在成本高、可控性差和性能不稳定的问题，亟需更高效、可靠的CSKG构建方案。

Method: 设计TACTIC-KG框架，将CSKG构建分解为提取、类型化、验证和策展四个模块，分别由专门的轻量级LLM代理执行，实现任务的专业化和协作。

Result: 在人工标注的CTI报告上，代理专门化在提取F1分数、类型化准确性和结构图相似性方面持续优于大规模单体内文学习基线。

中文摘要：网络威胁情报（CTI）报告主要非结构化、异构且嘈杂，这限制了其直接用于自动分析和推理的可用性。网络安全知识图谱（CSKG）提供了对抗实体、动作和关系的结构化表示，但从自由文本CTI构建此类图仍然具有挑战性。最近的方法依赖单一大语言模型（LLM）进行端到端提取和补全，导致成本高、可控性有限且性能不稳定。本文介绍了TACTIC-KG，一种用于CSKG构建的智能体框架，该框架将任务分解为模块化的、专门的LLM智能体，负责提取、类型化、验证和策展。使用轻量级模型（3B-8B），TACTIC-KG提高了稳定性、召回率和图一致性，同时降低了部署成本。我们实现并评估了TACTIC-KG，与最近的最先进系统进行了比较。在人工标注的CTI报告上的实验表明，智能体专门化在提取F1分数、类型化准确性和结构图相似性方面始终优于更大的单体内文学习（ICL）基线。

Original abstract: Cyber Threat Intelligence (CTI) reports are predominantly unstructured, heterogeneous, and noisy, which limits their direct usability for automated analysis and reasoning. Cybersecurity Knowledge Graphs (CSKGs) provide a structured representation of adversarial entities, actions, and relations, but constructing such graphs from free-text CTI remains a challenge. Recent approaches rely on monolithic Large Language Models (LLMs) to perform end-to-end extraction and completion, leading to high cost, limited controllability, and unstable performance. This paper introduces TACTIC-KG, an agentic framework for CSKG construction that decomposes the task into modular, specialized LLM agents responsible for extraction, typing, verification, and curation. Using lightweight models (3B--8B), TACTIC-KG improves stability, recall, and graph consistency while reducing deployment cost. We implement and evaluate TACTIC-KG against recent state-of-the-art systems. Experiments on human-annotated CTI reports show that agent specialization consistently outperforms larger monolithic in-context-learning (ICL) baselines in extraction F1-score, typing accuracy, and structural graph similarity.

### [83] [Your Agent's Memories Are Not Its Own: Forged Reasoning Attacks on LLM Agent Memory and Defenses](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05029v1)
*Neeraj Karamchandani,Piyush Nagasubramaniam,Sencun Zhu,Dinghao Wu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 针对LLM agent记忆的注入攻击与防御，直接涉及agent安全控制。

TL;DR: 提出FARMA攻击污染LLM智能体的推理历史，并设计SENTINEL防御管道，成功将攻击成功率降至0%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体使用持久性内存存储推理历史，但这一机制引入了新的攻击面，现有防御主要保护事实知识而非推理历史。

Method: FARMA通过规避语言和自我参照强化插入伪造推理痕迹；SENTINEL使用基于五个加权信号的推理守卫进行分层检测。

Result: FARMA在基线条件下攻击成功率高达100%，能绕过关键字过滤和A-MemGuard；SENTINEL将攻击成功率降至0%，无假阳性。

Conclusion: 保护智能体的推理历史完整性至关重要，SENTINEL有效防御了针对推理历史的攻击。

中文摘要：持久性内存使大型语言模型（LLM）智能体能够存储事实知识、先前的决策、推理历史、工具使用信息和上下文。虽然这提高了智能体的功能和跨任务的连续性，但也引入了一个新的攻击面：智能体自身的推理历史。在本文中，我们提出了伪造放大理由记忆攻击（FARMA），它污染智能体的记忆推理而非其事实知识。它使用规避语言插入伪造的推理痕迹，绕过基于关键字的防御，然后通过自我参照强化来击败基于共识的防御。为了应对FARMA，我们引入了SENTINEL，一个分层防御管道，用于检测伪造的推理条目。其核心组件是推理守卫，它使用五个加权信号从结构上分析候选条目是否存在伪造。我们在多个智能体和不同的LLM模型上，通过50次试验评估了FARMA和SENTINEL，结果表明，在基线条件下FARMA的攻击成功率高达100%，并且能够击败关键字过滤器和A-MemGuard等防御机制。我们的评估还表明，SENTINEL将FARMA的攻击成功率降至0%，并且在326个良性智能体痕迹中没有观察到误报。我们的工作表明，不仅需要保护智能体的检索内容，还需要保护其推理历史的完整性。

Original abstract: Persistent memory has enabled large language model (LLM) agents to store factual knowledge, prior decisions, reasoning histories, tool usage information, and context. While this has improved the agent's functionality and continuity across tasks, it has also introduced a new attack surface: the agent's own reasoning history. In this paper, we introduce the Forged Amplifying Rationale Memory Attack (FARMA), which poisons an agent's remembered reasoning rather than its factual knowledge. It inserts forged reasoning traces using evasive language that bypasses keyword-based defenses, then amplifies them through self-referential reinforcement that defeats consensus-based defenses. To address FARMA, we introduce SENTINEL, a layered defense pipeline to detect forged reasoning entries. Its central component is the Reasoning Guard that structurally analyzes candidate entries for forgery using five weighted signals.
  We evaluate FARMA and SENTINEL across multiple agents and different LLM models with 50 trials and show that FARMA achieves an attack success rate of up to 100% under baseline conditions and is capable of defeating defense mechanisms like keyword filter and A-MemGuard. Our evaluation also shows that SENTINEL reduces FARMA's attack success rate to as low as 0% with no false positives observed across 326 benign agent traces. Our work demonstrates the need to protect not only an agent's retrieved content but also the integrity of its reasoning history.

</details>


### [84] [Agent Data Injection Attacks are Realistic Threats to AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05120v1)
*Woohyuk Choi,Juhee Kim,Taehyun Kang,Jihyeon Jeong,Luyi Xing,Byoungyoung Lee*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 直接研究AI agent的数据注入攻击，暴露安全漏洞，对agent安全控制有直接贡献。

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的AI代理安全威胁——代理数据注入攻击（ADI），通过伪装成可信数据的恶意数据操控代理执行非预期操作，并发现多个真实代理中的关键漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI代理安全研究主要针对指令注入，而ADI尚未被充分探索且能绕过现有防御，因此需要揭示这一安全缺口。

Method: 引入ADI攻击类别，分析真实世界代理（如Claude in Chrome、Codex等）中的漏洞，并在独立LLM和AI代理设置中评估ADI的有效性。

Result: 发现Web代理中存在任意点击漏洞，编码代理中存在远程代码执行和供应链攻击漏洞；ADI在多种模型和代理中均有效。

Conclusion: ADI暴露了当前AI代理缺乏将可信数据与不可信数据隔离的基本安全原则，亟需改进代理安全机制。

中文摘要：AI代理代表用户提示行事，消耗外部数据并基于代理上下文采取行动。先前关于AI代理安全的研究主要集中在间接提示注入（IPI）上。其研究最充分的类别是指令注入，其中攻击者控制的不可信数据被解释为指令。作为回应，已提出许多缓解措施以防止指令注入攻击。在本文中，我们引入了一个新的IPI类别：代理数据注入攻击（ADI）。ADI注入伪装成可信数据的恶意数据，例如安全关键元数据（如资源标识符或数据来源）或代理上下文数据（如工具调用和响应格式）。结果，代理在不知情的情况下基于攻击者控制的数据执行了非预期的操作。ADI与指令注入攻击具有相似的攻击影响，因为它导致代理行为异常并执行非预期操作。尽管影响相似，但ADI仍未被充分探索，并且容易绕过现有的IPI防御。我们在真实世界的代理中发现了几个关键漏洞，允许攻击者发起各种攻击：对Web代理的任意点击攻击（Chrome中的Claude、Antigravity和Nanobrowser），以及对编码代理的远程代码执行和供应链攻击（Claude Code、Codex和Gemini CLI）。我们评估了现成模型和AI代理中的ADI漏洞，并发现ADI在独立的LLM和AI代理设置中都很有效。ADI暴露了代理安全中的一个关键缺口，表明当前的AI代理没有采用一个基本的安全原则：当前代理没有将可信数据与不可信数据隔离。

Original abstract: AI agents act on behalf of user prompts, consuming external data and taking actions based on the agent context. Prior research on AI agent security has primarily focused on indirect prompt injection (IPI). Its most well-studied category is instruction injection, where attacker-controlled untrusted data is interpreted as an instruction. In response, many mitigations have been proposed to prevent instruction injection attacks. In this paper, we introduce a new category of IPI, agent data injection attacks (ADI). ADI injects malicious data disguised as trusted data, such as security-critical metadata (e.g., resource identifiers or data origins) or agent context data (e.g., tool call and response formats). As a result, agents unknowingly execute unintended actions based on attacker-controlled data. ADI has similar attack impacts as instruction injection attacks, because it causes agents to misbehave and execute unintended actions. Despite the similar impact, ADI remains underexplored and easily bypasses existing IPI defenses. We found several critical vulnerabilities in real-world agents that allow an attacker to launch various attacks: arbitrary click attacks on web agents (Claude in Chrome, Antigravity, and Nanobrowser), and remote code execution and supply-chain attacks on coding agents (Claude Code, Codex, and Gemini CLI). We evaluate ADI vulnerabilities across off-the-shelf models and AI agents, and find that ADI is effective in both standalone LLMs and AI agent settings. ADI exposes a critical gap in agent security, signifying that current AI agents do not employ a fundamental security principle: current agents do not isolate trusted data from untrusted data.

</details>


### [85] [When Claws Remember but Do Not Tell: Stealthy Memory Injection in Persistent Personal Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05189v1)
*Yechao Zhang,Shiqian Zhao,Jiawen Zhang,Jie Zhang,Gelei Deng,Xiaogeng Liu,Chaowei Xiao,Tianwei Zhang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 持久agent记忆注入攻击，agent安全控制相关。

TL;DR: 研究持久性个人代理中的隐形内存注入威胁，提出WhisperBench基准和MemGhost攻击框架，实现了高成功率攻击并能跨架构和防御转移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 持久性个人代理整合长期记忆与外部访问，为攻击者提供了新途径：通过将恶意内容写入持久内存并作为可信状态重用，可造成长期妥协。

Method: 提出WhisperBench基准（108个案例，5个风险类别）和MemGhost框架（单邮件黑盒攻击），后者使用环境代理模拟执行、目标代理将内存采纳和对话隐蔽性转化为密集奖励，通过监督微调和强化学习训练攻击策略。

Result: 在56个保留测试中，MemGhost在OpenClaw/GPT-5.4上成功率达87.5%，在Claude Code SDK/Sonnet 4.6上达71.4%，且能跨架构（NanoClaw、Hermes Agent）和内存后端（文件系统、Mem0）转移，并绕过输入级、模型级和系统级防御。

Conclusion: 持久性内存可将普通外部处理转化为长期代理妥协的实用路径，凸显了新型安全威胁。

中文摘要：持久性个人代理结合了长期记忆与用户外部环境的访问权限，实现了个性化前景协助和主动式后台执行。这种整合也创造了一条新的妥协途径：不受信任的外部内容可以被静默写入持久性记忆，并随后作为可信状态被重用。我们将这种威胁研究为隐形内存注入，其中远程黑盒对手传递单个电子邮件载荷，必须诱导代理写入中毒内存，隐藏在代理对用户的响应中，并影响未来行为。我们引入了WhisperBench，一个包含108个案例的基准测试，涵盖五个风险类别以及事实和偏好中毒。它基于真实的IMAP/SMTP工作流和真实的电子邮件代理技能，能够对隐形内存注入攻击进行全周期评估。为了实现这种在单电子邮件传递且无运行时反馈下的黑盒攻击，我们提出了MemGhost，一个一次性载荷生成框架。MemGhost使用环境代理来模拟持久性代理执行，并使用目标代理将内存采纳和对话隐蔽性转化为基于密集评分的奖励，然后通过监督微调和强化学习训练攻击者策略。在56个保留测试案例中，MemGhost在GPT-5.4上的OpenClaw上实现了87.5%的端到端成功率，在Sonnet 4.6上的Claude Code SDK上实现了71.4%的成功率。它还跨个人代理架构（NanoClaw和Hermes Agent）和内存后端（文件系统和基于向量的Mem0）转移，并且对输入级、模型级和系统级防御仍然有效。这些结果表明，持久性内存可以将普通的外部处理转变为长期代理妥协的实用途径。

Original abstract: Persistent personal agents combine long-term memory with access to users' external environments, enabling personalized foreground assistance and proactive background execution. This integration also creates a new path to compromise: untrusted external content can be silently written into persistent memory and later reused as trusted state. We study this threat as stealth memory injection, in which a remote black-box adversary delivers a single email payload that must induce the agent to write poisoned memory, stay hidden in the agent's response to the user, and affect future behavior.
  We introduce WhisperBench, a 108-case benchmark spanning five risk categories and both fact and preference poisoning. Built on a real IMAP/SMTP workflow and an authentic email agent skill, it enables full-cycle evaluation of stealth memory injection attacks. To enable this black-box attack under single-email delivery and without runtime feedback, we propose MemGhost, a one-shot payload generation framework. MemGhost uses an environment proxy to emulate persistent-agent execution and an objective proxy to convert memory adoption and conversational stealth into dense rubric-based rewards, then trains the attacker policy with supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning.
  Across 56 held-out test cases, MemGhost achieves 87.5% end-to-end success on OpenClaw with GPT-5.4 and 71.4% on Claude Code SDK with Sonnet 4.6. It also transfers across personal-agent architectures (NanoClaw and Hermes Agent) and memory backends (filesystem and vector-based Mem0), and remains effective against input-level, model-level, and system-level defenses. These results suggest that persistent memory can turn ordinary external processing into a practical pathway for long-term agent compromise.

</details>


### [86] [aiAuthZ: Off-Host, Identity-Bound Authorization for AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05518v1)
*Sai Varun Kodathala*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: AI agent授权网关，解决agent安全控制，可迁移至coding agent可靠性与安全。

TL;DR: 提出一个授权网关aiAuthZ，通过消息签名、策略评估和审计日志防止AI代理被欺骗后执行越权工具调用，在15个模型上实现0%残余攻击成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI代理基于不可验证文本发出工具调用，易被上下文控制者伪造权威，现有模型拒绝攻击率差异大（38%-100%），需要独立于代理主机的安全机制。

Method: 设计aiAuthZ网关，在工具调用执行前验证调用者身份（HMAC-SHA256+一次性随机数+时间戳），评估角色和参数级策略（代理不可读写），记录SHA-256链审计日志，并生成HMAC认证的QR收据。

Result: 15个模型残余攻击成功率降至0%，增加决策延迟≤0.03ms；在AgentDojo银行套件上阻止所有7个攻击导向调用（一次误拒合法调用）；9个案例研究中阻止全部9个攻击，优于基线（4/9）。

Conclusion: aiAuthZ有效防止被欺骗的代理执行越权操作，但无法防止模型被欺骗本身。

中文摘要：AI代理根据其无法验证的文本发出工具调用，因此任何控制上下文的一方都可以伪造权威的外观。我针对来自已发布真实代理事件语料库的八种攻击场景评估了15个当代语言模型，发现完全评估的模型的拒绝率从100%到38%不等；最昂贵的模型虽然价格相差20倍，但只拒绝了半数攻击。我提出了aiAuthZ，一个将安全决策从代理主机移开的授权网关。在工具调用执行之前，网关通过每个消息的HMAC-SHA256签名（绑定到一次性随机数和时间戳窗口）验证调用者身份，并评估代理既不能读取也不能修改的基于角色和参数级别的策略。每个决策都加入SHA-256哈希链审计日志，每个接受的消息生成一个HMAC认证的QR收据，在八个传输通道上实现了94%的平均验证率，在25次错误密钥试验中零伪造被接受。有了网关，15个模型的残余攻击成功率降至0%，增加的决策延迟不超过0.03毫秒。在AgentDojo银行套件上，aiAuthZ阻止了评估代理发出的所有七个攻击者导向的工具调用，代价是一次合法首次付款，而一个基线方法允许两次注入成功。来自同一事件语料库的九个在范围内案例研究中，aiAuthZ阻止了九个中的九个，而一个没有身份绑定的策略基线只阻止了四个中的九个。网关不能防止模型被欺骗；它防止了被欺骗的模型在每个通过它的调用中超出已验证用户权限的行动。实现和所有实验发布在https://github.com/Sports-Vision-Inc/aiAuthZ。

Original abstract: AI agents issue tool calls on the basis of text they cannot verify, so any party who controls part of the context can forge the appearance of authority. I evaluate 15 contemporary language models against eight attack scenarios derived from a published corpus of real agent incidents and find that refusal varies from 100% down to 38% across fully evaluated models; the most expensive model refused only half of the attacks despite a twentyfold price spread. I present aiAuthZ, an authorization gateway that moves the safety decision off the agent's host. Before a tool call executes, the gateway verifies caller identity with a per-message HMAC-SHA256 signature bound to a single-use nonce and a timestamp window, and it evaluates a role-based and argument-level policy that the agent can neither read nor modify. Every decision joins a SHA-256 hash-chained audit log, and each accepted message yields an HMAC-authenticated QR receipt that achieves 94% mean verification across eight transmission channels, with zero forgeries accepted in 25 wrong-key trials. With the gateway in place, residual attack success falls to 0% for all 15 models at no more than 0.03 ms of added decision latency. On the AgentDojo banking suite, aiAuthZ blocks all seven attacker-directed tool calls the evaluated agents emit, at the cost of one legitimate first-time payment, while a spotlighting baseline allows two injections to succeed. Across nine in-scope case studies from the same incident corpus, aiAuthZ blocks nine of nine, against four of nine for a policy baseline without identity binding. The gateway does not prevent a model from being deceived; it prevents a deceived model from acting beyond the verified user's authority on every call routed through it. The implementation and all experiments are released at https://github.com/Sports-Vision-Inc/aiAuthZ.

</details>


### [87] [When Agents Remember Too Much: Memory Poisoning Attacks on Large Language Model Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06595v1)
*George Torres,Sharad Shrestha,Satyajayant Misra*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 研究agent记忆投毒攻击，提出防御，直接涉及agent安全。

TL;DR: 本文提出GhostWriter攻击，利用个人AI代理的记忆子系统进行注入，成功率高，并提出了AM-Sentry防御机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 个人AI代理在处理敏感信息时与不可信源交互，现有记忆系统缺乏安全治理，导致安全漏洞。

Method: 提出GhostWriter攻击（注入+激活两阶段）和AM-Sentry防御（记忆保存策略和记忆检索屏障）。

Result: GhostWriter实现约98%注入率和约60%激活率；AM-Sentry显著降低其成功率并保持代理效用。

Conclusion: 需要以安全为中心的记忆治理，AM-Sentry可有效防御此类攻击。

中文摘要：由大型语言模型驱动的个人AI代理能够使用可用工具进行推理和行动，例如访问电子邮件、管理日历和推送代码到远程仓库，且几乎无需监督。当配备长期记忆时，代理可以回忆与当前任务相关的具体细节，从而减少对大型上下文窗口的需求。目前，长期记忆代理倾向于分为两个不同的领域：对话代理和行动规划代理。个人助理代理处于这两个领域的交汇点，在处理敏感信息的同时与不可信信息源交互，从而产生了先前未考虑到的安全漏洞。在本工作中，我们引入了一种新颖的攻击向量GhostWriter，该攻击利用使用工具的个人代理中的当前记忆子系统来毒化其记忆存储。GhostWriter分为两个阶段：注入阶段，攻击者向目标代理发送隐藏的攻击载荷；激活阶段，被毒化的记忆被检索。我们表明，GhostWriter对最先进的代理实现了约98%的近乎普遍注入率和约60%的高平均激活率。这种攻击之所以可能，是因为缺乏以安全为中心的记忆治理。作为回应，我们提出了Agentic Memory Sentry（AM-Sentry），它利用了两种缓解技术：记忆保存策略和记忆检索屏障。我们的实验表明，AM-Sentry在保持代理效用的同时显著降低了GhostWriter的成功率。

Original abstract: Personal AI agents powered by large language models can reason and act using available tools to access emails, manage calendars, and push code to remote repositories, all with minimal oversight. When augmented with long-term memory, an agent can recall specific details relevant to the current task, reducing the need for large context windows. Currently, long-term memory agents tend to fall into two distinct domains: conversational and action-planning agents. Personal assistant agents sit at the convergence of these two domains and handle sensitive information while interacting with untrusted information sources, creating previously unaccounted security vulnerabilities. In this work, we introduce the novel attack vector, GhostWriter, which exploits current memory subsystems in tool-using personal agents to poison their memory store. GhostWriter operates in two phases: injection, where an adversary sends a hidden attack payload to the target agent; and activation, in which the poisoned memory is retrieved. We show that GhostWriter achieves near-universal injection rates of approximately 98% and a high average activation rate of approximately 60% against state-of-the-art agents. This attack is possible due to the lack of security-focused memory governance. In response, we propose Agentic Memory Sentry (AM-Sentry), which leverages two mitigation techniques: a memory-saving policy and a memory-retrieval screen. Our experiments show that AM-Sentry dramatically reduces GhostWriter's success rate while preserving agent utility.

</details>
